# Copy Trade | GMGN Tutorial

**1\. Feature Overview**

The wallet copy trading feature allows you to select a target wallet (such as a KOL / smart money). According to the rules you configure in advance, the system will automatically follow that wallet’s **buy / sell** operations on-chain, so you can run **semi-automatic / fully automatic** copy-trading strategies.

* * *

**2\. Entry (App)**

1.  Open the App and use the bottom navigation to go to **“Track”**.
    
2.  In **“Rank / Radar”**, select the wallet you want to copy.
    
3.  Tap the **“Copy”** button on the wallet card to enter the **CopyTrade configuration** page.
    
4.  After you finish all settings, tap **“Copy”**, and the strategy will take effect.
    

* * *

1.  **How to configure a copy-trading strategy**
    

To configure a wallet copy-trading strategy, simply go through the items on the App screen from top to bottom:

1.  Confirm the copy-trade wallet address and note. 1.1 You can use one-tap copy trade from the **Rank/ Radar** pages; the system will automatically fill in the target wallet address. 1.2 You can also paste any wallet address you have saved yourself and add a note to distinguish different strategies.
    
2.  In **Buy settings**, choose the wallet to follow, the copy-buy mode, and the scaling-in (add-position) logic.
    
3.  In **Sell settings**, configure auto copy-sell, take-profit and stop-loss rules, and other exit conditions.
    
4.  In **Filter settings / Platforms & blacklist**, define which tokens are allowed to be copy-traded.
    
5.  In **Fees & Anti-MEV mode**, control slippage, priority fee, tip fee, and the anti-MEV protection level.
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FqGXYKZ96AltUhT6mQkL3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df32834d8-f4be-409d-a9f0-08a0975956c4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=62d23791&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F5jo6vs6NKyGVDomtETtY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da99f94a3-fb1d-4331-84db-c5e63aa6a754&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c47e6bea&sv=2)

* * *

**Wallet Copy Trading Configuration Table (in App Step Order)**

Step / Section

Field / Option (UI label)

Mode / How to Fill

Explanation

Recommendation / Example

Screenshot ref

1.  **Copy From**
    

**Copy From** (target wallet)

Auto-filled by system (when you enter from Top Traders / Radar)

The **wallet you want to follow** – your target wallet. It decides **who you are learning from on-chain**.

Usually no need to change. Just confirm it’s exactly the wallet you want to copy.

Fig.1 – left, “1.Copy From”

1.  **Buy**
    

**My Wallet** (funding wallet)

Choose from **Select Wallet** popup

This is the **wallet used for copy trading funds**. All copy **buys / sells** will use this wallet’s balance.

Strongly recommend using a **“copy-trading-only wallet”**, not your main large holding wallet.

Fig.1 – left, “My Wallet” + Select Wallet popup

**Fixed Buy** (mode dropdown)

Dropdown: **Fixed Buy / Max Buy / Fixed Ratio**

Decides **“when they buy, how much you follow with.”**Fixed Buy = same size each time; Max Buy = follow with an upper cap; Fixed Ratio = follow with N% of their amount.

Beginner: **Fixed Buy**.Advanced: **Fixed Ratio + Max Buy** (e.g. 120% with 1 SOL cap).

Fig.1 – left, “Fixed Buy”

**Amount**

Enter a number (in SOL)

In **Fixed Buy** mode, this is how many SOL you actually put in **each time** a copy buy is triggered.

Set by your capital size, e.g. 0.01 / 0.05 / 0.1 SOL.

Fig.1 – middle, “Amount 0.001”

**Skip Holdings**

Checkbox

When enabled, if you already hold this token in this wallet, the system can skip new buys according to your logic.

For conservative mode, keep it **on** to avoid over-concentrating in one token.

Fig.1 – middle, “Skip Holdings”

**Increase Times**

0 / 1 / 2 …

Number of times you are allowed to **add positions for the same token** while still holding it. Resets after full exit.

Recommend 0 or 1: 0 = never add once you have a position; 1 = at most one extra add-on.

Fig.1 – middle, right side “Increase Times” text

1.  **Sell Method**
    

**Copy Sell**

On / Off switch

On: when the target wallet sells **X% of their own position**, you sell the **same % of the part you bought by copy**. Does **not** affect positions bought manually.

In most cases, keep **Copy Sell = On** to fully follow their rhythm.

Fig.1 – middle, “Copy Sell”

**TP/SL** (ladder TP/SL)

Switch + multiple rows (**TP % / SL % / Sell %**)

Allows multiple **take-profit / stop-loss levels** for the same token. When any level is hit, it auto sells that level’s **Sell %**.

Example: level1 +30% sell 20%; level2 +60% sell 30%; SL -15% sell 30%.

Fig.1 – middle, TP/SL area

**Dev Sell**

Switch + fields: **Dev Sell ≥ %** + **Auto Sell %**

When contract dev sells up to a certain ratio (e.g. 25–30%), you auto sell a set % to avoid being stuck by dev dumping.

For new / high-risk tokens, recommended: Dev Sell ≥ 30%, Auto Sell 30%–50%.

Fig.1 – middle, “Dev Sell” row

**Migrated Sell**

Switch + **Migrated Sell %**

For tokens that do **“full bar → migrate → launch”**. After migration launch, auto sell part / all position by this %.

Suggest at least 30%–50% to lock some profit after migration.

Fig.1 – middle, “Migrated Sell” row

**Single TP/SL**

Switch + **Take Profit % / Stop Loss %**

Simple mode: one TP and one SL. When hit, it sells according to the set ratio (usually all or big part).

Example: TP 300% / SL 10%. For “simple mode” users.

Fig.1 – right, “Single TP/SL” block

**Trailing Stop Loss**

Switch + trailing %

Based on **drawdown from highest price**. E.g. set 20% ⇒ when price falls 20% from the top, auto sell to lock gains.

Common 15%–30%, often used together with Single TP.

Fig.1 – right, toggle “Trailing Stop Loss”

1.  **Filter**
    

**MC**

Min / Max (K)

Market cap range. Only follow tokens whose market cap is between these values.

Example: 5k–100k USD (enter 5–100 K). Adjust to your risk appetite.

Fig.2 – left, “MC” block

**Liq**

Min / Max (K)

Liquidity range. Too low = slippage huge; too high = less volatile, not ideal for short scalps.

Example: min 5k liquidity; can go slightly lower for very early plays, but not too low.

Fig.2 – left, “Liq” block

**Copy Buy Amount**

Min / Max (SOL)

Range of **single buy size** of the target wallet that you are willing to follow. Outside this range = no copy.

Example: 0.5–5 SOL ⇒ ignore tiny test buys and giant whale buys.

Fig.2 – left, “Copy Buy Amount”

**Holders**

Min / Max

Filter by current holder count. Too few holders often means just created or extremely concentrated.

Example: Min = 50, Max left blank or very high.

Fig.2 – left / middle, “Holders”

**Token Ratio**

Min / Max (%)

How much of total supply this buy represents. Avoid buys that are too big (control risk) or too tiny (not meaningful).

Example: only follow when Token Ratio is between 0.01%–1%.

Fig.2 – left / middle, “Token Ratio”

**Age**

Min / Max (m / h / d)

Token **age since creation** (not LP launch). You only play tokens whose creation time falls within this range.

Example: 10 seconds–1 day ⇒ only newly created tokens.

Fig.2 – left / middle, “Age”

**Min Burnt**

Min (%)

Minimum **LP burnt / destroyed** %. Below this, you don’t copy, to avoid projects with no LP lock (not 100% safe).

Example: ≥ 50%.

Fig.2 – left / bottom, “Min Burnt”

1.  **Platform & Token Blacklist**
    

**Platform**

Multi-select buttons: Pumpfun / Boop / Moonshot / Raydium / …

Only **buys on selected platforms** will trigger copy trading. Does **not** affect selling.

Common: only Pumpfun; or Pumpfun + Raydium + one or two others.

Fig.2 – middle, “Platform” button group

**Token Blacklist**

Manually input token contract addresses, one per line

Tokens you never want to touch again. Once added, this token will not trigger any copy buy or copy sell.

Up to 20 tokens. Only add ones you’re sure you will not re-enter.

Fig.2 – right, “Token Blacklist”

1.  **Slippage & Fees & Boost**
    

**Slippage Limit**

**Auto** / manual %

Auto: system estimates needed slippage from depth; Manual: you set a % yourself (too low ⇒ many failures).

Default: **Auto**. Manual only when you know what you’re doing.

Fig.2 – right, “Slippage Limit”

**Fee Settings → Priority Fee (SOL)**

Auto / manual (SOL)

Extra fee paid to block producers. Higher = faster confirmation, but too high + frequent trading = eats profit.

Typical range: 0.0002–0.0006 SOL; minimum 0.0001 SOL.

Fig.2 – right, “Priority Fee (SOL)”

**Fee Settings → Tip Fee (SOL)**

Auto / manual (SOL)

Similar to **Jito tip**: paid to MEV / special relays to speed up confirmation & ordering.

Start from 0.0001 SOL and adjust after seeing effect.

Fig.2 – right, “Tip Fee (SOL)”

**Boost mode(Anti-MEV)**

**Off / Red. / Sec.**

Anti-MEV & sandwich-protection mode. **Off** = fastest but highest MEV risk; **Red.** = reduced MEV, medium speed; **Sec.** = safest, best protection but slightly slower.

Officially recommend **Sec.**. Only use **Off / Red.** if you are extremely speed-sensitive and can accept MEV risk.

Fig.2 – right, “Boost mode(Anti-MEV)”

**4\. How to View Orders and Strategy Status**

**4.1 View All Copy Trading Strategies**

**Entry:** App bottom **\[Track\] → “CopyTrade”→ “Ongoing”**

You can see:

*   The name of each strategy, target wallet, and current status (**Share / Paused/Details**);
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FVTb703pUZJOGykttN25m%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50044be7-7481-4f39-91b7-16b7df5c4f4f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c57b94f4&sv=2)

* * *

**4.2 View a Single Strategy in Detail**

Tap any strategy to enter its detail page. You can view:

*   **Current positions** (Tracking Profit, Realized Profit, Unrealized PnL, etc.);
    
*   **Activity All/buy / sell history**;
    
*   **CopeTrade Failed / Filter List** (such as slippage too low, insufficient balance, network timeout, etc.).
    

* * *

**4.3 Copy Trading Message Notifications**

**Entry:** Assets page top-left **\[Settings\] → \[Notification Settings\]→ \[Enable SOL Alerts\]→ \[Copy trade\]**

You can configure whether to receive copy-trading related notifications.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FFrVOll3HKn7dE3qTgOeV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82f2e77f-5c3d-4834-891f-2cba67feb13c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f7809c1d&sv=2)

* * *

**5\. FAQ**

**Q1: If I enable “CoeySell / TP&SL / Dev Sell / Migrated Sell” at the same time, which one runs first? Will it sell more than I hold?**

**A:** The system does **not** have any manually set priority. Whichever condition is met first will execute first. Each rule is calculated based on your **remaining position at that moment**, so it will **not sell more than you actually hold**.

* * *

**Q2: The target wallet has already bought a token. Why didn’t my strategy follow?**

**A:** Common reasons include:

*   The trade was blocked by **Filter / Platform / Token Blacklist**;
    
*   Your wallet balance was too low to reach your **minimum buy amount**;
    
*   Slippage, Priority Fee or Tip Fee was too low, so the transaction failed to be confirmed on-chain;
    
*   The strategy was automatically paused by the system (for example, after consecutive failures or repeated “insufficient balance”).
    

We recommend checking the **“Filter List ”** section in that strategy’s detail page to see the specific reason.

* * *

**Q3: Why do my orders fail so often?**

**A:** Possible reasons:

*   Slippage is set too low, so orders cannot be filled when the price moves quickly;
    
*   Priority Fee / Tip Fee is too low, so during network congestion your transaction is not easily included in a block;
    
*   The current network or node is unstable.
    

You can try slightly increasing slippage and fees.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FLkL4bSdwwLtNKmM4VLpc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a42b00d-167f-42d2-a1d6-a0c4bcebe84b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f3e5fd0c&sv=2)

* * *

Q4: I often see profitable trades, but overall my total PnL is not high. Why?

A: When you copy trade frequently, fees become a larger part of the cost, mainly including:

*   Priority Fee / Tip Fee set too high;
    
*   The amount of money you pay for the next purchase is small, and the amount you pay for the purchase is very large. The construction options and control system increase the rate and the height of the weight.
    

* * *

Q5: How many wallet copy trading strategies can I create at most?

A: Currently, up to 10 wallet copy trading strategies are supported (same limit on Web and App).

When you reach this limit, you’ll need to **close or delete** some existing strategies before creating new ones.

* * *

# TRENDING | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trending#trending)

TRENDING


--------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FpfPZMtFmZwuZAPKhN4gu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c428edc-f152-41b0-8a92-ac86f0f90bb0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=192d90e0&sv=2)

Creation time

Liquidity/ Market Capitalization

Number of Holders

Number of transactions in 1 hour

1h Vol

Transcation volume in 1 hour

Current meme price

Percentage price fluctuation of this token in 1 minutes/ 5 minutes/ 1 hour

Degen Aduit

[CA Security Check](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/ca-security-checks)

*   We have a Trending page for you to see the top tokens that people are buying and selling
    
*   We offer multiple options for you to filter and sort by, just like the NEW PAIR page. Additionally, you can select different time intervals (1 minute/ 5 minutes/ 30 minutes/ 1 hour) to see tokens that have been trending across those time frames
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fa2lqVkl0ZFa2drxrpCZc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f66d6ae-c5b8-4aa8-813f-103fb6c69a90&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c393645c&sv=2)

*   In this section on the left, you can click on the little star to add it to the watch list;
    
*   You'll see how popular it is as well as the number of fires;
    
*   You'll see if it has a CTO after its logo appears, and if the emoji of two people appears yellow;
    
*   You'll see if it has an AD activated in Dexscreener;
    
*   You'll see if the network is updated in Dexscreener and its own network as well as in the contract.
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trending#nextbc)

NextBC


----------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FCrI2sKkGraXrKWWXU3uq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98f86942-5fd1-419f-b665-92bb2e237696&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d7eda663&sv=2)

*   Blue Chip tokens: Blue chip tokens refer to tokens on each chain that have been verified and recognized by the market, have high value, and will not easily return to zero, such as sol chain neiro, popcat
    
*   Blue Chip Holders: holders who own certain blue chip tokens
    
*   Blue Chip index: The blue chip index refers to the proportion of holders of the token who also own blue chip tokens.
    
*   Meaning of Blue Chip Index: In a token, the more holders of blue chip tokens, that is, the higher the blue chip index, the more optimistic the blue chip holders are about this coin, and the more likely this coin is to become the next high-value blue chip token.

# MEME | GMGN Tutorial

**1.What is Pump.fun?**

Pumpfun is a famous MEME token fair-launch platform with no presale and no team allocation.

**2.What is Pump Inner Trading Process?**

In one sentence, pumpfun has productized what the Meme project aims to achieve, providing a comprehensive service from token name and logo to liquidity and liquidity burning.

After successfully deploying a Meme token on pump.fun, once the token market cap reaches $69,000, the liquidity of pump.fun will be automatically added to Raydium.

**3.Why Trade Tokens on Pump.fun?**

Participating early in the token's early stages can result in higher gains, but also comes with higher risks. The token price can fluctuate sharply, requiring careful monitoring and quick trading.

**4.What Services Can GMGN Provide?**

GMGN's website and TGBOT both support trading on the Pump Inner Market and provide essential data for trading Pump, offering you more data to support playing with Pump.

**5.Visit Pumpfun Trending Channel**

Use various criteria to filter out high-quality Pump tokens👇🏻:

[![Logo](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgmgn.ai%2Fstatic%2Ffavicon2.ico&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e47fbfa&sv=2)GMGN.AI Fast Trade, Fast Copy Trade, Fast AFK Automation.gmgn](https://gmgn.ai/?chain=sol&ref=Spencer)

6.**What is Moonshot?**

Seen as a competitor to Pump.fun, their functions and operational processes are basically the same

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/meme#meme-page-overview)

MEME Page Overview:


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FcE2edikvYwBQQENcyfGE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e902649-6b19-468e-8150-7b64e4cda1d2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7603580b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F4EEYd24eWgdnpJxzUaMf%252FSnipaste_2024-07-29_22-42-41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1a5aef2-33f3-4da1-8c9e-d0c9dbc35263&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98d06d5c&sv=2)

**Unique fair launch token mechanism on Pump.fun:** There is two process of token launching on pumpfun - Trading on Pump and trading on Raydium. The swapping process is no different from normal tokens. The only distinction is that after the Pump inner market is fully filled, there is a waiting period before liquidity is added to Raydium automatically, ranging from 10 minutes to around an hour.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FzCYLsb3uDHPp1nGDFtS2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D212faf05-36c2-4956-adc0-bec57af055ab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5477acec&sv=2)

**Pump.fun Filled Complete Alerts via GMGN MEME coin tools：** If you're on the go and cannot monitor the market via the GMGN web dashboard, GMGN also offers a Pump Max-Out Alert Bot. Through Telegram, you can receive real-time alerts when a pool is filled and when secondary markets open, then jump in with a one-tap trade link.

You can also use the GMGN App to track these Pump tokens on mobile — enable push notifications, watch price and volume in real time, and place the same trades directly from the token detail screen with a single tap.

# Safety Tip | GMGN Tutorial

This article will introduce common hacker phishing methods and how to set up security in web plug-in wallets and GMGN TG wallets to prevent theft.

**In the dark forest world of blockchain, first keep in mind the following two major security rules:**

*   **Zero Trust** Simply put, it means to be skeptical, and always be skeptical of any platform, robot, plug-in wallet authorization signature, etc. that requires the input of a private key
    
*   **Continuous Security Validation** In order to trust something, you have to validate what you doubt, and make validating a habit.
    

1.  [Stolen: Common phishing and attack methods used by hackers](https://docs-gmgn-ai.translate.goog/cn/~/changes/QPvrIv5rRiWBRIdXmPYO/an-quan-ti-shi#id-1.-bei-dao-chang-jian-hei-ke-diao-yu-yi-ji-gong-ji-shou-duan)
    
2.  [Anti-Stolen: Take precautions in plugin wallets and TG wallets](https://docs-gmgn-ai.translate.goog/cn/~/changes/QPvrIv5rRiWBRIdXmPYO/an-quan-ti-shi#id-2.-fang-dao-zai-cha-jian-qian-bao-yi-ji-tg-qian-bao-zhong-zuo-hao-yu-fang)
    
3.  [Equipment Security](https://docs-gmgn-ai.translate.goog/cn/~/changes/QPvrIv5rRiWBRIdXmPYO/an-quan-ti-shi#id-3.-she-bei-an-quan)
    
4.  [What to do if assets stolen](https://docs-gmgn-ai.translate.goog/cn/~/changes/QPvrIv5rRiWBRIdXmPYO/an-quan-ti-shi#id-4.-bei-dao-le-zen-me-ban)
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/safety-tip#id-1.-bei-dao-chang-jian-hei-ke-diao-yu-yi-ji-gong-ji-shou-duan)

1\. Stolen: Common phishing and attack methods used by hackers

**Scams in TG:**

1) Please remember that the official admins will not send you a private message first!!! Scammers pretend to be GMGN admins to send fraudulent messages to defraud private keys or steal TG accounts!

*   Common situation: You send a message in the group, and the scammer asks you to cooperate under the pretext of helping you solve the problem, which eventually leads to theft. Some scammers will hide the user name and fill in the real admin's linl in the bio, which is very confusing and can easily lead the stolen user to think it is an official scam!
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FIrqWVcGnqOAhbRJ9Okwh%252FSnipaste_2024-12-22_07-04-30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11707920-0fc4-4cc1-96d7-9890d1bce746&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=414dcec3&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FTwv2D1UHZexBlrlMNSpZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df60c9601-8512-4b21-b261-159326f71621&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ea3765f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FZMxTpih09OquKvg4Jtg7%252FSnipaste_2024-12-22_07-09-53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b4db85f-b80a-4b5f-aff8-adbfd4629f01&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bb80ccf0&sv=2)

2) Do not click on any ads that appear above the GMGN bot! These are scammers who may steal your wallet! The GMGN official bot will never ask for your wallet's private key first!

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FiLVH0DBabZapQaiyWPfl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6bb628d-2a20-420d-a7d2-c45fb5c46b5d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f53979a0&sv=2)

3) In some token TG groups or links sent by scammers, there will be such so-called "security verification". Please do not click it! Do not enter any of your account information, including mobile phone number, password, etc.!

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FgFNJiaTqbuc19wQiEwvL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D788a00d1-f876-4170-8229-c908112d8988&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c82be57&sv=2)

4) The scammer copied a GMGN fake group, pulled you into the group, and posted a fraudulent link in the fake group to defraud the private key! Because there are a lot of robots in the group, it looks like there are a lot of people, and they will copy the real group messages, which can easily be mistaken for the official group. Please confirm whether it is a real group through the official GMGN Twitter! ! [https://x.com/gmgnai](https://x.com/gmgnai)

*   It is recommended that users check the "Do not allow anyone" option in "Privacy and Security - Groups and Channels". This will not allow anyone to add you to unfamiliar groups and channels, which can effectively prevent you from being pulled into fraudulent groups.
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FrePqyTXQXvUsZliBYqtj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2fbaf8cc-4d90-40f1-8ce0-36153b6a7b78&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=da785a2e&sv=2)

5) The scammer pretends to be an official Telegram admin and sends you a message. The scam words are as shown in the picture, and they guide you to click on the scam link. Please do not click it! ! Just report and block it!

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F3y9LwRWu2nziPI9e0VIy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2410b8a-5499-4977-ae0d-76b3782dfb3c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba28aaa5&sv=2)

**Scams in Web3 plugin wallets:**

1) The most important safety principle to be followed in signature security is: what you see is what you sign. Therefore, you need to regularly check whether the wallet has authorized unfamiliar applications that you are not familiar with. Please enter the wallet to check the authorization list and cancel unknown authorizations!

*   Airdrop scam: The attackers airdropped NFTs to users in batches (Figure 1). Users entered the target website through the link in the description of the airdropped NFT and connected their wallets (Figure 2). After they clicked the "Mint" button on the page, the approval window popped up (Figure 3). Note that there was no special notification or message in the pop up window at this time. Once they approved, all SOLs in the wallet would be transferred away
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FEn40cyaTiWhIYJajYefT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da75ecd5b-c27b-4a43-b4cb-75a7bc60b7f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=227aa0a9&sv=2)

2) Unknown transfers: Sometimes you will receive small amounts of unknown transfers in your wallet. Most of them are related to advertisements or scams. Don’t be curious. It will not affect the normal operation of your wallet. Don’t worry too much

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FEhlnQMynstZG9SePnruI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1e0e5fc-d68e-4f95-b6a0-339b09daa881&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe29ce09&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/safety-tip#id-2.-fang-dao-zai-cha-jian-qian-bao-yi-ji-tg-qian-bao-zhong-zuo-hao-yu-fang)

2\. Anti-stolen: Take precautions in plugin wallets and TG wallets

**Telegram Security Precautions:**

1) It is recommended that users who are not so familiar with "TG Privacy and Security" follow the following settings, especially remember to turn on the items marked in red in the picture, which can effectively ensure the security of your TG account

*   Two-step verification: After it is turned on, even if a hacker gets your phone number and password, when logging in on a new device, you still need to enter a separate password after entering the SMS verification code, fully ensuring security
    
*   Phone number: Prevent hackers from directly obtaining your mobile phone number and sending you fraudulent text messages or other fraudulent activities
    
*   Groups ＆ channels: Stolen 4) has relevant examples, which can effectively prevent being pulled into fraudulent groups
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FUYCQwbx4tC03jtBqWyDn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31dcadd7-601d-4622-a93e-7a84f7f9239d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=750f3eb7&sv=2)

2) Confirm whether your Telegram app is installed through the official channel

3) Check whether Telegram has authorized a strange fake bot to avoid the balance in the wallet being transferred by a fraud bot due to entering a mobile phone number or clicking a fraud link. It is recommended to verify the consistency through multiple GMGN official channels before making a transaction

**Web3 plugin wallet:**

1) Enter the web3 plug-in wallet to query the authorization list, cancel unknown authorization, and confirm that the authorized applications are the corresponding official applications

2) Turn on Auto-Lock timer to prevent others from seeing your private key when the device is away from you

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FOe8lV74veC45BxsV6HbN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3d28573-fa9f-419c-8de5-f33693ffbe05&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86af8f30&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FkWP2ACwz3vkosQmdHHxV%252FSnipaste_2024-12-22_07-28-05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01012730-f09a-4554-ab2a-8d52f1b4fc5b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=99be7f71&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/safety-tip#id-3.-she-bei-an-quan)

3\. Equipment Security

1) If your device is an Android phone/Windows computer/non-iPad tablet, please be careful not to click on unknown links or download unknown applications to avoid Trojans or malicious programs in your phone/computer, and regularly use security software to check the device, eliminate viruses, and prevent risks

2) If your device is an Apple device, there are still some fraudulent apps in the app store and in test software that has not been officially launched. You need to be careful

3) Security principles:

*   For all the knowledge from the Internet, refer to at least two sources, corroborate each other, and always stay skeptical
    
*   Segregate. Don't put all the eggs in one basket
    
*   For wallets with important assets, don't do unnecessary updates
    
*   What you see is what you sign. You need to be aware of what you are signing, and of the expected result after the signed transaction is sent out. Don't do things that will make you regret afterwards
    
*   Pay attention to system security updates. Apply them as soon as they are available
    
*   Don't download ＆ install programs recklessly can actually prevent most risks
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/safety-tip#id-4.-bei-dao-le-zen-me-ban)

4\. What to do if assets stolen

Almost all Web3 users have been stolen in their web3 journey. We recommend that users whose funds have been stolen fill out [the SlowMist Security Team's stolen application form](https://aml.slowmist.com/recovery-funds.html)
 , which can track the hacker's address and try to recover the funds

1) Stop loss first Stop loss is about limiting your loss. It can be broken down to at least two phases:

*   The Immediate Action Phase. Act immediately! If you see hackers are transferring your assets, think no more. Just Hurry up and transfer the remaining assets to a safe place. If you have experience in front running trades, just grab and run. Depending on the type of asset, if you can freeze your assets on the blockchain, do it as soon as possible; if you can do on-chain analysis and find your assets are transferred into a centralized exchange, you can contact their risk control department
    
*   The Post-Action Phase. Once the situation is stabilized, your focus should be on making sure there would not be secondary or tertiary attacks
    

2) Protect the scene When you find that something is wrong, stay calm and take a deep breath. Do remember to protect the scene. Here are a few suggestions:

*   If the accident happens on a computer, server or other devices connected to the Internet, disconnect the network immediately while keeping the devices on with power supply
    
*   Unless you are capable of handling this by yourself, waiting for security professionals to step in for analysis is always the better choice
    

3) Analyze the causes

*   The purpose of analyzing the cause is to understand how the assets were stolen: private key theft/TG account theft/device hacking, etc.
    
*   For example, at least clarify the following points:
    
    *   Summary 1: Who was involved, when did this happen , what has happened, and how much was the total loss?
        
    *   Summary 2: The wallet addresses related to the loss, the wallet address of the hacker, the type of the coin, the quantity of the coin. It could be much clearer with the help of just a single table
        
    

4) Fill out the SlowMist Security Team Theft Application Form

It is recommended that the stolen users fill out [the SlowMist Security Team's stolen application form](https://aml.slowmist.com/recovery-funds.html)
 , which will restrict hackers and related addresses from depositing and withdrawing funds from CEX, and track the hacker's address to try to recover the funds

⚠️GMGN's first purpose is security, there is no loophole that leads to the transfer of wallet balances, and in case of theft, please check yourself according to the above-listed situations. GMGN does not perform any operations on the user's wallet, and we do not have the ability to transfer any user's wallet balance.

[PreviousQ＆A](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/q-a)
[NextMEME](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/meme)

*   [2\. Anti-stolen: Take precautions in plugin wallets and TG wallets](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/safety-tip#id-2.-fang-dao-zai-cha-jian-qian-bao-yi-ji-tg-qian-bao-zhong-zuo-hao-yu-fang)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FZCZZPDDNgPOwGs235dbj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4317d98-a028-4133-ad5b-8e8918215824&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2599aa7f&sv=2)

MintDisable

"Yes" indicates safety, meaning that the token creator cannot issue additional tokens to manipulate the market

Blacklist

"No" indicates safety, meaning that the project cannot blacklist any wallet's transactions, reducing the risk of financial entrapment "Yes" means you are on the blacklist of this token developer, you cannot sell this token, it will remind you that your wallet is frozen

Burnt

Displaying the burn pool percentage: the higher the ratio, the better, with 100% indicating that the project cannot withdraw from the liquidity pool

Top 10

"Yes" indicates a relatively safe condition, meaning that the total holdings of the top 10 token holders are less than 30% of the total supply

Insiders

Wallets that did not buy tokens after trading opened, but hold tokens, may indicate that the token creator's holdings were transferred to multiple wallets to secretly sell off. Typically, legitimate projects distribute these through airdrops to users, and it is necessary to check the official Twitter for any airdrop events

# Q＆A | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/q-a#q-how-to-query-token-ca-smart-money-walllet-informations-within-your-tg-group)

Q1: How to Filter the Right Quality Meme at GMGN


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Many newfish aren't clear about how to screen the right tokens, and will only look for popular coins, but usually the price of popular coins are high, they have passed the early growth stage, It's a risky time to buy. Behind the question of how to filter high-quality meme is that you don't know how to judge the signals conveyed by various indicators of a meme through the data provided by GMGN, resulting in the inability to select a portion of the meme that you think has potential and is safer. 2) Initially you can focus on the security of a meme first, and it is recommended that you should check out these pages: [⚡How to become a Degen](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/how-to-become-a-degen)
 [🎯Insider Traders,Snipers,First 70 Buyers](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/insider-traders-snipers-first-70-buyers)
 [🆗CA Security Checks](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/ca-security-checks)
 3) You can choose to follow the smart money before forming your own meme trading system: GMGN has big data on smart money, after follow smart money, you can receive real-time trading dynamics of smart money. Especially with the release of the new meme coin,there is a concentrated entry of smart money. details： [💰Track Smart Money](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/track-smart-money)
 4) GMGN can only provide you with data, this article is not as investment advice, specific meme selection ideas, trading strategies; Position selection and so on need to be gradually improved after you get started.

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/q-a#q2-jin-fang-jia-mao-guan-li-si-xin-guan-li-yuan-yong-yuan-bu-hui-zhu-dong-si-xin-ni)

Q2: Beware of fake adminis private messages. GMGN group admins will never DM you private messages first.


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Recently, many users have been sent private messages by scammers pretending to be administrators, claiming to solve problems. Users sent private keys to them or clicked on fraudulent links, which led to the theft of their wallets. We would like to remind all users to be careful. GMGN official administrators will never take the initiative to send private messages to anyone, nor will they ask you for private keys. 2) Case of fraudulent account disguised management: hide the user name (user name area), write the real administrator's username in the introduction to confuse users, and commit fraud. The picture shows a fraudulent account. Please be careful to distinguish and do not trust anyone who takes the initiative to send you private messages.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FL8Io8Fhi0hSGIkHQkGla%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D730f6f51-be0e-474d-b660-74e70c76b946&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7e50d9&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/q-a#q3-how-to-open-the-browser-console-to-assist-gmgn-in-resolving-your-issue)

Q3: How to Open the Browser Console to Assist GMGN in Resolving Your Issue


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 1: Record the Issue

*   Take a full-screen screenshot of the problem, preferably record a video.
    

Step 2: Open Console and Take Screenshots

*   Right-click a blank area of the webpage in the browser, select “Inspect.” It will automatically open Developer Tools; click “Console”
    
*   Drag the Console area larger, and look for red error messages (marked red or labeled “Error”)
    
*   Take screenshots including all red errors, yellow warnings, prioritizing the earliest error, and capture as much content as possible
    

Step 3: Contact Support

*   Send the screenshots to customer support, or DM the official Twitter account.
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FxTtn84NyWL6e51FJYpLl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De378fe3d-0882-4d00-a9a8-24ebaee6df0c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40a99956&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/q-a#q4-webpage-no-sound-issue)

Q4: Webpage No Sound Issue


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you've already checked the Chrome webpage sound toggle, GMGN notification settings, and the notification sound switches for various functions in the bottom left corner of the GMGN webpage, but there’s still no sound, you can follow these steps to resolve the issue:

*   Go to Browser Settings: Settings / Privacy and Security / Site Settings / Additional Content Settings / Sound
    
*   Click the "Add" button next to "Allow to play sound," enter gmgn.ai and confirm.
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Ffi0c95R8dgngQptd2HW1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D569d3aa1-3531-4249-bb97-ead36dc4db6b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9787c2f&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/q-a#q5-the-wallet-was-stolen-or-the-balance-of-the-wallet-was-emptied)

Q5: The wallet was stolen or the balance of the wallet was emptied


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Common situation: 1) Whether Android phone, it has clicked an unknown link before, resulting in a Trojan horse or malicious program in the mobile phone/computer. 2) Whether Telegram app is downloaded through official sources; whether third-party Telegram Translator plugin from unknown sources is downloaded. 3) Whether Telegram has authorized an unfamiliar fake bot and the balance in the wallet has been transferred by the scam bot by entering a cell phone number or clicking on a scam link, and it is recommended to identify the same through multiple official GMGN channels before making transactions. 4) The wallet has authorized the scam app, you can enter the wallet to query the authorization list and cancel the unknown authorization. _e.g: some scammers use NFT mint places to win prizes and attract you to sign authorization on the website._ 5) If you need to import or export the private key, it is recommended to partially copy and partially manually enter it to reduce the risk of theft due to Trojan reading the clipboard. ⚠️GMGN's first purpose is security, there is no loophole that leads to the transfer of wallet balances, and in case of theft, please check yourself according to the above-listed situations. GMGN does not perform any operations on the user's wallet, and we do not have the ability to transfer any user's wallet balance. We fully understand the feelings of being stolen, the reason for theft is basically the above mentioned: equipment security problems, the use of fake fraud bot, tg abnormal authorization, etc. These are GMGN official can not control, at present we can only give you some self-checking advice, and tell how to reduce the subsequent risk. Suggest to check: [OKX Web3 ＆ SlowMist: Experience Sharing of "Hundreds of Scams"](https://www.theblockbeats.info/en/news/53517)
 We suggest that stolen users fill out [the Slow Mist Security Team's Stolen Application Form](https://aml.slowmist.com/recovery-funds.html)
, which allows you to track the hacker's address and try to recover funds.

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/q-a#q-how-to-query-token-ca-smart-money-walllet-informations-within-your-tg-group-1)

Q6: Why did you not receive SOL after selling or SOL became WSOL?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) It may be because your slippage and priority fee are set too high, and the principal is less, resulting in actual losses after selling, mistakenly thinking that SOL has not received, and the SOL balance in the wallet has not increased. eg: Someone sold a total of 0.12SOL, but gave a priority fee of 0.2SOL and asked us why he did not receive SOL 2) It's possible that because you have WSOL in your wallet, the SOL will automatically be converted to WSOL when you sell it; Due to the SOL chain mechanism problem, you may receive WSOL instead of SOL at transaction settlement. GMGN has now launched the exchange WSOL → SOL function, welcome to experience.

Specific steps: Enter /start in our bot @GMGN\_sol\_bot, click the wallet, click Exchange WSOL → SOL to quickly exchange the received WSOL to SOL

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FezNKJH0FgP7wnup6hdWr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63290a03-6852-453b-9974-e08b9c899e0a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4e7c93f&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/q-a#q7-can-not-follow-the-wallet-or-no-data-on-the-follow-page-how-to-solve-it)

Q7：Can not follow the wallet or no data on the follow page, how to solve it


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Logout and re-sign, connect to the wallet and see if it is solved. 2) If there is still no data, clean up the webpage cookie can be solved. Take google chrome as an example: Settings--Privacy and security--Third-party cookies--See all site data and permissions--Clean up gmgn data.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F1NwNPL0JBOq8xMlmnJGX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c23f611-4922-4c39-8813-66e53a65f1f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aeb95d6e&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/q-a#q-how-to-query-token-ca-smart-money-walllet-informations-within-your-tg-group-2)

 2) Data API：GMGN is no plan to open data API at present, but we will open the data crawling IP whitelist for trading users.What we care about is whether you have brought us: Transaction Volume/User volume. You must at least satisfy one of them, Otherwise the application will not be approved. details： [🤝🏻 Cooperation-API: 🔄Access data API](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-api-data-crawling-ip-whitelist)

 3）Set admin role for the bot（p3） 4）Group administrator send **/set**, add smart money wallet and referral code in the Settings（p4） Click [here](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-referral-invite-bots-to-telegram-group-to-earn-trading-commissions-automatically)
 for detailed tutorials

# FOLLOW: Monitor Square/ Follow/ Watchlist | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/follow-monitor-square-follow-watchlist#follow-page-overview)

FOLLOW Page Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FJPXIhvYnRriPr8RYxBiK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b9f230b-6a53-466e-8149-f4005bdd8455&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ece85fb8&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/follow-monitor-square-follow-watchlist#id-1.-monitor-square)

1\. Monitor Square


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fc6RNMK1w3sWLeTFKchRO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea3df868-f4ff-4aa1-a90f-ed6227230d54&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b891bd9&sv=2)

GMGN Monitor Square allows you to view the all inflow of funds in all your followed wallets, helping you to catch the GEM in time

*   You can freely choose the follow inflow time range 1m/5m/1h/6h/24h
    
*   You can see various data of tokens, including MCap, transaction volume, social media and other information
    
*   Click the icon in the lower left corner could hides the tokens you are not interested in.
    
*   You can buy with one click by using the Quick Buy button in the lower right corner
    
*   The list on the left can also directly view the ollowing inflow information
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/follow-monitor-square-follow-watchlist#id-2.-follow)

2\. Follow


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FvpszIRxOqBA8fJWmI0ED%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26078afe-7884-4dad-ab7e-8e8197edc306&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95b94cb3&sv=2)

*   Click on the red area to automatically redirect to the Telegram page and follow the official GMGN signal bot
    
*   Click on the wallet address to view the wallet details page you are interested in: [Wallet detail page](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/wallet-detail-page)
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/follow-monitor-square-follow-watchlist#id-3.-watchlist)

**3\. Watchlist**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FRSPxfICZZCpggIlLR8BJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd03655b6-c2df-41bb-8019-82364be2fdd3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f12e03fa&sv=2)

*   Supports grouping your collect tokens, click the little star to the left of the token to add the token to your custom grouping list
    

**Token Notes / Renames**

**Web**

On Web, click the **edit** icon next to a token name to add or edit a note. Token notes are now supported across all major token lists and pages.

**H5 (mobile web)**

On the **Trenches** page in mobile web, you can also tap the edit icon next to a token to add a note, so you can tag tokens directly in your browser.

**GMGN App**

In the GMGN App, go to the bottom **Discover** tab and open the **Favorites** list. Long-press any token to rename it or add a custom note, making it easier to label and manage your key tokens on mobile.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FmfaA87IgGKwPMT8itA8A%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e334e73-9fe4-462d-9ea2-367dd57dfad2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2d98e19&sv=2)

*   Click to view your favorite token transaction details page: [Token page: Chart - multicharts, Activity, Trading system](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system)
    

[PreviousHOLDING](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/holding)
[NextALERT: Sniper New, Following, Limit Orders](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/alert-sniper-new-following-limit-orders)

# ALERT: Sniper New, Following, Limit Orders | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/alert-sniper-new-following-limit-orders#id-1.-sniper-new)

1\. Sniper New:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/alert-sniper-new-following-limit-orders#web-signal-page-bottom-signal-tab)

Web – Signal page (bottom “Signal” tab)

From the bottom **Signal** tab you can open the Signal page and see multiple types of market signals, including:

*   **Dex Paid** signals – Dex Paid Ad, Dex Boost Paid, Dex Bar Paid, Update Social, etc.
    
*   **Price Alert** – Price Up, ATH, Key MC and other price-based triggers
    
*   **Other Signals** – Pump Live, CTO and more special events
    

You can filter by **Age**, **MC** and **Total Fees**, and quickly sort for tokens with strong moves and high attention

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/alert-sniper-new-following-limit-orders#gmgn-app-ai-signal)

GMGN App – AI Signal

In the GMGN App, go to the bottom **Monitor** tab and switch to the top **AI Signal** tab to:

*   View AI-curated, high-quality token signals
    
*   Tap a signal to open the **Token Detail** page for deeper analysis and instant **Buy** execution
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/alert-sniper-new-following-limit-orders#id-2.-wallet-tracker)

2\. **Wallet Tracker**:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Web – Wallet Tracker**

On the **Wallet Tracker** page (bottom **Wallet Tracker** tab), you can see all activity from the wallets you track, turn on GMGN web notifications, and connect the **0-Delay Bot** to receive real-time trade alerts for these wallets

**GMGN App – Wallet tracking**

In the GMGN App:

*   Go to the bottom **Track** tab
    
*   Switch to the top **Track** tab to view the list of wallets you are tracking
    
*   Switch to the **Wallet Tracker** tab to see their latest buy/sell actions
    
*   Turn on app notifications to receive push alerts whenever these tracked wallets make new trades
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FPGobtOItSYyCPXeO8rJe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f1a2a58-f2cf-4968-bd93-173e259b8a18&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b011beea&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/alert-sniper-new-following-limit-orders#id-3.-order-management)

**3\. Order Management:**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Web – Orders on the token page**

There is no standalone “Open Orders” page anymore. On Web, open any **token detail** page and switch to the bottom **Orders** tab. Here you can view and manage all of your orders for this token, including **Limit**, **Auto Trading**, **Migrated Snipe**, **Sell on Dev Sell**, **Buy on Dev Sell** and **Advanced** strategies.

**GMGN App – Orders under Assets**

In the GMGN App:

*   Go to the bottom **Assets** tab
    
*   In the wallet header, switch to the **Order** tab
    
*   Inside **Order**, you can toggle between **Advanced**, **Limit**, **Auto Trading**, **Dev Sell**, etc., view details of each order and use **Close All Orders** to manage them in one tap
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FI8dMUHChqFc280ohhdS3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1dfd3c6a-eeed-42ad-b3ed-49f37c70ddb4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b5aed2db&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/alert-sniper-new-following-limit-orders#disclaimer-please-check-token-security-audit-before-trading)

⚠️ Disclaimer: Please check token security audit before trading!

[PreviousFOLLOW: Monitor Square/ Follow/ Watchlist](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/follow-monitor-square-follow-watchlist)
[NextWallet detail page](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/wallet-detail-page)

**Suspected phishing wallet:** Token transfer detected

1.  Many phishing-tagged wallets from one token source spread tokens. This fakes a wide range of holders
    
2.  Shady devs airdrop tokens to KOLs/famous wallets, fooling retail into thinking they bought in. phishing icon will warn you

# Wallet Alert on Telegram | GMGN Tutorial

*   Monitor Solana wallet notification Bot [https://t.me/GMGN\_alert\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_alert_bot)
    
*   Monitor ETH wallet notification Bot [https://t.me/GMGN\_ETH\_alert\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_ETH_alert_bot)
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/wallet-alert-on-telegram#id-1.-deng-lu-telegram-zhang-hao)

1\. Log in to your Telegram account


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> Notice:
> 
> 1.  Please check the login account type in the upper right corner to see whether it is a plug-in wallet login or a Telegram account login. If you are not sure, please log out and re-select connect Telegram to log in using a TG account.
>     
> 2.  If you often log in with the plug-in wallet and bind the Telegram Alert Bot, you can continue to receive notifications as long as you do not click to unbind. Once unbinded, rebinding to Telegram is not supported yet. You need to export the follow list to the Telegram account follow list (see the FAQ below for this tutorial).
>     

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FRgzKrK1w9TsmVCgAVlZt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a814569-18db-4c46-9845-4797eeed760b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1a17a234&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/wallet-alert-on-telegram#id-2.-guan-zhu-xi-huan-de-cong-ming-qian-qian-bao)

2\. Follow your favorite smart money wallet


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Visit [https://gmgn.ai/discover](https://gmgn.ai/discover)
 to find smart money that is interested

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fi5u88Y3ZEZtrPkqEUlxi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6a41608-cde7-4eab-89bc-9b1e230e7f0a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1bf06575&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/wallet-alert-on-telegram#id-3.-tg-bot-jian-kong-qian-bao-jiao-yi-xiao-xi-tong-zhi)

3\. TG Bot monitors wallet transaction message notifications


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Visit Telegram Alert Bot to receive transaction notifications from your followed wallets.

> Note: The website can follow up to 100 wallets; the /add command in Telegram Alert Bot can follow up to 10 wallets

*   Monitor Solana Wallet Notification Bot [https://t.me/GMGN\_alert\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_alert_bot)
    
*   Monitor ETH wallet notification Bot [https://t.me/GMGN\_ETH\_alert\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_ETH_alert_bot)

4\. Set up notifications


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 and click on the right side of the follow list to close the notification

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FpBVKegxpidB5cizW0glA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabde7cca-e19f-4070-a724-ed5130e57b5d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86daf83b&sv=2)

Visit Telegram Alert Bot, send command /set, you can choose all /only buy /only sell

5\. Frequently Asked Questions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/wallet-alert-on-telegram#id-1.-cha-jian-qian-bao-deng-lu-shi-ru-he-bang-ding-telegram-alert-bot)

**1\. How to bind Telegram Alert Bot when logging in to the plugin wallet?**

A: The plugin wallet does not support binding to Telegram Alert Bot. Please export your plugin wallet follow list and then import it into the follow list of the log-in Telegram account. Specific steps:

1) Visit the GMGN website and select the plugin wallet to log in

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FT42tV1n8j96UuYAxO30u%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df10a1a8f-00fe-45ea-8e09-5a972bb8b004&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bca2a6aa&sv=2)

2) Visit [https://gmgn.ai/follow](https://gmgn.ai/follow)
 and select Batch Export Wallet Address and Note Name

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FJWVTUpAlw1Cj8SHjGGbL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24582cd5-7424-4d4b-9958-e3f21b4622f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e58c7ea3&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FjvIf9pYqP4cxuF6wooFJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87054ea9-33d7-4979-8ea5-adb06dfa2f1f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ec0758f&sv=2)

3) Log out of the plugin wallet, re-login to Telegram, visit [https://gmgn.ai/follow](https://gmgn.ai/follow)
 , and select bulk import of wallet addresses and notes.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FT2db7YmEu4pc1y73TqS0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d51f147-c86f-42cf-9461-002d81c9a7b4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94abee8&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/wallet-alert-on-telegram#id-2.-jian-kong-qian-bao-tong-zhi-diu-xiao-xi)

2\. Monitor wallet notifications for lost messages

answer:

1.  **Reason 1: Telegram message notifications push frequency limit**
    

> Telegram limits the number of messages that can be sent per second for each bot application. The more people use the bot, the more messages are pushed, and the more likely it is that Telegram will limit the rate. GMGN cannot currently solve the problem of message push being limited.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FBNtQhA7eVGgcwFhgzVaP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94a2ce13-e301-45e3-933b-e1b841ef7a26&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d127d02&sv=2)

1.  **Reason 2: The plugin wallet has been unbound：**
    

Because Telegram Alert Bot message = plugin wallet login follow list + Telegram login account follow list. If the plugin wallet is unbound from TG, the notification bot will only push the TG login follow list.

> Solution: You can bulk export the follow list of the plug-in wallet, and then import it into the attention list of TG login, and support retaining the note name

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FLOsdpPOBq2OVL7NGlChV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D609f48d0-84d5-4d9d-b2e3-dd1db38fdb06&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d0e260b8&sv=2)

1.  **Reason 3: The Telegram notification switch may be turned off. Please check** [**https://gmgn.ai/follow**](https://gmgn.ai/follow)
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fc8HjAx3iIDHPls1AYs56%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a1f04ea-8532-46d7-aba4-5ae9785298b1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36072052&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/wallet-alert-on-telegram#id-3.-cha-jian-qian-bao-deng-lu-de-lao-yong-hu-ru-he-huan-bang-telegram-alert-bot-li-yi-bang-ding-de)

3\. How to change the plug-in wallet bound to Telegram Alert Bot for old users who have logged in with the plug-in wallet

Answer: Telegram Alert Bot does not allow changing the plugin wallet address. It can be unbound, but it is not allowed to be bound again after unbinding. You can only use TG to log in on the GMGN website and receive wallet notifications followed by the TG account.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fa77fdJoMxDlqgxKdyLwf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b9cfbc9-f47a-4338-bcb3-5188aaed17f2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ce015db&sv=2)

# Wallet detail page | GMGN Tutorial

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F4gcQzDnykvfkBWnqTuF9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38b894b1-c96f-4876-9df0-63338c0b54df&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=660effb5&sv=2)

**Upper functional modules:**

*   Click the button next to the wallet name to make a note of the wallet name
    
*   Click the button next to the contract address to copy the CA or jump to solscan.io to query wallet activities
    
*   Click on the tweet to jump to the wallet address of the wallet owner
    
*   Click on Wallet Copy to copy the transactions of that wallet. For details, please see: [Wallet Copy Trade: Copy Smart Money, automatically earn SOL!](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/copy-trade-copy-smart-money-automatically-earn-sol)
    
*   After you tap **Follow**, the wallet will be added to your tracked list. You can review all of its activity on the **Wallet Tracker** page (bottom _Wallet Tracker_ tab on Web) and connect the **0-Delay Bot** to receive real-time trade alerts for this wallet.
    
*   In the **GMGN App**, go to the bottom **Track** tab, then switch to the top **Follow** tab to see all wallets you follow. Switch to the **Activity** tab to view their latest buy/sell actions. Turn on app notifications to receive push alerts whenever these tracked wallets place new trades.
    

**Recent 7D/30D profit and loss/win rate:**

*   View the wallet's recent D profit and loss ratio and fund profit and loss amount
    
*   Check the current win rate and balance of the wallet
    

**PNL:**

7D TXS

7D/30D transcations numbers：Bought is green/ Sale is red

Totnl PNL

Total profit and loss

Unrealized Profits

The current unsold value of the tokens in this wallet

7D/30D AVG Duration

7D/30D average holding time

7D/30D Total Cost

Total cost of buying tokens in the last 7 days/30 days

7D/30D Token Avg Cost

In the last 7 days/30 days. The total cost of buying tokens divided by the number of tokens bought

7D/30D Token Avg Realized Profits

Average realized profit of each ghostwriter’s sold portion in the last 7 days/30 days (excluding unrealized profit)

**Distribution:**

*   You can see the increase or decrease of the amount and quantity of tokens purchased by the wallet in the last 7 days/30 days.
    

**Phishing check:**

Blacklist

The wallet bought the number of blacklist/ honeypot tokens. If it is too much, it may be a phishing wallet of the cabal team

Didn’t buy:

The number of non-bought tokens in the wallet can be used to analyze how many tokens are transferred from other wallets, thereby analyzing the wallet attributes

Sold > Bought

The number of tokens sold by this wallet is greater than the number of tokens bought

Buy/Sell within 10 secs

The number of tokens that complete buy/sell transactions within ten seconds. This may be a bot or a wallet that farm copy trade users

[PreviousALERT: Sniper New, Following, Limit Orders](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/alert-sniper-new-following-limit-orders)
[NextToken page: Chart - multicharts, Activity, Trading system](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system)

Last updated 24 days ago

# Cooking | GMGN Tutorial

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FNDJTSSgGfPgnPRmgkcTj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c616ece-0cda-4cf2-b36b-a5eafbe10443&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f1866226&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooking#tui-te-gua-dao-shuo-ming)

Cooking Instructions:

*   Use the GMGN Cooking function to quickly launch your token. GMGN charges 0 token launch fees！！！
    
*   Multiple ways to quickly issue tokens: Top cooking icon, Token re-launch, X Tracker cooking, Cooking via part of a tweet
    
    ![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FTwN4jt0gupwMeZZdZ3gF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52013b89-d2db-4da7-b34a-129fc2af60a4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a734adb8&sv=2)
    
*   Optional launchpads: Bonk, Pump
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FLkTTguuEwOW65KgZY4Le%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D04feb2e8-806f-409e-9330-59f182290a1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6544ed29&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooking#cooking-settings)

Cooking Settings：

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooking#id-1-choose-lunchpad)

1）Choose Lunchpad:

*   Offering Bonk and Pump; you can freely choose one for the cooking
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooking#id-2-select-image)

2）Select Image:

*   Supports custom token image upload
    
*   when you use Token re-launch or Cooking via part of a tweet. It will automatically fetch the image and use it as an option
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooking#id-3-ticker-and-coin-name)

3) Ticker and Coin Name

*   "Ticker" refers to the abbreviated symbol or shorthand for a token or cryptocurrency
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooking#id-4-social-media-link)

4）Social media link

*   Fill in your token's social media links, supporting X, Website, Telegram community links
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooking#id-5-dev-wallet-and-buy-token)

5) Dev Wallet and Buy Token

*   Select a single wallet as the dev wallet address for the token
    
*   Purchase at least 0.1 SOL and please reserve a portion of your balance for the launch fee on this launchpad. GMGN does not charge any cooking fee

# Auto Trading: Migrated Sell | GMGN Tutorial

Rule:

*   All SOL chain ungraduated tokens can set up Migrated Sell
    
*   Only when you complete settings and click create before the DEX has added official liquidity pool, your Migrated Sell order will be triggered
    
*   One token can only create one Migrated Sell task, and cannot be created after DEX adds official LP
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-migrated-sell#id-1.-raydium-kai-pan-zi-dong-ju-ji-web-duan)

1\. Migrated Sell - web version

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fj84DHwYcNgQIaLs7WxNP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8a114161-e299-4a09-9368-5bfc2999150c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=21f782ab&sv=2)

1) Create Migrated Sell task:

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FUbEtUfBJBJnfMQExVM7r%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D998a6d6a-d726-43b8-90c0-39006e1690cb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d0dd529&sv=2)

*   Click Auto trading on the pump token page, click Migrated Sell and enter the editing page
    
*   Set Sell Holdings ratio
    
*   Set slippage, priority fee, anti-MEV, and click save
    
*   After the settings are completed, click create in any ungraduated token you want to sell. The token will auto sell the amount of holding ratio you set when DEX adds official LP
    

2) View or delete your Migrated Sell task:

*   In the token page - Orders, you can view your current Migrated Sell tasks and could view or delete them
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FrZnjWXC76pzRNzu5aSbX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5aa0acd8-8300-44e9-af07-79d31175c78a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ad7e8baa&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-migrated-sell#id-2.-raydium-kai-pan-zi-dong-ju-ji-bot-duan)

2\. Migrated Sell- bot vision


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Create Migrated Sell task:

*   When you enter a ungraduated token contract address into the bot, you will see the Raydium Sell option, and you can set the selling ratiot of this token
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FyZtXPGTfRY36tRTsYChj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D619f7252-66e5-4162-94de-bff42943b7e0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d9642bd&sv=2)

2) Adjust Migrated Sell settings:

*   In the settings, you can click on Raydium Sell xx %, enter the holding ratio you want to sell in reply box when the token launchs DEX, and you can complete the change
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FLpbzjPGBXN5VmeHIuChl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50bd772b-b7ab-44d6-947a-0fd02950a0b0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dcc0df05&sv=2)

3) View or delete your Migrated Sell tasks:

*   Currently, the GMGN TG bot does not support viewing the Migrated Sell tasks. Please go to the GMGN site Auto trading dashboard to view it
    

[PreviousAuto Trading: Migrated Snipe](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-migrated-snipe)
