# Transaction/Limit Order failure | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#jian-yi-shi-bai-yong-hu-shou-xian-jian-cha-hua-dian-bi-li-you-xian-fei-fang-jia-mo-shi-she-zhi)

Suggest failed users check the slippage ratio, priority fee, and anti-MEV settings first


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Slippage ratio: Manual buy/sell is recommended to be automatic; auto buy/sell and other limit order operations recommend slippage of 30%-35%; for new and popular coins,suggest 50% or more
    
*   If there is no requirement for transaction speed, suggest 0.002 SOL ; for auto buy/sell and other limit orders, suggest 0.006 SOL or above. If the transaction amount is greater than 1 SOL,suggest 0.01 SOL or above
    
*   Enabling the anti-MEV mode can effectively prevent transactions from being sandwiched by MEV bots, but enabling the anti-MEV mode requires a priority fee of at least 0.002 SOL
    

✅Tips: To learn about common fees/settings such as slippage and priority fees, please click: [GMGN Fees and Common Fees/Settings](https://docs-gmgn-ai.translate.goog/cn/~/changes/WZ0l4KjzcPDGB69hW3nh/gmgn-shou-xu-fei-he-chang-jian-fei-yong-she-zhi)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#jiao-yi-chao-shi-shi-bai-yuan-yin)

Transaction timeout/failure reason


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#id-1.-jiao-yi-zhuang-tai-huo-qu-chao-shi-yuan-yin-ji-jie-jue-ban-fa)

**1\. Reasons and solutions for timeout in obtaining transaction status**

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Fw8HX4KFUA2MEu1Zx610H%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02365c00-9cd3-4c3a-b303-5c803db32147&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b58982&sv=1)

In most cases, it is caused by low priority fees and slippage settings in the wallet; the transaction may be successful even if it is timed out, and you need to check the status on the chain

Error number

Transaction timeout reason

Solution

A1

The priority fee is low, the node packaging speed is slow, and it is easy to time out after the countdown ends.

Increase priority fees

A2

The slippage is low and cannot be triggered when the token price fluctuates greatly (such as violent fluctuations )

Increase slippage ratio

A3

Anti-MEV RPC service failure

Switch to normal mode (turn off anti-pinch)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#id-2.-jiao-yi-shi-bai-yuan-yin-ti-jiao-shi-bai-zhi-xing-shi-bai-wu-ke-yong-lu-you)

**2\. Reasons for transaction failure (submission failure/execution failure/no available route)**

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FyXT91Smd1LmUX1TuyJcc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3926aede-4d5c-4d97-a361-11cd06bff7c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e9498b96&sv=1)![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FKuA11JxA5zi1SkSO9qAV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5d6569d0-dd1e-48a5-872e-bc1c0b65f631&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bdc09011&sv=1)

1) Transaction submission failed (not uploaded to the chain):

Error number

Reasons for transaction submission failure

Solution

B1

Insufficient wallet balance. The wallet SOL balance is insufficient for the purchase and sale amount, or insufficient to pay for Gas. It is recommended that the SOL chain wallet reserve an amount of at least 0.05 SOL.

Make sure there is still a certain balance in the wallet after the transaction

B2

Insufficient wallet tokens when selling. When there are no tokens in the wallet, the transaction cannot be submitted.

Check the amount of tokens in your wallet to ensure the selling amount is within the range

B3

The purchase submission failed. The token itself is limited. It may be that the purchase is limited during the initial stage of the project.

You need to find relevant information on the token social media to confirm

B4

The sale submission failed, maybe because the item is Pixiu or you are on the blacklist

If it is confirmed to be a Pixiu/blacklisted, it cannot be sold

B5

The wallet still shows login, but the wallet login status is abnormal at this time

Reconnect your wallet

2) Transaction execution failed (already uploaded to the chain):

Error number

Reasons for transaction failure

Solution

C1

Usually, the transaction execution fails due to low slippage. Failure to submit to the chain for execution will consume Gas/priority fee.

It is recommended to increase the transaction slippage when the market is in a new market or when the token is in fomo, suggest use auto slippage

3) No available route (not on the chain):

Error number

Reasons for transaction failure

Solution

D1

The token creator/project owner remove Liq, resulting in no available routing

Please confirm whether the project party has burned the pool before trading. Trading will not be possible after the pool is removed

D2

Solana pump.fun, moonshot and other tokens cannot be traded when the token market value reaches $69K and the official is adding a pool and waiting for the opening of Raydium/Meteora DEX

Wait for the token launch to raydium before trading can resume

D3

The sol chain is crowded or there is a problem with the node service provider

If the problem cannot be solved, please give feedback to the community in time.

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#gua-dan-chao-shi-shi-bai-yuan-yin)

Order timeout/failure reason


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#id-1.-wang-ye-bot-gua-dan-yi-ji-zi-dong-hua-jiao-yi-chao-shi)

**1\. Web page/BOT pending orders and automated trading timeouts**

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FbXLQ2Spt5APjRv8sKC1a%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D951c1617-13b7-4f0f-a6f1-b66cce42bec8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7866a9c&sv=1)

In most cases, it is caused by low priority fees and slippage settings in the wallet; the transaction may be successful even if it is timed out, and you need to check the status on the chain

Error number

Reasons for timeout of pending orders and automated trading

Solution

H1

The priority fee is low, the node packaging speed is slow, and it is easy to time out after the countdown ends.

Increase priority fees

H2

The slippage is low and cannot be triggered when the token price fluctuates greatly (such as violent fluctuations such as K-line pins)

Increase slippage ratio

H3

Anti-pinch RPC service failure

Switch to normal mode (turn off anti-pinch)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#id-2.-wang-ye-bot-gua-dan-yi-ji-zi-dong-hua-jiao-yi-shi-bai-gua-dan-wei-chu-fa-gua-dan-chu-fa-dan-ji)

**2\. Web page/BOT pending orders and automated transactions failed (pending orders not triggered/pending orders triggered but transaction failed/no available routing)**

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FyXT91Smd1LmUX1TuyJcc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3926aede-4d5c-4d97-a361-11cd06bff7c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e9498b96&sv=1)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F53CZDFaURGMPYLbaPAca%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09721340-300e-4f57-9322-9008b0941268&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a063cf02&sv=2)

1) Limit order creation failed:

Error number

Reasons why limit order creation failed

Solution

G1

The network is unstable

Please try refreshing the page to recreate the limit order

2) Limit order is not triggered (not uploaded to the chain):

Error number

Reasons why limit orders are not triggered

Solution

J1

Due to the pin, it is mistakenly believed that the limit order price has been reached, but it cannot actually be triggered

The pin insertion situation basically cannot be triggered, which is a normal situation and does not need to be solved

J2

If you place an order or perform other operations on the web page, the wallet may still show login, but the login status of the wallet may be abnormal.

Reconnect your wallet

3) Limit order is triggered but the transaction fails:

Error number

Reasons why limit order is triggered but transaction fails

Solution

K1

After the limit order is triggered due to low slippage, the submission to the chain fails to execute, which will consume Gas/priority fee (already on the chain)

Increase transaction slippage, such as automatically or by more than 30%

K2

The wallet balance is insufficient when the order is triggered, the wallet SOL balance is insufficient for the order amount, or insufficient to pay for Gas. It is recommended that the SOL chain wallet reserve amount is at least greater than 0.05 (not on the chain)

Make sure there is still a certain balance in the wallet to execute the order after the order is successfully placed

K3

When the sell order is triggered, there are not enough tokens in the wallet. When there are no tokens in the wallet, the transaction cannot be made (not on the chain)

Check the amount of tokens in your wallet

K4

The buy order failed. The token itself is limited. It may be the initial purchase time limit of the project (not on the chain).

You need to find relevant information on token social media

K5

The sell order failed, maybe because the project is Pixiu or you are on the blacklist (not on the chain)

If it is confirmed to be a Pixiu/blacklisted, it cannot be sold

4) No available route (not on the chain):

Error number

No route available reason

Solution

L1

The token creator/project owner remove Liq, resulting in no available routing

Please confirm whether the project party has burned the pool before trading. Trading will not be possible after the pool is removed

L2

Solana pump.fun, moonshot and other tokens cannot be traded when the token market value reaches $69K and the official is adding a pool and waiting for the opening of Raydium/Meteora DEX

Wait for the token launch to raydium before trading can resume

L3

SOL chain is crowded or there is a problem with the node service provider

If the problem cannot be solved, please give feedback to the community in time.

✅Tips: If the execution fails, you can go to [https://solscan.io/](https://solscan.io/)
 to query the failure hash to understand the failure reason

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#tg-qian-bao-jiao-yi-bao-cuo-xin-xi)

TG wallet transaction error information

Check the TG wallet transaction error information and match it with the error number above to find out the timeout/failure reason. We cannot count the transaction error information of the web3 plug-in wallet, so we do not collect it.

TG Wallet transaction error message

Error number

Other reasons

trade\_error\_0x1: "Insufficient funds in wallet.",

B1

trade\_error\_0x11: "Account is frozen.",

B2/B3

trade\_error\_0x1e: "Exceeds desired slippage limit.",

C1

trade\_error\_0x28: "Insufficient funds in pool.",

D1

trade\_error\_0xbc4: "Duplicate submission is invalid.",

The transaction order has been submitted

trade\_error\_0x1773: "Exceeds desired slippage limit.",

C1

trade\_error\_0x1775: "Liquidity has migrated to Raydium.",

D2

trade\_errtrade\_error\_40001300: "haven't bind tg",

The login status is abnormal, please log in to your TG wallet account again.

ttrade\_error\_40001400: "build withdraw tx error",

B1

B2

G1

TG Wallet limid order error message

K2

J1/H1/2/3

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#ru-guo-reng-ran-dui-jiao-yi-shi-bai-chao-shi-yuan-yin-you-yi-wen-ke-yi-dao-gmgn-guan-fang-she-qun-zh)

**If you still have questions about the reasons for transaction failure/timeout, you can go to the GMGN official community to provide feedback. ✈️ GMGN community:** [**https://t.me/gmgnai**](https://t.me/gmgnai)

*   [1\. Reasons and solutions for timeout in obtaining transaction status](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#id-1.-jiao-yi-zhuang-tai-huo-qu-chao-shi-yuan-yin-ji-jie-jue-ban-fa)
    
*   [2\. Reasons for transaction failure (submission failure/execution failure/no available route)](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#id-2.-jiao-yi-shi-bai-yuan-yin-ti-jiao-shi-bai-zhi-xing-shi-bai-wu-ke-yong-lu-you)
    
*   [Order timeout/failure reason](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#gua-dan-chao-shi-shi-bai-yuan-yin)
    
*   [1\. Web page/BOT pending orders and automated trading timeouts](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#id-1.-wang-ye-bot-gua-dan-yi-ji-zi-dong-hua-jiao-yi-chao-shi)

Web page/BOT pending orders and automated transactions failed (pending orders not triggered/pending orders triggered but transaction failed/no available routing)](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure#id-2.-wang-ye-bot-gua-dan-yi-ji-zi-dong-hua-jiao-yi-shi-bai-gua-dan-wei-chu-fa-gua-dan-chu-fa-dan-ji)

# CopySignal: Copy Trade with PUMP CTO Signal | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/copysignal-copy-trade-with-pump-cto-signal#pump-cto-signal)

PUMP CTO Signal


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a community take over issue (CTO) happens to a token launched with PUMP.FUN on Solana, the GMGN Sniper Bot will automatically buy the token according to your preset parameters and token filters. Please DYOR before copy trading with PUMP CTO Signals.

**PUMP CTO signal history preview** [https://t.me/gmgnsignals/42382](https://t.me/gmgnsignals/42382)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/copysignal-copy-trade-with-pump-cto-signal#copy-signal-dashboard)

Copy Signal Dashboard


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Visit GMGN Sniper Bot [https://t.me/GMGN\_sol\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)
    
2.  Send `/copysignal` command to the Bot or tap Copy Signal button on `/start` dashboard.
    
3.  PUMP CTO Status:
    
    🟢 indicates copy buying is enabled
    
    🔴 indicates copy buying is disabled
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F6Aev2J1sW4JA8Jc7jXAk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbfae1890-9ce5-4d86-a161-9be706068385&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b6796d85&sv=2)

/start dashboard

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F2HSyVPL7oOl9f6qYuikz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D973cafb5-0013-49dd-a165-e331ce60148e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd6abc0&sv=2)

Copy Signal Dashboard

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/copysignal-copy-trade-with-pump-cto-signal#pump-cto-setting)

PUMP CTO Setting


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FEePrqt7tqwTa4uOZTS8P%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa9e6009-60ab-4ce7-8af8-5225fbcf7f44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2d226f9&sv=2)

1.  You might notice that Trade Signals might be sent frequently, which may quickly cost your SOL balance. Please set your preferred token filters, and tap the 'Auto Sell' button to enable the Auto TP/SL orders. (Tap `/autosell` to set presets) to control trading risk.
    
2.  Auto Buy Status:
    

🟢 On: Indicates copy buying is enabled

🔴 Off: Indicates copy buying is disabled

1.  Trade Settings for Copy Trading with PUMP CTO Signal:
    
    1.  Buy: Set the SOL amount you want to buy with each triggered trading signal
        
    2.  Buy Tip: Set the gas fee (tip fee included) for each buy transaction triggered by trading signals
        
    3.  Buy Slippage: Set the slippage for each buy transaction triggered by trading signals
        
    4.  Buy Anti-MEV Status: If enabled (🟢 On), buy transaction will be sent to Anti-MEV rpc (JITO for Solana)
        
    5.  Auto Sell Status: If enabled (🟢 On), take-profit/stop-loss limit orders will be created automatically when buy transaction confirmed. NOTICE: please preset Auto Sell parameters with sending `/autosell` command to the bot.
        
    
2.  Token Filters for Copy Trading with PUMP CTO Signal:
    
    1.  Min Liq: Set the minimum pool liquidity value of the token for copy buying
        
    2.  Max MC: Set the maximum market cap value of the token for copy buying
        
    3.  Max Holders: Set the maximum number of token holders for copy buying
        
    4.  Max Open: Set the maximum time period after the token opens trading for copy buying
        
    5.  Min 5m Vol: Set the minimum 5-minute trading volume of the token for copy buying
        
    6.  Min 5m TXs: Set the minimum 5-minute trading transactions of the token for copy buying
        
    
3.  To reset token filters, please reply with "none" or "0" while editing.
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/copysignal-copy-trade-with-pump-cto-signal#pump-cto-copy-trading-sample)

PUMP CTO Copy Trading Sample

**Low Latency Wallet Tracking Bot**

Exclusive private node, push channel acceleration, millisecond-level monitoring speed, one-click fast transaction, **breaking the upper limit of 500 monitored wallets** (log in with multiple accounts and fill in the same group ID when configuring). Please visit [https://gmgn.ai/follow/?chain=sol&tab=follow](https://gmgn.ai/follow/?chain=sol&tab=follow)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F80kEvvTdti0QLiVHYY8j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D014030b5-28c8-4bc9-ae30-cca2f98b1e6d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=625f7807&sv=2)

**Frequently Asked Questions**

**Q: Why can’t test messages be sent?**

**Solution:** In general, group IDs starting with -4 or -1 can be used to send test messages. If your Telegram account is registered with a virtual phone number, it may trigger Telegram’s security risk controls, causing the bot to fail to send messages within the group you created.

To troubleshoot:

1\. Try typing /groupid in the group. If @GMGN\_vip\_bot can send a response, it indicates that the group permissions are configured correctly.

2\. If the bot does not respond, try adding @GMGN\_vip\_bot as a group admin or invite a few more friends to the group. Then, try sending the /groupid command again to check if the bot can send messages.

Note: The group ID is not permanent. As the number of group members increases, the group ID may change from starting with -4 to starting with -1. In such cases, you will need to reconfigure the bot form for instant notifications.

**Setup steps:**

1.  Click to create a Telegram group
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FIlkIyz4iNWZ5p4aQNnNL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9370557d-ef12-4e62-9411-98b59aa524fe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a67db337&sv=2)

1.  [Click here](https://t.me/GMGN_vip_bot?startgroup=true)
     to invite Bot [@GMGN\_vip\_Bot](https://t.me/GMGN_vip_bot)
     to the newly created Telegram group. Or click info in the upper right corner of the group, click Add to add members, and search for "@GMGN\_vip\_Bot" (Note that the Bot's unique ID is "@GMGN\_vip\_Bot", do not add other scammers' bots)
    
2.  Copy the group ID, or click the "Create Notification" button to automatically fill in the group ID after jumping
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F8g1J16uj1cclIDVvcJJB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D04307058-551b-4332-9f5a-c29d5f637c71&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57f40261&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F1YwMtjXNnfWNeHqFQG0T%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8161df5a-4614-4312-96cc-1d9928d0fb76&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e68c3c&sv=2)

1.  Create a group bot: Click [@BotFather](https://t.me/BotFather)
     , enter /newbot in the dialog box, fill in the bot name first, then fill in the bot username (must end with "bot" and cannot be repeated with other people's bots). After successful creation, copy the bot API token in the red box in the figure below.
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FVEjO7JCBHT24CqY3KyLf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2acb03e-f479-4cd9-81ff-bc9da2e7d2f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e6b7acc&sv=2)

1.  Paste the bot API token into the form. A maximum of 10 bot tokens can be entered.
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FdErZu04WVgLRvtolOIfx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7570307-3f9d-4b69-bdbd-e80b9a262d29&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4ea1944c&sv=2)

1.  Invite the newly created bot to the Telegram group
    
    ![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FkYGKewGf3H6kl1zXtU9s%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27621609-b381-4151-b630-c9708db43682&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c482a427&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FXdy25ptJb8sA7RROYqT3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bc30e3e-7a60-4d99-ba0b-d83462e75bf0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b07add9&sv=2)

# Trailing Take Profit | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-take-profit#id-1.-how-trailing-take-profit-works)

1\. **How Trailing Take Profit Works:**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When the price hits your profit price, Trailing Take Profit will be activated. If the price continues to rise, the order will be held until the price falls back by the percentage you set, the order will be closed. The drawback is that if the price reverses immediately after the trailing feature is activated, you may lose part of the profits.

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-take-profit#id-2.-trailing-stop-example)

**2\. Trailing Stop Example**：


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

User A creates a Trailing Take Profit order to buy SOL , and set 20% take-profit rate and 5% drawdown. The average buy price is $140. Below is the operational logic of TTP.

**No**

**SOL Price(USD)**

**Take Profit price(USD)**

**TTP status**

**No**

**SOL Price(USD)**

**Take Profit price(USD)**

**TTP status**

1

150

\-

Waiting

2

160

\-

Waiting

3

168

159.6（168 \* （1-5%））

Trailing Sell is active

4

162

159.6

Trailing Sell is active

5

170

161.5（170 \* （1-5%））

Trailing Sell is active

6

180

171（180 \* （1-5%））

Trailing Sell is active

7

190

180.5（190 \* （1-5%））

Trailing Sell is active

7

185

180.5

Trailing Sell is active

8

180.5

180.5

SOL sold at market price, **the profit rate is 28.9%**

**Here are some examples of drawdown parameters:**

*   TP +50%, drawdown percentage 10%
    
*   TP +100%, drawdown percentage 15%
    
*   TP +200%, drawdown percentage 20%
    

Please note that the drawdown ratio should not be set too high. For instance, if a token rises by 100% and then falls by 50%, it will have returned to your buy price, not a 100% drop.

**Click to view:** [**How to Enable Trailing Take Profit**](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-quick-buy-take-profit-stop-loss#how-to-enable-trailing-take-profit)

[PreviousAuto Trading: Quick Buy ＆ Take-Profit / Stop-Loss](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-quick-buy-take-profit-stop-loss)
[NextTrailing Stop Loss](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-stop-loss)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [2\. Trailing Stop Example：](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-take-profit#id-2.-trailing-stop-example)

# 🤝🏻 Cooperation-Referral:📸Share transaction profits | GMGN Tutorial

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FZvNFpZNjjt4eIkZKCs1g%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91d76f51-c91d-4504-8b98-df7dbc87a12a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6bd76dd7&sv=2)

**Method 1:**

Go to the page of the token you hold, and click to share the transaction.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FoNZ7O19lN9iRNmHeG3ad%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dedb56418-face-432d-8b6a-828b89e63dad&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=62e611e1&sv=2)

**Method 2:**

1.  Go to your wallet page (search for your wallet at the top of[https://GMGN.ai](https://gmgn.ai/)
     or log in at the top right, then select "My Wallet" from the dropdown menu to enter).
    
2.  On TABs like Recent PnL, Holdings, Activity, click the share button on the right to share.

# Invite @GMGNAI_BOT | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/invite-gmgnai_bot#id-1.-invite-contract-query-bot-to-your-group)

1\. Invite Contract Query Bot To Your Group


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**@GMGNAI\_BOT** [https://t.me/GMGNAI\_bot](https://t.me/GMGNAI_bot)

**Quick Invite** 👉🏻 [Click here to invite @GMGNAI\_bot to your Telegram Group](https://t.me/GMGNAI_bot?startgroup=true)

**Bot description:**

1) Check Token Analysis: Anyone can send **a token contract address** to the group and the bot will automatically reply with token prices, pool liquidity, insiders and other token analysis data.

2) Check Wallet PnL Analysis: Anyone can send **a wallet address** (Solana Only) to the group and the bot will automatically reply with wallet analysis such as 7d PnL, Realized Profit, Unrealized Profit, Winrate, Holding Token Analysis, Last 5 trades.

Supported Chains: ETH, Solana, Base, BSC

# How to become a Degen | GMGN Tutorial

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/how-to-become-a-degen#if-you-are-new-to-gmgn-and-want-to-try-to-make-money-by-trading-new-tokens-here-are-some-tips-you-sh)

If you are new to GMGN and want to try to make money by trading new tokens, here are some tips you should focus on.

1.Keep an eye on the "Sniper New" section at the bottom left corner of [http://gmgn.ai](http://gmgn.ai/)
. When you see a new coin, click on it and follow these steps:

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FxGyqehaU2iSBz1O7vTeq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dce94c08b-26a4-492f-a81b-6bfcd2e48e31&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5630495&sv=2)

2.Check LP Burned or not: If LP not burned, there's a 60% chance it could be a rug pull.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FoHpDoLc5DTp4qJTuKZy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea900ad9-efcc-42f7-8417-fd341beaa0dc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e167f4ad&sv=2)

3.Inspect Rat Trading: Rat trading holdings should not exceed 20%, and ideally, there should be some present.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fwp6WOzUcDHEpC5SCdlGE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D348c68de-72dc-4c7d-b8b6-4e2ccb12bf0b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c3ca6c8&sv=2)

4.Check Snipers: If a top holder snipes at the opening with less liquidity, there's a 90% chance of a dump, causing instant losses as you buy at the peak of the price, causing momentary losses.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FG5FdpLDM794AO3rbv9yv%252FUntitled.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc65d20e2-a34c-4a76-96c9-305000e000fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12fb5db4&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FmNii65lQ2QRqIhcNwH0f%252FUntitled%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df265fa15-cd1f-4421-8311-2defdfa76867&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d3592de4&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FX6tvnKYpysPt4sO3pqzn%252FUntitled%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D66ceb492-1c87-4ecf-885a-6f0c09bea1e9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ecde088&sv=2)

5.Prefer Larger Pools: Pools with over 100 SOL are preferable. Those with only tens of SOL are susceptible to dumps. However, do not always rely on this pattern, as some scammers may exploit it to deceive you.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fi1j1CdiYkHgtG5uN55qg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27c91af3-625c-4907-b8c2-84da00ee465a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ed4b7620&sv=2)

6.Monitor Opening Trades: Look for genuine trading activity. If there are over 60 trades in the first minute or 600 trades in the first 5 minutes, it indicates real activity, not wash trading.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F0XjJSLaNeSYhxxmddavl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71a94abf-1d34-4842-97cd-4d371b266c1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95b1b309&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FUQoEalzHelOKWwjftnf4%252FUntitled%2520%283%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03441a33-0d7e-492a-a8d8-2933ceb32398&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d91f0da&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FNkAcZ8AQO8z51osMN55U%252FUntitled%2520%284%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc556e80-4596-4c45-9dbf-f558113b5ff0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=824211c5&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/how-to-become-a-degen#disclaimer)

⚠️ **Disclaimer**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# TG Wallet: Connect TG, Multi-Wallet system | GMGN Tutorial

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FgcjA11V8lk7dFrWI4bG1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2cd9379b-9026-410a-b662-bac78a4796fb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=15f362e0&sv=2)

*   Flexibly choose multiple ways to connect to GMGN
    
*   「Connect Telegram, Connect Phantom, App Scan Code Login」 allows you to use Anti-MEV and various GMGN automation functions.Trade with plugin wallet doesn't support these features
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-connect-tg-multi-wallet-system#id-1.-deng-lu-telegram-zhang-hao-gmgn-tg-qian-bao-deng-lu)

1\. Connect Telegram (GMGN TG wallet login)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FoemcQX45uDzDm27ypSbg%252FGroup%25201312322481.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D743f01d9-a1dc-4cd1-a159-4998b08c085e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c16def7d&sv=2)

*   Click Connect in the upper right corner and click Connect Telegram
    
*   After jumping to Telegram site, click Open Telegram to jump to [@gmgnaibot](https://t.me/gmgnaibot)
     login bot
    
*   Then the bot will send a new login link. Click Login Website to complete the TG wallet login site
    
*   When you login with GMGN TG wallet for the first time, a new wallet address will be automatically generated in the corresponding chain; the yellow frame parts are the trading bots corresponding to each chain, click them to enter, please follow this tutorial to export the private key: [TG Wallet: Import ＆ Export private key, Deposit, Withdraw](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw)
    
*   ⚠️ Please note that a login link can only be used once; you can copy the login link to the browser you want to use
    
*   ⚠️ Please note that the multi-wallet system currently only supports direct buy/sell transactions
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-connect-tg-multi-wallet-system#id-2.-duo-qian-bao-guan-li)

2\. Connect Phantom

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FQAHCKOv4Ax1krhSYJMfy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7eb79fc9-11c4-4b6a-8cf6-a8e691580776&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cd97fe3b&sv=2)

*   Support Phantom Wallet for Login, Custodial Account Creation, and Transactions
    
    *   Details: GMGN will create a multi-chain custodial wallet account based on your Phantom wallet (single-chain or multi-chain, requiring at least one Solana chain wallet). New wallet addresses are generated for each chain
        
    *   If you need to log in with Phantom on a new device, please import the same wallet account from the old device into the new device Phantom in advance to ensure that you log in to the same escrow account
        
    
*   **For the safety of user wallet funds, GMGN all chains** ( SOL chain / EVM chain / Tron chain ) **are prohibited from exporting private keys**
    
    *   Phantom's escrow account supports Multi-wallet systems
        
    *   SOL chain Deposit, Withdrawal, Consolidaten, Distribution, withdrawal of meme coins, please read: [3\. Multi-wallet management](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-connect-tg-multi-wallet-system#id-2.-duo-qian-bao-guan-li-1)

*   Phantom custodial accounts support new user referral across all chains, with independent referral data
    
*   ⚠️ Note: To trade with Phantom Wallet, use the “Trade with Wallet” option at the bottom. Data (Follow / Watchlist) from the two login methods are not shared, functioning as separate accounts

# Trailing Stop Loss | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-stop-loss#id-1.-zhui-zong-zhi-sun-de-yun-xing-yuan-li)

1\. **How Trailing Stop Loss Works:**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trailing stop is a more advanced function of stop loss setting. **The stop loss price will increase as the token price rises, aiming to reduce losses** . Suppose the token has experienced a surge, but the surge is not enough to trigger the take profit price you set. If the trailing stop is not turned on, the order will only be closed when the price drops to the stop loss price, and you will face a turn from profit to loss; but if the trailing stop is turned on, you may be in a profitable state when the stop loss order is closed.

**Example:** The user sets the take-profit ratio to +200% (i.e., a 3-fold increase), and the stop-loss ratio to -40%. After the order is opened, the maximum increase of the token is +190%, and then it starts to fall and never recovers:

*   Without a trailing stop, the order will not be automatically sold until the token drops to -40% again, which means that the user will miss out on gains and end up suffering losses instead.
    
*   If the trailing stop is turned on, the order will continuously adjust the stop loss price every time the token rises. When the token rises to the maximum value of +190%, the order will adjust the stop loss price from -40% to +74%. By adjusting the stop loss price, the token is given enough room for maneuver while ensuring profits when the token actually falls.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-stop-loss#kai-qi-zhui-zong-zhi-sun-hou-zhi-sun-jia-jiang-yu-zui-gao-jia-bao-chi-gu-ding-de-zhi-sun-bi-li)

After opening the trailing stop loss, the stop loss price will maintain a fixed stop loss ratio with the highest price:

> Stop loss price = Highest price \* (1 - drawdown percentage%) = 290% \* (1 - 40%) - 1 = 290% \* 0.6 -1 = 74%

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-stop-loss#id-2.-shi-yong-zhui-zong-zhi-sun-shi-qing-zhu-yi)

2\. Please note when using trailing stop loss:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The trailing stop will continuously adjust the stop price. **As long as the token price keeps rising, your stop price will rise accordingly** . Therefore, the trailing stop will only keep rising and cannot be lowered.
    
*   There is no activation price for trailing stop loss. When an order is created, the trailing stop loss will start immediately.
    
*   Trailing stop loss will not adjust your take profit price, so when you turn on trailing stop profit and trailing stop loss at the same time, and the drawdown percentage of the trailing stop profit you set is greater than the stop loss percentage, the stop loss price will be higher than the take profit price.
    
*   If both trailing take profit and stop loss are enabled at the same time, and the price reaches the take profit price, the order will be closed when the actual price decline reaches the smaller value between the take profit drawdown and the stop loss ratio.
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-stop-loss#zhui-zong-zhi-ying-yu-zhui-zong-zhi-sun-de-qu-bie-shen-me-shi-zhui-zong-zhi-ying-lian-jie-lian-guo-q)

3\. The difference between trailing take profit and trailing stop loss:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Click to view -** [**What is trailing take profit**](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-take-profit)

*   **Different applicable scenarios:**
    
    *   Trailing Take Profit: The goal is to maximize your profit as much as possible
        
    *   Trailing Stop: The goal is to minimize your losses
        
    
*   **Is there a trigger price?**
    
    *   Trailing Take Profit: Yes, the trigger price is the take profit price you set
        
    *   Trailing Stop: None
        
    

**Click to view -** [**How to enable trailing stop loss**](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-quick-buy-take-profit-stop-loss#how-to-enable-trailing-stop-loss)

[PreviousTrailing Take Profit](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-take-profit)
[NextAuto Buy: Auto Buy ＆ Limit buy](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-buy-auto-buy-limit-buy)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [1\. How Trailing Stop Loss Works:](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-stop-loss#id-1.-zhui-zong-zhi-sun-de-yun-xing-yuan-li)
    
*   [2\. Please note when using trailing stop loss:](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-stop-loss#id-2.-shi-yong-zhui-zong-zhi-sun-shi-qing-zhu-yi)
    
*   [3\. The difference between trailing take profit and trailing stop loss:](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/trailing-stop-loss#zhui-zong-zhi-ying-yu-zhui-zong-zhi-sun-de-qu-bie-shen-me-shi-zhui-zong-zhi-ying-lian-jie-lian-guo-q)

# GMGN Fees ＆ Settings | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#tips-you-can-get-details-of-various-transaction-fees-by-querying-the-transaction-hash-at-https-solsc)

✅Tips: You can get details of various transaction fees by querying the transaction hash at [https://solscan.io/](https://solscan.io/)



--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FwzU4K3zogvABiB0kvB0m%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55e8c03e-011a-4fec-adde-3c55209711f9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72df809d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#id-1.-gmgn-shou-xu-fei-wu-xu-she-zhi)

1\. GMGN Fee (no need to set)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

GMGN only charges a 1% handling fee for a single transcation, and there are no additional charges. For users who have questions about transaction fees, please first check your priority fee and slippage settings.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F8zelSgXd0HyCUhXWTVTm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc28385b6-1e8e-44b7-84ae-86b13fdb6515&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fcaf7377&sv=2)

The transaction amount in the figure is 1 SOL, and the GMGN fee is 0.01 SOL (WSOL is the token used for transactions on the Solana chain, 1 WSOL = 1 SOL)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#id-2.-gas-fei-wu-xu-she-zhi)

2\. Gas Fee (no need to set)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note: Gas Fee refers to the fee that users need to pay to network validators when executing transactions or interacting with smart contracts, which is commonly known as on-chain fees.

*   Solana chain uses SOL as the gas unit
    
*   The ETH chain uses Gwei as the Gas unit because the price of ETH is high and the fee calculation is inconvenient: 1 ETH = 1,000,000,000 Gwei (9 zeros)
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#id-3.-hua-dian-xu-yao-she-zhi)

3\. Slippage (need to be set)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Description: Slippage refers to the maximum acceptable deviation of the number of tokens declared for a single transaction. For example, if the slippage is 30% when buying, if the actual tokens received are between 70% and 100%, the on-chain transaction will be successful. If the actual tokens received are less than 70%, the on-chain transaction will fail (exceeding the slippage range).

2) The purpose of setting a slippage limit ratio is to ensure that you will not suffer unexpected losses due to slippage. Once the actual execution price exceeds the set slippage ratio, the transaction will be automatically cancelled.

3) When trading MEME, experienced traders will significantly increase slippage to cope with the sharp rise and fall caused by token FOMO and FUD sentiment, because the demand is to buy and sell quickly, and they don’t care how many tokens they can actually receive.

✅Tips: Manual buying and selling is recommended to be automatic; the recommended slippage for automatic buy/sell and other pending order operations is 30%-35%; for new and popular tokens, it is recommended to be 50% or more. Sometimes auto slippage has lag, can not guarantee 100% success, please be careful to follow your needs to trade

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FcvXWHbmXx8uJ2IMfB14P%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D247ed3cd-4478-43dd-9b95-6956accc9853&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6569a59a&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#id-4.-fang-jia-mo-shi-fang-mev-san-ming-zhi-gong-ji-xu-yao-xuan-ze-shi-fou-kai-qi)

4\. Anti-MEV mode (Anti-MEV sandwich attack) (need to choose whether to turn it on)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Note: The core attack method of the MEV bot is Sandwiching, which is the so-called sandwich attack, which is equivalent to the preemptive strategy adopted by high-frequency trading companies: in a typical sandwich attack, the MEV bot reads the incoming transaction information and preemptively executes the order, thereby pushing up the token price when you buy it.

*   _The MEV bot detects your transaction and automatically generates a buy transaction before the block is packaged your trading. The transaction fee is higher than yours, so the robot's transaction is executed first._
    
*   _After the bot's transaction is executed, due to the automatic market making mechanism, the unit price of the token will be raised, and the price increase will directly affect the subsequent transactions. Therefore, when it is your turn to trade, the token price has risen, and the actual number of tokens you get is not as much as when you first placed the order. This difference is also called the slippage amount. (But it is different from the normal slippage, which is the slippage caused by the MEV bot )_
    
*   _After our transaction is executed, the token price will continue to rise. At this time, the bot generates another transaction to sell the lower price bought in the previous transaction, just making a profit from the difference. The two transactions generated by the bot just sandwich our transaction, so we call it sandwich attack_
    

2) Enabling Anti-MEV mode can effectively prevent transactions from being sandwiched, but the priority fee must be at least 0.002 SOL to enable it.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FAD8T4V5F7jAEWOcAnJj2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85b9257d-7914-4ae7-a8d2-badb39d1ae80&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f7faa8dd&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#id-5.-you-xian-fei-xu-yao-she-zhi)

5\. Priority fee, Tip fee, Custom RPC (need to be set)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FdkwoayIWa37q4n4Ek6VJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dccf534a3-3aa6-492b-b0d8-197727337db3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c39cf03f&sv=2)

Priority/Tip fee: max 2 SOL

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#id-1-priority-and-tip-fee-description)

1) Priority and Tip fee description:

Priority and tip fees are additional fees paid to speed up transaction processing, used to bribe nodes to prioritize your tx, and are not collected by GMGN

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F3IHYaAkBX8HjGxTLfYkI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D384b1e09-d2cb-4b1b-a2c0-272c7d326a97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e02abfa6&sv=2)

✅ Transaction on-chain fee = Priority fee + Tip fee + Gas

*   Priority fee: Paid to validators to prioritized confirmation. (minimum 0.0001 SOL)
    
*   Tip fee: Paid to private nodes for faster processing. (minimum 0.0001 SOL)
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#id-2-anti-mev-rpc-submission)

2) Anti-MEV RPC Submission

*   **Off protection**: transactions sent to all nodes, very fast
    
*   **Reduced protection**: transactions sent to limited nodes, fast, may be front-run
    
*   **Secure protection**: transactions sent to safe nodes, slightly slower, with compensation
    

⚠️ Note: For anti-MEV protection, the minimum Tip fee is 0.0001 SOL (a higher value is recommended, as low fees may result in slower on-chain processing during busy network conditions)

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#id-3.-custom-rpc-you-can-choose-to-connect-to-a-specific-rpc-server-self-hosted-or-third-party-provided)

**3\. Custom RPC**: You can choose to connect to a specific RPC server (self-hosted or third-party provided)

*   **RPC Node**: Transaction submission - Sends transactions to the blockchain for validation and recording
    
*   Custom RPC will be used as a backup RPC for simultaneous on-chain submission
    
*   If a custom RPC is used for submission, both priority and tip fees will be charged at the same rate
    

✅ **Tips**: For transactions with no speed requirement, a total on-chain fee of 0.002 - 0.005 SOL is generally sufficient. For auto buy/sell limit order placement, a fee of 0.006 SOL or higher is recommended. During busy network conditions, manually increasing the priority/tip fee is advised for faster tx confirmation

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#id-6.-dai-bi-fa-xing-ping-tai-shou-xu-fei-wu-xu-she-zhi)

6\. Token issuance platform fee (no need to set)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note: For example, for tokens issued on Pump.Fun, a 1% handling fee will be charged by the Pump.Fun platform during transactions. For the specific handling fee ratio, please refer to the instructions of each token issuance platform.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FZ8AGisRTLqJ0FIx8sGEd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df580afa9-7e88-4a2b-b065-e03665b61f37&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=165378de&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-fees-settings#if-you-have-any-questions-you-can-ask-your-trading-questions-in-the-official-gmgn-group)

If you have any questions, you can ask your trading questions in the official GMGN group 👇🏻:

[![Logo](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftelegram.org%2Fimg%2Fapple-touch-icon.png&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c3e5dfa1&sv=2)💎GMGN Degen Group - OfficialTelegram](https://t.me/gmgnai)

[PreviousTransaction/Limit Order failure](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/transaction-limit-order-failure)

# Track Smart Money | GMGN Tutorial

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/track-smart-money#copy-trade-smart-money-to-earn)

_Copy Trade Smart Money to Earn_


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Follow smart money and key opinion leaders (KOLs), and track their trading activities in real time to discover new MEME tokens and trade quickly (please carefully check contract safety before copying trades).

**Steps:**

1.  Follow Smart Money:
    
    *   On the Ethereum chain: [https://gmgn.ai/discover?chain=eth](https://gmgn.ai/discover?chain=eth)
        
    *   On the Solana chain: [https://gmgn.ai/discover/?chain=sol](https://gmgn.ai/discover/?chain=sol)
        
    *   On the Blast chain: [https://gmgn.ai/discover?chain=blast](https://gmgn.ai/discover?chain=blast)
        
    
2.  Receive notifications in the bottom left corner to track what smart money is buying in real time.
    
3.  New activities will trigger a red bubble notification with a sound alert (sound toggle must be enabled).
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FtikTbGRf7Gfv4pw4fcXc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D474eb620-c3ad-4c36-9e4a-dceb8df36813&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3587b0cc&sv=2)

# Auto Trading: Migrated Snipe | GMGN Tutorial

Rule:

*   All SOL chain ungraduated tokens can set up Migrated Snipe
    
*   Only when you complete settings and click Buy xx SOL before the DEX has added official liquidity pool, your Migrated Snipe order will be triggered
    
*   One token can only create one Migrated Snipe task, and cannot be created after DEX adds official LP
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-migrated-snipe#id-1.-raydium-kai-pan-zi-dong-ju-ji-web-duan)

1\. Migrated Snipe - web version

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FPyD9CSUD0zwcDcyxJozI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92ae9d49-36c4-47a0-a307-aa0460d10cb9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=583b67bf&sv=2)

1) Create Migrated Snipe task:

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FVYlZouH54z61UiXDHFLE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5ef499c-a801-4edf-a2e7-c9bc61601688&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c3131d80&sv=2)

*   Click Auto trading on the token page, click Migrated Snipe and enter the editing page
    
*   Set Buy Amount, TP: take profit (Trailing Take Profit), SL: stop loss (Trailing Stop Loss)
    
*   Set slippage, priority fee, anti-MEV, and click save
    
*   After the settings are completed, click Buy in any token you want to snipe. The token will auto buy the amount of SOL you set when DEX adds official LP
    

2) View or delete your Migrated Snipe task:

*   In the token page - Orders, you can view your current Migrated Snipe tasks and could view or delete them
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FPZXZRpfjlzM834EsQUuW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De63747dc-abfc-465a-ba81-e977f71a5d70&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17faf729&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-migrated-snipe#id-2.-raydium-kai-pan-zi-dong-ju-ji-bot-duan)

2\. Migrated Snipe - bot vision


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Create Migrated Snipe task:

*   When you enter a ungraduated token contract address into the bot, you will see the Snipe Raydium option, and you can set the amount of SOL used to snipe the token separately
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FSyOsfrA9zYx9ocdl7cGG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb8913c1-7f86-4df0-9174-50e3037d7792&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fcfacd32&sv=2)

2) Adjust Migrated Snipe settings:

*   In the settings, you can click on Snipe Raydium xx SOL, enter the SOL amount you want to use for sniping in the reply box, and you can complete the change
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FqjDrZtCAcF7j5HoP0NDY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D40295472-30db-4f98-8e35-521c11222dcf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c20137b&sv=2)

3) View or delete your Migrated Snipe tasks:

*   Currently, the GMGN TG bot does not support viewing the Migrated Snipe tasks. Please go to the GMGN site Auto trading dashboard to view it

# Auto Buy: Auto Buy ＆ Limit buy | GMGN Tutorial

Supported Chains: Solana

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-buy-auto-buy-limit-buy#id-1.-send-contract-to-buy-automatically-with-telegram-bot)

1\. Send contract to buy automatically with Telegram Bot


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Send the contract address (or pump.fun token webpage link) to the GMGN Sniper Bot (Telegram Bot), and the Bot will immediately buy the specified amount of tokens without multiple clicks.

1) Add GMGN Telegram Sniper Bot as a friend: [https://t.me/GMGN\_sol\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)

2) Set the preset value of auto buy: send /start, click Settings - Auto buy to enter (or click /set from the lower-left menu of Bot to enter the Settings page)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fj8Mhd5Gnxw3Mrk0dDpKx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8cc449aa-dc9e-474a-8d0b-b2a1f29d9436&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4cae0c30&sv=2)

3) Click to turn on the auto buy, and then set the auto buy:

**Buy**: enter Auto Buy SOL amount for each transaction (now --) **Min Liq**: enter the minimum liquidity value to execute Auto Buy (now --). E.g. enter 1000, and the bot will Auto Buy only when the pool exceeds $1K. **Max MC**: enter the maximum token market cap to execute Auto Buy (now --). E.g. enter 250000, and the bot will Auto Buy only when the market cap is below $250K.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FFXUFacxsJCGanFzCdbJV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a46951b-e53c-49f2-a60f-c76e7bd3429c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90017d2d&sv=2)

4) 🎉 Successfully set!Send the token contract to bot, and the bot will auto buy at the preset purchase amount

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-buy-auto-buy-limit-buy#id-2.-limit-buy-order-with-gmgn-web)

2\. Limit Buy Order with GMGN web


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Open the GMGN Trending page [https://gmgn.ai/trend?chain=sol](https://gmgn.ai/trend?chain=sol)
 , click on the hot token you want to buy

2) In the right area of the token details page, click to Buy Dip, then click to bind TG bot wallet, it will automatically jump to GMGN sniper robot, click "Yes" to complete the binding

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FYuH9lBpfLHlQJy0HwEUs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0660e286-4a3b-4bcc-b43e-04a6390a86d7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c26aaef2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FlpebUPBk3nB4tCfq8YyZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daba4c99c-d426-4465-a45d-56f450596f4d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8af44992&sv=2)

3) Return to GMGN website after binding successfully

*   Click on the bound TG wallet
    
*   Click to Buy Dip
    
*   Complete purchase quantity, slippage, anti-mev Settings
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fgr7gKnfyRlB1084N5mV8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D530b7bec-4ded-48c8-957e-ceead1a175e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b063db14&sv=2)

3) 🎉 Click to create order buy, and successfully complete the Buy Dip limit order!

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-buy-auto-buy-limit-buy#id-3.-limit-buy-order-with-telegram-bot)

3\. Limit Buy Order with Telegram Bot


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Add GMGN Telegram Sniper Bot as a friend: [https://t.me/GMGN\_sol\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)

2) Enter /start in the GMGN Sniper Bot, click Buy/Sell and enter token CA

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FgEakWKDuJuBqCl8cZiqT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71aa5d4e-e65c-464e-b457-d13512e5af30&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2273739c&sv=2)

3) After entering the contract, the buy/sell interface will automatically pop up click the Limit. Then select the purchase SOL quantity button in the area, and also support custom purchase quantity (If you need to modify the preset purchase value, please click on the bot menu /set to set it)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FO2vSRxaOkMtPO3Avqi5D%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd275d80a-6a7f-48d6-b328-4fc14bf77bcd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=15e64e6&sv=2)

4) Set the trigger price (support input price, or positive or negative percentage), and check the validity period of the Limit Buy order (support 3 days /24 hours /1 hour)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FblDJQ985zlz0HOpciWNC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72e5bb0e-ac16-4142-a2ae-b99b90e11326&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a597a19&sv=2)

5) 🎉 Click to create order buy, and successfully complete the auto buy (Buy Dip) limit order!

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FipZ8S9eWiyYMU9MaxnKo%252FSnipaste_2024-08-18_03-52-31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a847b01-27f1-4767-86c8-954685b0fbbd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c21cb1f3&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F7lLgw2TSUTYHhXYhCKG0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc76fbe86-fe2a-467a-928a-0b3ee08ded2b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2173fd2&sv=2)

# Auto Trading: Dev Sell | GMGN Tutorial

Rule:

*   Unlimited tokens species. When the token creator sells part of holdings in a single transaction, it will be automatically sold.
    
*   Only when you have position, complete settings and click creater, it will automatically follow Dev to sell after Dev sells part of his holdings
    
*   A token only has one running Dev sell task and submits one transaction. But it can be submitted multiple times
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-dev-sell#id-1.-raydium-kai-pan-zi-dong-ju-ji-web-duan)

1\. Dev Sell - web version

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FNhG1CvKcGhmiKJ1lXs8B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27eebb3b-7518-4b6e-a1e8-b27c6ebb9b65&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab9affa0&sv=2)

1) Create Dev Sell task:

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FqKCof50c83YTXvV99vyK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a00e962-a4b8-45b0-b1d3-e7f4b815f20f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74bad77e&sv=2)

*   Click Auto trading on the token page, click Dev Sell and enter the editing page
    
*   Set Sell Holdings ratio and Dev Sell ratio
    
*   Set slippage, priority fee, anti-MEV, and click save
    
*   After the settings are completed, click create in any token you want to follow dev to sell. The token will auto sell the amount of holding ratio you set when Dev actual selling ratio ≥ Dev sell ratio you set
    

2) View or delete your Dev Sell task:

*   In the token details page - Position, you can view your current Dev Sell tasks and could view or delete them
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FnUwP8PQSeiG7VsF77wA8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7090e799-48b8-4b35-9003-2ccda4d66507&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8415435&sv=2)

3) When buying any token, if Dev Sell is also selected, it will automatically create a Dev Sell task

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FfRB7dGxymCicbwsDwFbq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f868b4e-0de5-483c-b859-3132a78002ec&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6573350&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-dev-sell#id-2.-raydium-kai-pan-zi-dong-ju-ji-bot-duan)

2\. Dev Sell- bot vision


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Create Dev Sell task:

*   When you enter a token contract address into the bot, you will see the Dev Sell option. Click it to create a follow-up Dev automatic sell task. When the token creator sells part of his holdings in a single transaction, the token ratio you set will be automatically sold
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FETkzyCc6hNmdJAGfpP5R%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e39613c-7f99-4e00-9b51-b7fc5a048f9b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f0afcc6&sv=2)

2) Adjust Dev Sell settings:

*   In the settings, after setting the Dev sell ratio, set the automatic Sell ratio. When the Dev sell ratio is greater than the ratio you set, your position will be automatically sold according to the automatic Sell ratio you set
    
*   In the settings, you can click the Dev Sell ratio and the Sell ratio, enter them in the reply box and send to complete the change
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F6tOdDKDCTbYD9HoDlX5W%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95787fe0-a15b-4e14-8f8e-fb85b0249416&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72bee51b&sv=2)

3) View or delete your Snipe Raydium tasks:

*   Currently, the GMGN TG bot does not support viewing the Dev Sell tasks. Please go to the GMGN site Auto trading dashboard to view it
    

[PreviousAuto Trading: Migrated Sell](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-migrated-sell)
[NextCopySignal: Copy Trade with PUMP CTO Signal](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/copysignal-copy-trade-with-pump-cto-signal)

# Auto Trading: Quick Buy ＆ Take-Profit / Stop-Loss | GMGN Tutorial

Supported Chain: Solana

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-quick-buy-take-profit-stop-loss#id-1.-automated-trading-gmgn-web-version)

**1\. Automated Trading - GMGN Web Version**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) **Experience Auto Trading by Logging in via Telegram**: In the trading section, select "Auto" and click "Connect Telegram" or the "Connect" button in the upper right corner. You will be automatically redirected to the GMGN login bot. Click "Log In", then click "Open" link to complete the TG login.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FN5w0nmSLzbF5LZ5bbU6q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9fbaa8ee-c938-4a5f-a02f-7231128e0ddd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae6e38f3&sv=2)

Open the GMGN login bot and click "Login" and "Open"

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fizg63opnK3OaXNWENTce%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D67a85281-f1b2-45a7-90de-be784781813d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f3af6aa5&sv=2)

2）**Set Auto Trading Parameters:** After successful login, Click "Set" to configure the parameters of your Auto Trading strategy.

*   Set the amount and take-profit or stop-loss values (at least one value must be filled in).
    
*   The settings for slippage, priority fee, MEV, remain consistent with the buy/sell settings. Changes made on the Auto Trading settings page will update the buy/sell values as well. Similarly, if the parameters for buy/sell are adjusted, automated trading will also place orders according to the modified values.
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FhqOM8xRYfLhDMG3OpifH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55f04d03-57ad-4b4c-aad0-3548d3eda7b2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eded3b8f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F2iMVVzoDtC3d6SxbLFRe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D934747bb-b201-4fc3-8202-d1a7e07e55e9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d1f3e9d&sv=2)

3) **Create and Run Auto Trading Orders:**

*   After saving the automated strategy parameters, click "Buy XXX SOL" on the trading page to create an automated trading order.
    
*   The created automated trading orders can be viewed in the "Strategy Order" list.
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FQMEagjqmYcRjZKhfo9Q2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f8d9f46-54a4-460a-bcd3-28c0d75b4a40&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe0560fa&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fu7p0Tf2xCTIoL1NuOLqB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6518752e-cf70-428e-a885-45fe5172969f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b49df47&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-quick-buy-take-profit-stop-loss#ru-he-kai-qi-zhui-zong-zhi-ying)

**2\. How to Enable Trailing Take Profit**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Open the trading panel, select \[Auto\], you need to set:

1.  Buy amount and take profit ratio;
    
2.  Enable Trailing Take Profit (once enabled, it will show the minimum profit: assuming the worst-case where the price immediately drops after hit the take-profit ratio);
    
3.  Set the drawback percentage (the order will close immediately when the percentage drop from the highest price exceeds the drawback percentage).
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FaFwZOaXb2cd88H5xh8zb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D578247d4-a0cd-4e43-9ec8-dcd7a28916c6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=effc3f49&sv=2)

After enabling Trailing Take Profit, Auto trading panel will change to **TTP**. When you click to buy XX SOL, the system will immediately buy the token and execute the order according to the parameters you set.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FjlgnYMOCE7Fo0ptnF7AM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91283ff7-429d-43b0-9657-baeec1483143&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dfa7f6a7&sv=2)

**Viewing Trailing Stop Orders**

You can view the order information in \[Auto Orders\] list.

*   When the Trailing Take Profit has not been triggered, the status is a **gray dot**. Hover will display: Trailing Take Profit is pending, and show the trigger price. Trigger price = buy price \* (1 + TP ratio%)
    
*   After TTP is triggered, the status changes to a **green dot**. Hover will display: Trailing Stop activated, and the highest price reached, and the current stop-profit price.
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FdPsHAq8IL3aK3aMiIW5J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2129d1e4-de5c-4968-8cc7-9fce2cd50e88&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab6d4354&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FXVwTJAVgMZginlLLcJUf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1af1818-1494-4f54-8d08-dd6eb70edd1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dce0381f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-trading-quick-buy-take-profit-stop-loss#how-to-enable-trailing-stop-loss)

**3\. How to Enable Trailing Stop Loss**

In the Auto trading settings page, set stop-loss ratio and then enable trailing stop-loss.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FJOg0xni3Buqa1BPqUe5F%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4744695-112d-43f4-9a06-d876440a88dd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b8ed96a&sv=2)

[PreviousCopySignal: Copy Trade with PUMP CTO Signal](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/copysignal-copy-trade-with-pump-cto-signal)
