# CA Security Checks | GMGN Tutorial

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/ca-security-checks#disclaimer-token-security-checks-are-for-reference-only-and-cannot-guarantee-100-accuracy.-please-ca)

**⚠️ Disclaimer: Token security checks are for reference only and cannot guarantee 100% accuracy. Please carefully compare multiple security tools before trading.**

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/ca-security-checks#solana-token-security-checks)

Solana token security checks


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FryJAWwqhZR4cjV7XIF76%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3aa2676-c956-482c-ba2b-9551a5b63236&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebbc6d13&sv=2)

*   **MintDisable:** "Yes" indicates safety, meaning that the token creator cannot issue additional tokens to manipulate the market.
    
*   **Top10 hold:** "Yes" indicates a relatively safe condition, meaning that the total holdings of the top 10 token holders are less than 30% of the total supply.
    
*   **Blacklist:** "No" indicates safety, meaning that the project cannot blacklist any wallet's transactions, reducing the risk of financial entrapment. “Yes”means:you are in this token dev‘s blacklist.you can't sell this token,it wil alert you that your wallet is frozen.
    
*   **Burnt:** Displaying the burn pool percentage: the higher the ratio, the better, with 100% indicating that the project cannot withdraw from the liquidity pool.
    
*   **Rug probability****:** Display the probability of this token being a rug pull by analyzing the holders. The more holders who frequently buy rug pull tokens, the higher the likelihood that this token could be a rug pull.
    
*   **Rug History****:** Display which rug pull tokens may have been previously launched by the creator of this token.
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/ca-security-checks#eth-token-security-checks)

ETH token security checks


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FrA7yaeUc2vjvuKl3C2AN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e59ad82-df11-43a9-b871-b88450e65181&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e4f9a58e&sv=2)

*   **Honeypot:** When "Yes," it indicates a honeypot, where the token creator uses technical measures to restrict the sale of tokens, leading to potential investment losses. Honeypot detection relies on third-party data sources such as Goplus, and the GMGN website may display this information with some delay, thus not guaranteeing timeliness or accuracy. Before trading, it is crucial to consult multiple token security audit tools to verify the token's safety.
    
*   **Verified:** The token's contract has been made open source on [Etherscan.io](http://etherscan.io/)
     , allowing for the source code to be reviewed.
    
*   **Renounced:** Contract permissions have been relinquished. However, be aware that some token contracts might fake "renouncement" and still update the code, transforming the token into a Honeypot, or blacklisting trader wallets to prohibit the buying, selling, or transferring of tokens.
    
*   **Locked/Burned:** Display the risk of liquidity pool withdrawal. The liquidity pool's LP tokens have either been locked (retrievable upon expiration) or burned (transferred to a burn address, making them irretrievable).
    
*   **Buy/Sell Tax:** Displays the transaction tax that needs to be additionally paid to the token creator during buying and selling. If the sell tax is excessively high (e.g., 99%), it indicates a Honeypot, making it impossible to sell, run away!

# 🤝🏻 Cooperation-API:🕹Integrate GMGN ETH/Base/BSC Trading API | GMGN Tutorial

✅ Approved: API Key sent to your email ❌ Rejected: No notification sent

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-api-integrate-gmgn-eth-base-bsc-trading-api#authentication)

Authentication

*   GMGN provides professional users with SOL/BSC/Base/ETH Trading API. Access is granted solely based on sufficient **Trading Volume** on GMGN. Review will be completed within 24 hours after submission
    
*   To access the GMGN Trade API, apply for permission by filling out the following Google Form: [https://forms.gle/CWABDLRe8twvygvy5](https://forms.gle/CWABDLRe8twvygvy5)
    
*   Upon approval, GMGN will issue an API Key to your email. Include the API Key in the request header with the name: `x-route-key`
    
*   Each API Key is rate-limited to one call every 5 seconds
    

**ETH/Base chain Swap transaction steps:**

1.  **Get the transaction route, recommended slippage, and recommended gas price at the same time**
    

*   Get transaction routing: [Get the available routing for ETH/Base transactions](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-api-integrate-gmgn-eth-base-bsc-trading-api/get-the-available-routing-for-eth-base-bsc-transactions)
    
*   Get recommended slippage: [Get the recommended slippage value of ETH/Base token](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-api-integrate-gmgn-eth-base-bsc-trading-api/get-the-recommended-slippage-value-of-eth-base-bsc-token)
    
*   Get recommended gas price: [Get the recommended gas price for ETH/Base chain](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-api-integrate-gmgn-eth-base-bsc-trading-api/get-the-recommended-gas-price-for-eth-base-bsc-chain)
    

1.  **After selecting the route, call the simulated transaction**
    

[💻Swap transaction simulation (ETH/Base)](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-api-integrate-gmgn-eth-base-bsc-trading-api/swap-transaction-simulation-eth-base-bsc)

1.  **After the simulated transaction is passed, get the returned data field and use normal rpc or anti-pinch rpc to submit the formal transaction**
    

Submit transaction signature, you can use ethers js library

Signature transaction tutorial [https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/providers/#Signer-signTransaction](https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/providers/#Signer-signTransaction)

Ethers js library [https://github.com/ethers-io/ethers.js](https://github.com/ethers-io/ethers.js)

# Insider Traders,Snipers,First 70 Buyers | GMGN Tutorial

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/insider-traders-snipers-first-70-buyers#disclaimer-the-holding-status-of-insider-traders-snipers-and-the-first-70-buyers-cannot-guarantee-re)

⚠️ Disclaimer: The holding status of insider traders, snipers, and the first 70 buyers cannot guarantee real-time accuracy and is provided for auxiliary reference only.

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/insider-traders-snipers-first-70-buyers#insider-trading-holder-ratio)

Insider Trading Holder Ratio


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FBR0XxwbSwZyuZIqOQvXj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3caa8b9-4c84-4653-a9aa-34b5568fde99&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1568fdcd&sv=2)

*   Insider Trading: Wallets that did not buy tokens after trading opened, but hold tokens, may indicate that the token creator's holdings were transferred to multiple wallets to secretly sell off. Typically, legitimate projects distribute these through airdrops to users, and it is necessary to check the official Twitter for any airdrop events.
    
*   Insider Trading Holder Ratio: The proportion of holdings by insider trading wallets to the total token supply, the higher the ratio, the more concerning it is.
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/insider-traders-snipers-first-70-buyers#snipers-first-70-buyers-top-10-holders)

Snipers, First 70 buyers, Top 10 Holders


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FahEZ7JsWpHPnAXF8aCTx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f0afd35-d443-42ad-b1d6-07b17739288b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2fbbda03&sv=2)

**Top 70 Buyer Wallets:** Wallets that were the first 70 to buy tokens after the opening of trading.

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/insider-traders-snipers-first-70-buyers#wallet-labels)

**Wallet Labels:**

*   **Snipers:** Buyers who purchased within the first few blocks after trading opened.
    
*   **Scammer Wallets:** Wallets that frequently buy rug pull tokens, suspected to be secondary accounts of the token creators involved in rug pull schemes.
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/insider-traders-snipers-first-70-buyers#explanation)

Explanation:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F45U20QMmTqU6hlZ6y9LH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D193ee83f-4198-4456-bc58-39d86a3ac1ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5411abc&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/insider-traders-snipers-first-70-buyers#holding-status-explanation)

**Holding Status Explanation:**

*   **Hold**: The number of tokens bought initially remains the same as the current holding.
    
*   **Buy More**: More tokens were bought after the initial buy.
    
*   **Sell Part**: Some tokens were sold after the initial buy, but there are still holdings left (on the Solana blockchain, it's temporarily impossible to distinguish between transferred and sold tokens).
    
*   **Sell All**: All tokens bought initially have been sold.
    
*   **Transferred**: No tokens were sold, but a portion was transferred, and there are still holdings remaining.
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/insider-traders-snipers-first-70-buyers#statistical-percentage-explanation)

**Statistical Percentage Explanation:**

*   **Total Bought**: The amount of tokens initially bought by the first 70 buyers divided by the total token supply.
    
*   **Current Total Holdings**: The actual amount of tokens currently held by the first 70 buyers divided by the total token supply.
    
*   **Top 10 Holders**: Wallets currently ranked in the top 10 by holding amount (excluding liquidity pool addresses, with a list that changes in real time); the amount of tokens these wallets currently hold divided by the total token supply.

# SnipeX | GMGN Tutorial

Try GMGN SnipeX Now 👇🏻

*   Web: [https://gmgn.ai/snipex?chain=sol](https://gmgn.ai/snipex?chain=sol)
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FjerA0Mo8VXxeawr2tT0j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b296968-70fc-4b20-ac9d-cb28d8573e81&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76f88ca7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/snipex#tui-te-gua-dao-shuo-ming)

SnipeX Instructions:

*   Monitor Twitter for new tweet, reply, updates proflie, repost. When a token contract is detected, automatically buy it with simple SnipeX parameter settings.
    
*   **SnipeX Task Limits**:
    
    *   Max concurrent tasks: 10
        
    *   Task lifetime: 7 days
        
    
*   **Supported Chain**: Solana only
    
*   **Access Requirement**: Telegram wallet users only
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/snipex#gua-dao-can-shu-she-zhi)

SnipeX **settings:**

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/snipex#id-1-twitter-account)

1) Twitter Account:

*   Enter the Twitter handle (without "@")
    
*   Duplicate Twitter handles are not allowed (for both paused and active SnipeX tasks)
    
*   The Twitter account must **exist** and **not have tweet protection enabled** to create a task
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/snipex#id-2-monitoring-types-select-at-least-1)

2) Monitoring Types (Select at least 1):

*   New Tweet
    
*   Reply
    
*   Update Profile
    
*   Repost
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/snipex#id-3-auto-buy-rules)

3) Auto-Buy Rules:

*   **Buy Not Graduated Pump tokens:** If the detected token is a Pump.fun token and not graduated, the bot will auto-buy after checking advanced settings
    
*   **Buy Graduated/Others Tokens:** If the detected token is a Pump.fun graduated token OR a non-Pump token, the bot will auto-buy after checking advanced settings
    
*   **Snipe If Immigrating:** If the token is a Pump.fun token that’s graduated but not yet migrated to raydium, the bot will bypass advanced checks and auto-snipe upon migration.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/snipex#id-4-sell-method)

4) Sell Method:

*   **No Sells:** Manual selling required.
    
*   **Custom TP/SL**: Take-Profit & Stop-Loss
    
    *   **Single**: Supports trailing stop-loss
        
    *   **TP&SL in batches:** Max 10 TP&SL conditions; Enter a negative value in the "TP%" field to set a stop-loss.
        
    

**5) Advanced Settings**

*   **Market Cap limit:** You can set the market cap limit when buying tokens
    
    *   For example, if you set the minimum market cap to 50,000, the purchase will only be executed when the token market cap is higher than 50,000 USD
        
    *   For example, if you set the maximum market cap to 100,000, the purchase will only be executed when the token market cap is less than 100,000 USD
        
    
*   **Liq Limit:** You can set the liquidity (pool) limit when buying tokens
    
    *   For example, if you set the minimum liquidity to 50,000, the purchase will only be executed when the token liquidity (pool) is higher than 50,000 USD
        
    *   For example, if you set the maximum liquidity to 100,000, the purchase will only be executed when the token liquidity (pool) is less than 100,000 USD
        
    
*   **Age limit:** You can limit the creation time of the token. Only buy tokens whose launch time falls within this specific interval
    
    *   For example, if you set the minimum token creation time to 10s, the purchase will only be executed if the token launch time is greater than 10 seconds
        
    *   For example, if you set the maximum token creation time to 1D, the purchase will only be executed if the token launch time is less than 1 day
        
    
*   **Min Burnt ratio:** You can set the minimum liquid burnt ratio limit
    
    *   For example, if you set 50%, the purchase will only be executed when the token burnt ratio is greater than or equal to 50%
        
    
*   **Skip Holdings**: Won't buy the holding tokens
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/snipex#id-6-set-snipex-trading-parameters-priority-fee-anti-mev-slippage)

6) Set SnipeX trading parameters : Priority fee, Anti-MEV, Slippage

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/snipex#id-1.-snipex-web)

1\. SnipeX - web


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) GMGN Home page, click the SnipeX

2) For the user who has obtained the SnipeX whitelist, click Create Task

3) SnipeX parameter setting:

5) SnipeX alerts

*   You’ll receive SnipeX alerts via [**@GMGN\_sol\_bot**](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)

**Left** column


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-1.-holding-watchlist-following-list)

**1\.** Holding/ Watchlist/ Following list

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FsvWRg0hxYnWFmP5aiqta%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b684d27-7d9f-4022-841a-2d5641223421&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b9901e1&sv=2)

*   Holding: Quickly understand the price changes of your collection of tokens
    
*   Watchlist: Quickly understand the price and profit changes of the tokens you hold, and you can sell them quickly at any time when watching the chart
    
*   Followed: Receive alerts on the wallets you have followed, and choose whether to enable sound notifications, so you can follow wallet to buy at any time when watching the chart
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-2.trending-pump)

**2\. Trending/ Pump list**

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FXGyI0auu2mn4E7lxb9am%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd824acfc-5283-4ab4-9a47-2a5fb37611c2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88f1ce3b&sv=2)

*   Trending: Filter out popular tokens that best suit your trading strategy by checking time, number of transactions, price, and price percentage
    
*   Pump: Filter out the Pump token that best suits your trading strategy by checking time, number of transactions, MKT Cap, and MKT Cap percentage
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#central-part)

Main interface - Chart:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-1.kxian-tu-biao-gong-neng)

1\. Chart function

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FROUaklhsfYxXDG6enoNn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0eac64e-1526-4a80-85c4-ffbc587bd7d4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=37832d81&sv=2)

Observe the price or MKT Cap trend of tokens on the chart, and use the abundant tools in the tool bar to help you trade better

Data:

*   Freely choose SOL/USD as the unit; freely choose to display the currency Price/MCap
    
*   Move the mouse on the chart to quickly browse the prices at different points, and click the + sign to draw a horizontal line
    

Settings:

*   Show/Hide trades: You can click on Show/Hide Trades icons above the chart, and flexibly choose to view the trading positions of different wallets in conjunction with the trading activities below
    
*   Right-click on a blank area of ​​the chart and check Hide marks on bars to choose whether to display the Dev trading icon.
    
*   Right click on the price/market value column on the right and click Move scales to left/right to freely choose to put the price column on the left or right
    
*   Click on fx indicators and select the chart indicator you use most often, for example, enter volume to add a volume indicator chart
    

Full screen chart:

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F2Bb9aKfEljZbqJrzIfzi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0d2c6fd-dbce-41e1-9878-0e3917c584bb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eea1c954&sv=2)

*   Click the full screen expansion button in the upper right corner of the chart to expand the chart in full screen
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-2.-cross-chain-multicharts)

2\. Cross-chain multicharts

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FFsLEwo4G6GhHhXeuIt5d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D125f2238-5406-4ed3-8724-cd42da90f8ec&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d4a222c2&sv=2)

GMGN supports cross-chain multicharts and separate transactions. Click Multicharts above the chart and enter CA to open it. It supports browsing up to 8 charts at the same time!

*   Marks, Avg price lines, and limit order lines on each chart are displayed normally
    
*   Each individual chart can choose its own time granularity
    
*   You can switch back and forth between different charts. The top information, activity, and transaction modules all display the tokens of the currently selected chart.
    
*   When switching coins from the list in the left column of the token details page, other added charts will not be cleared, only the currently selected chart will be replaced
    
*   After you switch chain and open the token details page, the previously added multicharts will not be cleared, only the last selected chart will be replaced, realizing the cross-chain multichart mode
    

Frequently Asked Questions:

*   How to add a chart of another chain when I'm in the sol chain token? Answer: Please open the multicharts mode first, select the chart that you want to be replaced, then switch the chain in the upper right corner, and then enter the token details page you want to add in to complete the addition of the crosschain multicharts.
    
*   After adding multicharts, a single chart becomes smaller and the display range is not enough. What should I do? Answer: 1) Drag the separator between the bottom of the chart and the active to expand the chart display range 2) Flexibly select the time granularity of a single ghostwriter and use the mouse wheel to adjust the chart display range 3) Collapse the left column to expand the display range of the main interface 4) Use the full-screen expansion mode in the upper right corner
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-2.-yi-jian-mai-mai)

3\. Instant trade/ Sell inits

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FFKaUi4jQ10qOrJfDq1WE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6018663d-3069-484b-90cb-8124faf9ec20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=29be1a06&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-1-instant-trade-below-the-chart-you-can-choose-whether-to-open-the-instant-trade-function-the-tradin)

1) Instant trade: Below the chart, you can choose whether to open the instant trade function, the trading window is freely draggable

*   Click the settings button next to “Instant trade” in the top left to customize your trading parameters
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-2-sell-inits-this-feature-helps-you-quickly-sell-tokens-to-recover-your-initial-cost)

2) Sell inits: This feature helps you quickly sell tokens to recover your initial cost

*   Available Conditions
    
    *   Available: You have holdings, and total buy cost exceeds total sell proceeds
        
    *   Unavailable: Total buy cost is less than or equal to total sell proceeds (you’ve recovered cost or made a profit)
        
    
*   How It Works
    
    *   Recover initial cost amount = Total buy cost - Tota realized proceeds
        
    
*   Applicable Scenarios
    
    *   Multiple Purchases: All buy costs are summed up
        
    *   Previous Sales: Deduct sell proceeds to calculate the remaining recover initial cost amount
        
    *   Price Drop or Token Transfer: If the holding value is below the initial cost, click "sell init" to sell all tokens
        
    *   Excludes transferred-in tokens; only considers buy and sell transactions
        
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-2.transactions-bottom-part)

Main interface - Trading activities

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FiLor7FPPcRtsToFgZclr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47aa94d1-c513-45a4-91b8-88e13a63abfd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=618de0d0&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-1.-jiao-yi-huo-dong-li-shi)

1\. Trading activity history

*   Supports the display of transaction activity records in seconds, helping you to keep abreast of the latest developments in token transactions
    
*   In the top right corner, you can see the bubble maps button, which will take you directly to their website to see the correlation between token holding addresses!
    
    ![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FS2UtQsu88koZIUYUd1Cr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5f5f3ce-9929-4f92-b500-77bf644b5fae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58026d5a&sv=1)
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-2.-huo-dong)

2\. Activity

*   You will get the latest transaction information, updated in real time. Transactions are also classified by _smart money, KOL/VC, whales, new wallets, snipers, large holders, developers, followed, and rat warehouses._
    
*   Click on different wallet types to quickly view what each wallet has done, and the transaction position and transaction time icons will be displayed on the K-line (select a new wallet as shown in the figure, and the transaction icons of new wallets will appear on the chart)
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F85V7AZ82JE1MGm2JIktQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D306343eb-0387-4555-b4db-582b14f8fe8e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f1f2fc41&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#right-column)

3\. Traders

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fkuro0aFjiC1ICzEGTIKd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c131479-fd1f-46bf-8183-0611ef5be9d0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2908a51&sv=2)

*   You will get all the historical trader information of the token. Transactions are also categorized by _smart money, KOL/VC, new wallet, followed, mouse trading, Bot Degan_
    

SOL Bal/Age

Current SOL balance of the wallet address/first activity time of the wallet

Source/TF time

The source of the account funds and the time of the transfer

Bought/Sold

The total buy/sell amount of this wallet address

Pnl

Total profit = realized profit + unrealized profit. Click SOL/USD to switch the display units of total buy/total sell/total profit/realized profit/unrealized profit.

Realized

The realized profit after selling the tokens by this wallet

Unrealized

The wallet still holds unrealized profits from not selling the tokens

Avg Cost/sold

Average buying price/average selling price

TXs

Green is the number of buys/red is the number of sells

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-4.-chi-you-zhe)

4\. Holders

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Flv6wi4afsy3chgF6swlR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcacefd24-0699-47f2-aaa0-6067a63b67a6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=510752d&sv=1)

*   Mark suspected insider trading to determine whether the dealer wants to use these small wallets to disperse the tokens and try to crash the market and run away
    
*   Mark suspected phishing wallets. If the transferred tokens are not purchased, they will be marked.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-5.-lan-chou-chi-you-zhe)

5\. BC Owners

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FhHXLTlLlQHE99oUheEl7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ee62b1b-84d5-4cdc-b7eb-e840d57589a3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2ce6694&sv=2)

*   Blue-chip tokens: Blue-chip tokens refer to tokens on various chains that have been verified and recognized by the market, have high value, and will not easily return to zero, such as Sol Chain Neiro, Popcat
    
*   Blue chip holders: holders of certain blue chip tokens
    
*   Blue Chip Index: The Blue Chip Index refers to the proportion of token holders who also own blue chip tokens.
    
*   The meaning of blue chip index: In a token, the more holders of blue chip tokens, the higher the blue chip index, the more blue chip holders are optimistic about the coin, and the more likely the coin will become the next high-value blue chip token.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#id-6.-wo-de-jiao-yi-gua-dan-ce-le)

*   For details, please see the Positions page tutorial:

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/token-page-chart-multicharts-activity-trading-system#you-lie)

Right column

####

# Auto Sell: Auto sell ＆ Take-profit/Stop-loss | GMGN Tutorial

Multiple TP/SL

*   [GMGN Web](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#ru-he-kai-qi-zhui-zong-zhi-ying-1)
    
*   [Telagrem Bot](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#telagrem-bot)
    

Limit Sell Order

*   [Fixed Amount Limit Order - GMGN Web](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#fixed-amount-limit-order-gmgn-web)
    
*   [Holdings Percentage Limit Order - GMGN Web](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#holdings-percentage-limit-order-gmgn-web)
    
*   [Fixed Amount Limit Order - Telegram Bot](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#fixed-amount-limit-order-telegram-bot)
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#ru-he-kai-qi-zhui-zong-zhi-ying)

1\. Multiple **TP/SL**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#ru-he-kai-qi-zhui-zong-zhi-ying-1)

**GMGN Web**

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F5AREv3fqGBjUyZCLYYXx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd02df117-f049-440b-a349-41ce6b29fe0a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dbd09a9f&sv=2)

GMGN supports presetting multiple take-profit, stop-loss limit orders when buying by GMGN TG wallet

*   Take Profit: Automatically triggers a sell when the price reaches the take-profit price. Take-profit price = current price + current price \* take-profit percentage
    
*   Stop Loss: Automatically triggers a sell when the price falls to the stop-loss price. Stop-loss price = current price - current price \* stop- loss percentage
    

1) Check the option next to the Advanced Trading Strategy button to choose whether to turn on

2) Click \[+add\] button to start adding TP/SL limit orders

3) Click the trash-can button on the right to delete the preset rule; click Add below to add a new preset rule

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#telagrem-bot)

Telagrem Bot

1) Add GMGN TG sniper bot to complete auto sell Settings: [https://t.me/GMGN\_sol\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)

2) Set autosell preset values:

*   Send /start, click Setting - Auto sell to enter (Or click /set from the lower left corner menu of Bot to enter the Settings page)
    
*   Or send /autosell to enter quickly
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FZlCgbWaXtPgHSUa9UFbO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81ab2491-5df3-470b-9c20-20d0d32ac1e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14b7b3a0&sv=2)

3) Click to turn on the auto sell, and then set the auto sell:

Click \+ Add Preset Order

**Set Stop-Loss Order with a** **negative** **percentage price change** (E.g. -50%). Set the sell amount percentage of bought amount (≤100%)

**Set Take-Profit Order with a** **positive** **percentage price change** (E.g. 50%). The total T/P sell amount percentage should add up to 100%

**Slippage**: Set slippage for Auto Sell orders

**Anti-MEV**: Will be enabled if Anti-MEV is selected in Swap dashboard. Tap /set to edit Anti-MEV slippage

⚠️ Note: Green 🟢 indicates that Auto Sell has been successfully enable

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FzMQ2N3RwsnkuOnx47kr7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D571dc4e2-f70b-4ef2-89ed-62950ac7ee14&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73839e5b&sv=2)

4) 🎉Bot can automatically create take profit/stop loss limit sell orders with a validity period of 24 hours now.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FyNNDNIswpcQFfA2LuH0v%252FSnipaste_2024-08-18_03-49-02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34daa6fd-82e0-434f-bd59-6baeecf67855&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=333ae0c6&sv=2)

[⚠️ Auto sell attention items](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#auto-sell-attention-items-1)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#id-2.-limit-sell-order)

2\. Limit Sell Order


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#fixed-amount-limit-order-gmgn-web)

Fixed Amount Limit Order - GMGN Web

Fixed Amount Limit Order: Sell a fixed amount of tokens based on current holdings

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FSAcKrh3BVfaqTbU3bYLV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1026ed54-b6f6-4bf4-8ca1-7eb40f6db994&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b2c3a091&sv=2)

1）Click "Sell," select "Limit," choose Amount

2）Set sell amount, slippage, Anti - MEV settings.

*   When creating a limit order, the candle chart displays your order price line, which can be dragged by clicking the leftmost box to your desired sell price
    

3) 🎉 Click to create order, and successfully complete the fixed amount limit sell order!

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#holdings-percentage-limit-order-gmgn-web)

Holdings Percentage Limit Order - GMGN Web

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FdMxNZ7SJ5Ng0iDD66LZX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dadc1ec0e-8972-4ea6-90e5-b9a0a4077cc4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a74aae71&sv=2)

Holdings Percentage Limit Order: Sells a percentage of holdings when triggered, no need for multiple limit orders after adding positions

1）Click "Sell," select "Limit," choose Percentage

2）Set sell percentage slippage, Anti - MEV settings

*   When creating a limit order, the candle chart displays your order price line, which can be dragged by clicking the leftmost box to your desired sell price
    

3) 🎉 Click to create order, and successfully complete the holdings percentage limit sell order!

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#fixed-amount-limit-order-telegram-bot)

Fixed Amount Limit Order - Telegram Bot


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1) Add GMGN Telegram Sniper Bot as a friend: [https://t.me/GMGN\_sol\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)

2) Enter /start in the GMGN Sniper Bot, click Buy/Sell and enter token CA

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FMyn96rSPZL6ZnFG6uomx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf9ed262-4b8d-44ce-b9b5-4ab2bb469fdf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cc8d4097&sv=2)

3) After entering the contract, the buy/sell interface will automatically pop up. Click on Limit, click on Limit Sell, select the percentage of the number you want to sell, and also support custom sell quantity

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fx4AIFavjwMR5JdQDHS3H%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf24e065-9d8d-4481-986f-ae0b32c2f71b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ce7bc47f&sv=2)

4) Set the trigger price (support input price, or positive or negative percentage), and check the validity period of the Limit Sell order (support 3 days /24 hours /1 hour)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FQrIqHv712OQLQAlGNon6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e6934c9-383f-44e2-a133-d45d9cd43bc9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c6826936&sv=2)

5) 🎉 Click to create order, and successfully complete the auto sell (take profit/stop loss) limit order!

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FRDcemgww1FqiAvijBAkJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b6104ba-b29f-4269-b5fa-e40b7aeb90d1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b2ac50fb&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F3OE3cnywMo5be9Us3b4y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b34738a-3b30-4575-b728-01acafc77a24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=837c5f3e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#auto-sell-attention-items)

⚠️ Auto sell attention items:

Auto sell is calculated separately for each purchase, please note that it is not calculated according to the current total position. If there are multiple purchases, be sure to manually close the auto sell order of the previous purchase to avoid triggering take profit /stop loss. If it is not turned off, then each purchase will trigger the sell limit order you set several times, which may produce the following situations.

1\. Buy a single order and sell multiple preset orders with auto sell:

*   Suppose you want to sell 75% of a single purchase in batches: A certain purchase (buy 200 tokens), want to sell 50% at 50% rise (i.e. 200 x _50%=100 tokens); Then continue to increase by 50% (cumulative increase of 100%) and sell 25% of the purchase at that time (i.e. 200 x_ 25%=50); A single purchase of the last 50 remaining, twice sold 100+50 a total of 150; At the same time, set a stop loss of 30% to clear the single purchase of tokens; You should enter it like this：
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FuyX1NbeKoW89h70ENoDw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0bb0484f-1eb1-4462-808f-084ef51b84d2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9102c903&sv=2)

2\. Multiple purchases, auto sell of a single preset order to sell:

*   Suppose you buy two trades and execute the default preset order (100% stop profit) at the same time, and the prices are $1 and $1.2 respectively; Then these orders will be sold when the token price is $2 and $2.4 respectively; Then calculate your total profit based on the amount of your two separate purchases Estimating gains and losses is difficult, it is not recommended to try, it is best to manually turn off the last auto sell Settings.
    

3.Multiple purchases, auto sale of multiple preset orders to sell:

*   Suppose you have more than one buy, and set a number of preset orders. The auto sell order corresponding to each purchase will be gradually sold in batches according to the set of multiple take profit/stop loss conditions. Estimating gains and losses is difficult, it is not recommended to try, it is best to manually turn off the last automatic selling Settings.

2\. Grant Admin Permissions To The Bot


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F6S5mpdLRR13v16O7uTam%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b93def2-2dcc-4cd4-98d9-72e1a65e36d3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba680fc2&sv=2)

3\. Send /SET Command To Add Tracking Wallet


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Send /set command in the group, click “+ Track Wallet”, then send wallet address to track.

Measage Format: \[wallet\] \[label\]

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FkLK9SV6KfQ6NPiVitbJF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73cfaa10-a13b-4064-a6d4-252544633c4a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7fcfdbe5&sv=2)

# TG Wallet: Import ＆ Export private key, Deposit, Withdraw | GMGN Tutorial

*   [Export Private Key](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#export-private-key)
    
*   [Import Private key](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#dao-ru-si-yao)
    

1.  [TG wallet deposit - web](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-1.-tg-wallet-deposite-web)
    
2.  [TG wallet deposit - bot](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-2.-tg-wallet-deposit-bot)
    
3.  [TG wallet withdrawal](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-3.-tg-wallet-withdrawal)
    
4.  [Security- Google Authenticator](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-4.-security-google-authenticator)
    
5.  [Deposit USDT/USDC to GMGN wallet, withdraw meme coin, Reclaim Token Rent](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-5.-deposit-usdt-usdc-to-the-tg-wallet-withdraw-meme-coin-recover-token-rent)
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#export-private-key)

Export private key:


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

⚠️The first time you use the GMGN TG bots, it will automatically generate the SOL chain, EVM chain (ETH/Base/BSC chains share the same address, only the network is different), and Tron chain wallet addresses

*   For the safety of user wallet funds, GMGN all chains ( SOL chain / EVM chain / Tron chain ) are prohibited from exporting private keys; Wallets imported from outside also can‘t export private keys
    
*   Please note that when you import the private key to any EVM chain bot, the wallet address of the GMGN ETH, Base, BSC chain bots will be changed at the same time. Please pay attention to whether the wallet address has assets in other networks
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#dao-ru-si-yao)

Import private key:


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fv5aHeQBcLA7ewtu0Wb6a%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd88a9e12-9926-46b5-8a42-b40737ba454d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86c2f4b2&sv=2)

*   Please enter /start in bot, click wallet, click Add New Wallet/Change Private Key, click import private key, and enter the private key in the reply box (Tron bot doesn't support import peivate key currently)
    
    *   SOL bot: [@GMGN\_sol\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)
         , the transaction network for deposit: Solana
        
    *   ETH bot: [@GMGN\_swap\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_swap_bot)
         , the transaction network for deposit: Ethereum
        
    *   Base bot: [@GMGN\_base\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_base_bot)
         , the transaction network for deposit: Base
        
    *   Bsc bot: [@GMGN\_bsc\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_bsc_bot)
         , the transaction network for deposit: BNB smart chain
        
    *   Tron bot: [@GMGN\_tron\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_tron_bot)
         , the transaction network for deposit: Tron (TRC20) (Tron bot doesn't support import wallet now)
        
    
*   When you import a new wallet address to SOL chain bot, it will jump to the GMGN web multi-wallet management page and will not delete the old wallet address. Read more information about multi-wallet system, please click: [🔄 TG Wallet: Connect TG, Multi-Wallet system](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-connect-tg-multi-wallet-system)
    
*   When you import a new wallet address to EVM chain bots, the old wallet address will be automatically deleted. There is no way to help you recover your assets!
    
*   ⚠️Please ensure the private key is safe and no dangerous program accesses your clipboard. Suggest not to copy the entire private key, but to copy and enter part of it manually
    

GMGN TG wallet does not support exchanging stablecoins such as USDT/USDC to SOL/ETH. If you deposit USDT/USDC by mistake, please check: [5.](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-5.-deposit-usdt-usdc-to-the-tg-wallet)
 [Deposit USDT/USDC to TG wallet, withdraw meme coin, recover token ren](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-5.-deposit-usdt-usdc-to-the-tg-wallet-withdraw-meme-coin-recover-token-rent)
[t](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-5.-deposit-usdt-usdc-to-the-tg-wallet)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-1.-tg-wallet-deposite-web)

1\. TG wallet deposite - web


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FttYmKSYhShiJRMm0qwh8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02897b51-9eb8-4100-9056-28674ab627c9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=be0cb50c&sv=2)

*   After connecting to the TG wallet on the GMGN official website, click Transfer Funds in the upper right corner
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FL87uiGiJMtUt5EdDpJ1p%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2e204c5-88f8-4532-8e80-a8c2491a0183&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fbb7a3c1&sv=2)

*   When the web3 plug-in wallet is not connected: Use the web3 wallet APP on a mobile phone or other mobile device to scan the code to deposit SOL/ETH; or copy the wallet address below the QR code and transfer SOL/ETH directly to the TG wallet
    
*   When connected to the web3 plug-in wallet: Enter the number of tokens you want to deposit to the TG wallet in the input box, then click Deposit
    
*   Please make sure that the transfer network is correct. If you deposit via the wrong network, there is no way to retrieve it!
    
    *   The transfer network for SOL chain is: Solana, please deposit SOL
        
    *   The transfer network for ETH chain is: Ethereum, please deposit ETH
        
    *   The transfer network for Base chain is: Base, please deposit ETH
        
    *   The transfer network for Bsc chain is: BNB smart chain, please deposit BNB
        
    *   The transfer network for Tron chain is: Tron (TRC20), please deposit TRX
        
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-2.-tg-wallet-deposit-bot)

2\. TG wallet deposit - bot


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FrtS5htnglyFxW5SZdniM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D611a011c-6267-4189-b850-507d4b790891&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14294e64&sv=2)

*   Enter /wallet in the bot or click on the wallet to enter the wallet page to see your TG wallet address
    
    *   SOL bot: [@GMGN\_sol\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)
         . The transfer network for is: Solana, please deposit SOL
        
    *   ETH bot: [@GMGN\_swap\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_swap_bot)
         . The transfer network is: Ethereum, please deposit ETH
        
    *   Base bot: [@GMGN\_base\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_base_bot)
         . The transfer network is: Base, please deposit ETH
        
    *   Bsc bot: [@GMGN\_bsc\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_bsc_bot)
         . The transfer network is: BNB smart chain, please deposit BNB
        
    *   Tron bot: [@GMGN\_tron\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_tron_bot)
         . The transfer network is: Tron (TRC20), please deposit TRX
        
    
*   After clicking ‘Tap to copy’ to copy the wallet address, perform transfer and deposit operations in your other web3 wallets
    
*   ⚠️ Please ensure the transfer network is correct
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-3.-tg-wallet-withdrawal)

3\. TG wallet withdrawal


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   For the security of user funds, the GMGN Telegram Bot doesn't support direct withdrawal operations. The token withdrawal feature has been fully migrated to the GMGN Website.
    
    Bot users, please follow these steps to withdraw: [2) Withdrawal steps](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-2-withdrawal-steps)
    
*   Please complete the account security verification process before withdrawal. Withdrawals locked until security setup is complete: [4\. Security- Google Authenticator](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-4.-security-google-authenticator)
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-1-set-the-extraction-whitelist-address)

1) Set the extraction whitelist address:

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FovZu8iGXfSkr3AFRox5t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec0d7dd2-9cb0-4b7a-bee8-f99d672d3e2c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f06b8a4a&sv=2)

*   After completing the account security binding, please complete the whitelist address setting in the upper right corner of the \[Deposit/Withdrawal\] page. Transfers are limited to whitelisted addresses, after which transfers bypass 2FA for safer, quicker withdrawals
    
*   No withdrawals allowed until 3 hours after:
    
    *   First-time whitelist setup
        
    *   Whitelist address change
        
    
*   24-hour withdrawal hold after Google Authenticator re-binding
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-2-withdrawal-steps)

2) withdrawal steps:

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FJx01bdGB6MYziKsjYQXC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55af5806-a10a-4154-8496-d6516fbb5c42&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=459e36b&sv=2)

*   For the safety of your funds, GMGN TG bot cannot directly perform withdrawal operations. Click \[Withdraw\] in the bot to jump to the GMGN site. Click \[Deposit/Withdraw\] in the upper right corner to enter the withdrawal page. You can withdraw after setting the withdrawal whitelist wallet
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F92n3mjlhtGJveukbrvQE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9599ce2-40d9-4384-979e-0000edd1361a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7d291d09&sv=2)

*   Enter the \[Deposit/Withdraw\] page from the upper right corner of the SOL chain, and the current main wallet will be deposited/withdrawn by default
    
*   If you need to deposit/withdraw other wallets, please go to the multi-wallet manager page to deposit/withdraw
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-3-maximum-withdrawal-amount-notice)

3) Maximum Withdrawal Amount Notice:

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FzT6qVC19SX07HcMtVwq1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde256630-31be-4e63-b2dd-a2bcf363d306&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86366fbf&sv=2)

*   ⚠️ Each on-chain wallet must maintain a minimum balance to preserve data storage and cover transfer gas fees. Therefore, clicking "Max" will not transfer the entire balance
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FVedSJiN7XnTpSrQP6JMR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db23241c1-22f5-4c25-8bb6-08d22475db08&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c9e110e9&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-4.-security-google-authenticator)

4\. Security- Google Authenticator


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fr2sHQI31pwbdXz90k5QQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8323e997-c040-4ff8-8d0d-c3193a8ddc7f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea178359&sv=2)

*   Google Authenticator: a TOTP/HOTP-based 2FA solution, It is primarily used to enhance the security of your GMGN account and protect your assets. After binding, you will be able to perform withdrawal transfers to whitelisted addresses
    
*   To bind Google Authenticator, go to "Security" in the upper right corner of the GMGN site
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FW7eLaCo8tU3tUMmk17Cq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D729dacb1-bd78-48e7-93c9-9573c8d7b26a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d02680ce&sv=2)

*   After you have installed Google Authenticator, suggest click the avatar in the upper right corner, choose "Use Authenticator without an account" to turn off the cloud synchronization function. Turning off cloud synchronization has the following benefits:
    
    *   **Avoid centralization risks** : If the verification code is synchronized to the cloud through the Google account, once a hacker breaks into your Google account (such as through phishing or password leakage), they can obtain **all 2FA verification codes** , making the two-factor authentication invalid
        
    *   **Full control over 2FA** : Turning off cloud sync means that users have full control over their 2FA keys and do not need to trust a third party to store them
        
    *   **Avoid accidental overwriting** : When logging into a Google account on multiple devices, automatic synchronization may cause the authenticator data to be accidentally overwritten or lost
        
    
*   Use Google Authenticator to scan the QR code to add the GMGN 2FA verification code, and fill in the generated verification code in the specified location
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FwNk7AWdIak1fLiptWn5T%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D564726df-43ef-45ed-a394-00e33a826841&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6eb313ad&sv=2)

*   Now you have successfully completed the Google Authenticator binding and can start binding the whitelist address for withdrawal
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-5.-deposit-usdt-usdc-to-the-gmgn-wallet-withdraw-meme-coin-reclaim-token-rent)

5\. Deposit USDT/USDC to the GMGN wallet, withdraw meme coin, Reclaim Token Rent


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-1-deposited-usdt-usdc)

1) Deposited USDT/USDC

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FyvxkQKL0qUhovjhexD2J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17d6380a-5f1f-46be-9f6d-ae19755a75bf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=838df347&sv=2)

*   USDT: On SOL, ETH, Base, or BSC chains, you can directly swap USDT for SOL, ETH, BNB Search for USDT on GMGN, find the corresponding CA for each chain, and sell your holdings (ensure your wallet has enough balance for gas fees)
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FAGRt5E1Kh0kzDSfdNuS8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88e73878-0075-46bf-8517-caa465c94758&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2e4924b2&sv=2)

*   USDC: On SOL, ETH, Base, or BSC chains, you can directly swap USDC for SOL, ETH, BNB Search for USDC on GMGN, find the corresponding CA for each chain, and sell your holdings (ensure your wallet has enough balance for gas fees)
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-2-ti-qu-meme-bi)

2) Withdraw meme coins

*   For withdrawal of meme coins, please check: [4) Deposit, Withdrawal, Consolidaten, Distribution](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-connect-tg-multi-wallet-system#id-4-deposit-withdrawal-consolidaten-distribution)
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/tg-wallet-import-export-private-key-deposit-withdraw#id-3-reclaim-token-rent-sol-incinerator)

3) Reclaim token rent (SOL Incinerator)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FCYPVB4Kgqtwa0OG0tK8U%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7d2d254-a98f-42f5-b862-6b39311fdd1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2034a4b3&sv=2)

*   Tokens with a total holding value under $10 can be closed on the asset page to reclaim rent
    
    *   If you can't find the Reclaim Rent button, it may be because: you hold no tokens, and GMGN automatically reclaim rent upon clearing, no manual action needed
        
    *   For tokens cleared before the Reclaim Rent feature was launched, approximately 0.002 SOL in account rent was automatically refunded upon sell-off. You can verify this via historical sold off tx hashes

1.Initial information


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note: the first time you use the bot, a solana wallet address is automatically generated

Buy/Sell

Pump FOMO

Click to see the tokens whose prices have surged in the last minute

New LP

Featured Signals

Track SM Wallet

Invitation Rebate

View other details such as the number of invitees and rebate income

set up

You can set to enable automatic slippage/fast slippage, and you can customize fast slippage and anti-slippage; Modify your buy priority fee/sell priority fee; Support auto buy, you can customize the automatic buying strategy, for more details, please see: [Send contract to buy automatically with Telegram Bot](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-buy-auto-buy-limit-buy#id-1.-send-contract-to-buy-automatically-with-telegram-bot)
 Support auto sell, you can create an automatic selling strategy based on the buy transaction, for more details, please see: [Set up Auto Sell ＆ Take-profit/Stop-loss with Telagrem Bot](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss#id-1.-set-up-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss-with-telagrem-bot)
 Support custom buy/sell quantity, convenient and fast buying and selling

2\. Wallet


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Due to the SOL chain mechanism problem, you may receive WSOL instead of SOL at transaction settlement. GMGN has now launched the exchange WSOL → SOL function, welcome to experience. Specific steps: Enter /start in our bot @GMGN\_sol\_bot, click the wallet, click Exchange WSOL → SOL to quickly exchange the received WSOL to SOL
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-tg-sniper-bot-sol#id-3.set-up-the-bot)

3.Set up the bot


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FNoK0jIuufWHBYrv4zEDI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f151209-f5fb-4457-a0bb-cc887f0c2360&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28bb6369&sv=2)

we must go to **Setting** in the home and start the basic setup

autoslippage

will allow us to have an automatic slippage enabled or disabled. The idea is that, depending on price fluctuation, our slippage will change automatically. We can also configure it manually by disabling this option

**turbo slippage**

slippage that you will have configured

**anti-mev slippage**

it is the slippage used when you are attacked by a mev bot

**auto buy**

turn on auto buy, send the token contract to the Bot, and it will automatically buy immediately after reaching the preset value

**auto Sell**

bot can help you automatically create a profit/stop limit order valid for 24 hours

**custom buy/custom sell**

we will be able to configure the quantities we want to get out at the time of buying and selling

For details about auto buy/auto sell/limit order, please click [Auto Buy: Auto buy＆Limit buy](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-buy-auto-buy-limit-buy)
 [Auto Sell: auto sell＆take profit / stop loss](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/auto-sell-auto-sell-take-profit-stop-loss)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-tg-sniper-bot-sol#id-4.buy-sell)

4.Buy/sell


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here we will be encouraged to do an instant swap or put a limit order. Let's go with every configuration

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-tg-sniper-bot-sol#id-1-swap)

1) Swap

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F3f9XABhvguU7YkhAANDb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8b5795c-8925-4c82-892a-f84e251a9130&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b3aae04&sv=2)

**trubo mode**

swap quickly on chain

**anti-mev**

swap with anti-MEV RPC, the transaction speed is slightly slower

**buy**

we will get the quick purchases that we have set up before in the Settings section and an extra in case we want to buy an "x" amount

**sell**

we will get the percentages of quick sales that we have set before in the Settings section and an extra in case we want to sell an "x" quantity

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-tg-sniper-bot-sol#id-2-limit)

2) Limit

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FdbFrYhALg7q5kKiP9OHl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4fd2c039-470b-40bb-9560-6fbc1ddfe6e3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b77490f&sv=2)

**limit buy**

you can configure the number of SOLs you want to purchase in a limited order

**limit sell**

you can configure the number of tokens to be sold in each limit sell order (percentage)

**trigger price**

you want to execute the order at the price

**exp.3d/24h/1h**

it is the amount of time you want to keep the order open, for example exp 3d will keep the order open for 3 days

**create orde**r

once all the Settings have been made, we give this button and the command will be created

**⚠️**Telegram account security：


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

At present, we only have trading robots on the sol chain, please beware of fake robots and use GMGN official robots.

*   Don't share private keys.
    
*   The TG client should be installed from a formal channel such as Google Play or app store.
    
*   Do not install third party language packs.
    
*   Use the correct GMGN trading bot. There are fake bots on the market.
    
*   The TG account should be verified 2FA(two-factor authentication)to prevent the TG account from being stolen.

# Get the recommended slippage value of ETH/Base/BSC token | GMGN Tutorial

Get the recommended slippage value based on the input blockchain code and token contract address

Access point: https://gmgn.ai/api/v1/recommend\_slippage/sol/9U1NKvb9bUTrqcdymkQ2kDkLxSVyCLUrAfVswcSZPUMP

Request method: GET

Request parameters:

**Parameter name**

**Parameter Description**

**Is it necessary**

**Example**

token\_address

the contract address of the output token

yes

0xbacacd83b68c92ae07ef382d0c0277d1bd1c7c4d

token\_in\_address

enter the token contract address

no, the main purpose is to solve the problem of accumulated slippage when swapping two alt coins

0x0c48250eb1f29491f1efbeec0261eb556f0973c7

Return parameter:

**Parameter name**

**Parameter Description**

**Example**

msg

error message

amountIn is required

code

correct 0, Incorrect -1

0

data

returns the recommended slippage value. If it is 10%, it returns "10". display\_slippage is the displayed slippage value.

{

"recommend\_slippage":"1",

"display\_slippage":"1",

"has\_tax":false

}

[NextGet the recommended gas price for ETH/Base/BSC chain](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-api-integrate-gmgn-eth-base-bsc-trading-api/get-the-recommended-gas-price-for-eth-base-bsc-chain)

# Referral Link | GMGN Tutorial

* * *

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/referral-link#id-1.-obtain-referral-code)

1\. Obtain **Referral Code**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> The GMGN website and Telegram share the same referral code. You can obtain the referral code through the following two methods.

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/referral-link#method-1-obtain-the-referral-code-through-the-gmgn.ai-website)

Method 1: Obtain the referral code through the GMGN.AI website.

Visit the [GMGN.AI](https://gmgn.ai/)
 website, click on "Connect Telegram" button and after refreshing the page, the value of the "ref" parameter in the browser’s address bar will be your referral code.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FOB2TfBCxziMvX46Unzz0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8eeb8ec-d0d8-496c-81d6-5585849fa7dd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e4008e99&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FcEnHsMUA6qUUACy6jlec%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddce477bd-ec7c-4975-9eca-31c5dcac9a59&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=27a7872d&sv=2)

Referral code is 7rpqjHdf

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/referral-link#method-2-obtain-the-referral-code-through-the-telegram-bot)

Method 2: Obtain the referral code through the Telegram Bot

Visit one of the following GMGN Bots (either one, the referral code will be the same) to get your referral code:

*   [https://t.me/gmgnaibot](https://t.me/gmgnaibot)
     (Highly recommended)
    
*   [https://t.me/GMGN\_sol\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)

*   [https://t.me/GMGN\_swap\_bot](https://t.me/GMGN_swap_bot)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252Fi2y01M1c64vr38wg8qF3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D89ec2e6d-857e-4c5f-aa7a-2f2c8f721fe7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66a98c6&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/referral-link#id-2.-referral-link)

2\. Referral link


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

GMGN offers various formats of invitation links. If you’re a KOL, you can use the first format to earn both web and bot trading commissions from a single link. If you manage your own Telegram signal channel, you can try using the second or third formats.

1.  **Invitation to log in to the GMGN.AI website and trade via the Telegram Bot (Highly recommended):**
    

**Applicable scenario:** Quickly invite friends, and your referral code will be automatically bound when they click the link. Whether your friends are using a web extension wallet or the GMGN Telegram Bot’s private key wallet, and regardless of which chain they trade on, you can earn a commission from the trading fees.

1.  **Invitation to use a Telegram trading bot for a specific chain:**
    

**Applicable scenario:** Promoting a specific chain or managing your own Telegram signal channel, this link can direct users to the Telegram trading bot for the specified chain.

1.  **GMGN official website, channel page, specific token, wallet web invitation link**
    

**Applicable scenario:** Promoting a specific chain or managing your own Telegram signal channel, this link directs users to the specified page. After logging into their Telegram account on the website, the user’s referral code will be automatically bound.

# Get the recommended gas price for ETH/Base/BSC chain | GMGN Tutorial

This interface is used to obtain the recommended gas price of ETH/Base chain (real time)

Access point: /defi/quotation/v1/chains/{network}/gas\_price

Request method: GET

Input parameters:

none

Output parameters:

**Parameter name**

**Parameter Description**

E**xample**

msg

cause of error

success

code

error code, 0 means normal, -1 means error

0

data

last\_block, average, high, low, suggest\_base\_fee, eth\_usd\_price, high\_prio\_fee, average\_prio\_fee, low\_prio\_fee and other values

`{"last_block":17527078,"average":"16493364199","high":"17493364199","low":"16493364199","suggest_base_fee":"16493364199","high_prio_fee":"300000000","average_prio_fee":"100000000","low_prio_fee":"50000000","eth_usd_price":"1809.84970000"}`

[PreviousGet the recommended slippage value of ETH/Base/BSC token](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-api-integrate-gmgn-eth-base-bsc-trading-api/get-the-recommended-slippage-value-of-eth-base-bsc-token)
[NextSwap transaction simulation (ETH/Base/BSC)](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/cooperation-api-integrate-gmgn-eth-base-bsc-trading-api/swap-transaction-simulation-eth-base-bsc)
