Part Two


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#competing-on-the-grand-stage-gmgn-on-chain-strategies)

🐎 Competing on the Grand Stage - GMGN On-Chain Strategies


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**There are 4 strategies for on-chain assets.**

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#strategy-1-internal-market)

Strategy 1: Internal Market

Definition: The internal market strategy focuses on identifying investment targets within the Pumpfun internal market before liquidity migrates and while the project remains in its low market capitalization stage.

Typical Case Studies: With tens of thousands of meme coins being launched daily, there are always a few that can yield profits. There are too many to list specific examples.

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#skills-and-characteristics)

Skills and Characteristics:

*   This strategy requires continuous chain screening and prolonged monitoring, dedicating over 10 hours a day to tracking all internal market targets. It may even involve coordinating with multiple people to take shifts and adjust time zones.
    
*   Persistence is crucial, as you need to maintain this routine for several months, even if results aren’t immediate.
    
*   The demands on focus, stamina, and consistency are high, but the capital requirement is relatively low (mostly around 1 $SOL).
    
*   Each successful outcome may not be substantial but is consistently achievable, with potential earnings ranging from a few thousand to tens of thousands of USD daily.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#key-points)

Key Points:

*   Identify targets that can transform from a few tens of thousands of dollars in the internal market to hundreds of thousands (10x), millions (100x), or even tens of millions (1000x) in the external market.
    
*   Eliminate rugs, scams, and wash trading schemes; look for subtle hints of value in assets, such as iconography, websites, developer information, and leaked details from associated addresses.
    
*   The accumulation of experience is essentially an accumulation of familiarity. The current top players have spent approximately a year engaged in PVP internal market activities, working tirelessly. This level of dedication is necessary to sift through 20,000 new projects daily and find valuable opportunities among them.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#detailed-operation-process)

🔧 Detailed Operation Process

1.  Chain Screening: Use the GMGN pumpfun page to monitor all internal market targets.
    
2.  Eliminate: Exclude often-seen images (indicative of wash trading), rug addresses, and targets with unreasonable token distribution (such as wash trading schemes with large holdings, marked in GMGN's analysis section).
    
3.  Pick: Identify projects with thoughtfully designed images and websites and find addresses inadvertently left by devs (linked addresses).
    
4.  Place Bets: Top players don't place many bets daily; the aim isn't to gamble but to pursue strategies with favorable odds and probability. Invest in 1%-5% of the total supply of a token, waiting for the internal market to completed and liquidity to transition to the external market (Raydium), then sell off to secure short-term profits.
    
5.  Sell Off: Typically, once you've secured token positions internally and successfully migrated liquidity externally, most of your internal holdings should be sold off during the price surge towards a million USD market cap.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#strategy-2-external-market-phase-1)

Strategy 2: External Market Phase 1

Definition: The external market level one strategy involves participating in Pumpfun internal market targets after they migrate to the external market. This is when prices can fluctuate rapidly, allowing for PVP (player vs player) trading strategies to buy low and sell high.

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#typical-case-studies)

Typical Case Studies

*   $TRUMP
    
*   $Pnut
    
*   $Luce
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#skills-and-characteristics-1)

Skills and Characteristics

*   This strategy requires ongoing chain screening and continuous monitoring, spending over 10 hours a day observing the market.
    
*   You need a tightly-knit community (both large and small groups, as the accuracy of information may vary) to gather sufficient hot-topic information.
    
*   A well-organized address database is crucial, built around your specific needs. This includes not only collecting addresses of smart money, whales, and large holders but also being very familiar with their trading habits and characteristics.
    
*   A successful external market level one operation can yield returns ranging from tens of thousands of dollars (small PVP tokens) to millions of dollars (e.g., Trump).
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#key-points-1)

Key Points

*   Speed: Quickly get onboard shortly after good targets hit the external market.
    
*   Accuracy: Rapidly assess whether the current market cap of a target is worth investing in, determine the first phase ceiling, and evaluate the risk-reward ratio.
    
*   Firmness: Be willing to invest heavily when a very certain opportunity arises; decisively take profit at the target point; quickly cut losses if an error in judgment is detected.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#detailed-operation-process-1)

🔧 Detailed Operation Process

**1\. Gather Information Sources**

*   Chain Screening
    
*   Community Groups
    
*   Monitored Addresses
    
*   Monitored X (Twitter)
    

**2\. Quick Assessment and Buy-In**

As soon as you obtain the CA (contract address) and project information, make an immediate judgment. This requires experience, as well as collaboration with close friends to supplement information.

Each asset's situation is unique, and the timing of observation varies. Quickly determine whether to invest and how much to allocate.

**3\. Take Profit and Cut Loss**

Typically, the external market phase one is a PVP process. Once the PVP phase concludes, a retracement or drop of at least 80% is likely, and many assets may even go to zero and never recover. Therefore, participating in the external market phase one requires resolute profit-taking or loss-cutting. Experienced phase-one traders often adhere to the concept of "selling on the first sign of red," which highlights the importance of acting swiftly. Once the hype fades, assets engaged in PVP on Solana may face an 80% price drop or even go to zero.

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#case-study-usdtrump)

📜 Case Study: $TRUMP

**1\. Gather Information Sources**

Chain Screening: The $TRUMP token quickly appeared on the GMGN trending list, making it visible to anyone actively involved in chain screening.

Community: Active on-chain communities focused on memecoins, including both large and small groups, mentioned it. Initially, many speculated that it was due to a hacked social media account, which was a divisive piece of information that led many to not invest.

Addresses: Tracking smart money addresses that have already started investing could help you make quick judgments:

*   Whether to invest amid uncertainty.
    
*   Whether to increase your stake when the situation becomes clearer.
    

Twitter Scanning: Verify the $TRUMP Twitter account immediately to see if it posted this meme, confirming the information firsthand.

**2\. Quick Assessment**

Reflecting on the situation, the three key points to assess were:

First, Authenticity

*   Use $TRUMP's Twitter post as a turning point.
    
*   Before the tweet, the project was in an uncertain state; Bold Degens started investing based on details like pool size and fiat purchase options on the official site.
    
*   After the Twitter confirmation, authenticity isn't an issue anymore. The next step is deciding whether to invest and how much.
    

Second, 20% Circulation

*   At the time of $TRUMP's tweet, the market cap was $2 billion.
    
*   After the tweet, it quickly surged to $4 billion, then fell back to $3 billion, marking the best entry point.
    
*   Many who achieved significant results entered at this time.
    
*   Key insight: The actual circulating market cap wasn't $3 billion, but $600 million.
    
*   This information kept many from investing, but quickly checking the information on the official website would have led to better decision-making.
    

Third, Valuation

$TRUMP token valuation has two perspectives:

A. Comparison with Other Assets

*   Elon Musk's $PNUT reached a peak of $2 billion.
    
*   $TRUMP at a $3 billion market cap equates to a $600 million market cap (with 20% circulation).
    
*   Presenting a comparison-based buying opportunity at a value low.
    

B. GMGN Holder Analysis

*   GMGN's holder section reveals purchase prices and holding times for addresses.
    
*   The earliest buyers (except the bold few) purchased at a $3 billion market cap.
    
*   This information justified buying at that point.
    

Those degens who quickly and accurately assessed these three points and boldly placed large bets generally achieved returns of around $10 million (blockchain data is immutable and transparent, allowing everyone to see the clear profits of these addresses).

**3\. Take Profit and Cut Loss**

A good take-profit point should be when the project is listed on centralized exchanges like Binance, OKX, or Coinbase:

*   After listing, the market cap generally reaches its peak.
    
*   The buying power on centralized exchanges represents the final wave of demand.
    
*   At this point, it's best to gradually sell off your holdings.
    

Stop-Loss is determined by:

*   Enforcing a stop-loss based on a predefined loss percentage.
    
*   Fundamental changes (e.g., if Trump claims Twitter was hacked) trigger a stop-loss.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#strategy-3-external-market-phase-2)

Strategy 3: External Market Phase 2

Definition: The second stage of the external market refers to the strategy of identifying and purchasing valuable assets after a 50% or even 80% decline following the end of the first stage (PVP phase). This approach focuses on buying undervalued assets during significant market pullbacks.

**Typical Cases**

*   $AVA
    
*   $Swarms
    
*   $Pippin
    
*   $Ai16Z
    
*   $ACT
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#skills-and-characteristics-2)

Skills and Characteristics

**1\. Basic Requirements**

*   Strong investment research capabilities and a small team are essential.
    
*   Patience is required to avoid participating in the first-stage PVP.
    
*   Avoid being swayed by the rapid price fluctuations in the first stage, as this can disrupt your operational rhythm.
    

**2\. Characteristics of Investment Targets**

*   Select assets with long-term sustainability.
    
*   Exceptional meme potential.
    
*   Assets are backed by a clear team narrative and product.
    

**3\. Capital Requirements**

*   Participation typically requires tens of thousands to hundreds of thousands of dollars.
    
*   The goal is to achieve around 10x returns.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#key-points-2)

Key Points

**1\. Accurate Judgment**

*   Evaluate the team, narrative, product, token distribution, market capitalization, and other factors comprehensively.
    

**2\. Patience**

*   Maintain patience and avoid impulsive decisions.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#detailed-operational-process)

🔧 Detailed Operational Process

**1\. Information Sources**

Post-PVP hotspot assets, closely collaborating team screening, and tracking all significant targets within the sector.

**2\. In-Depth Research (Using AI Assets as an Example)**

Team Evaluation

*   Competence level.
    
*   Integrity and reputation.
    
*   Long-term development intentions (not just seeking quick profits).
    

Narrative Direction

*   Aligns with the current development trends in the AI sector.
    
*   Possesses imaginative and growth potential.
    

Product and Technology

*   Assess Product Market Fit (PMF) potential.
    

Token Distribution Analysis

*   Evaluate distribution fairness.
    
*   Team holdings ratio.
    
*   External market manipulators.
    
*   Market-making team situation (analyzed via GMGN data dashboard).
    

Market Cap Potential

*   Assess current market capitalization.
    
*   Verify potential for 10x or greater growth.
    
*   Determine entry value.
    

**3\. Position Building Strategy**

*   For large funds, patience is advised.
    
*   Gradually build positions over several days.
    

**4\. Take-Profit/Stop-Loss Strategy**

Take-Profit Approach

*   Gradually take profits when psychological targets are met.
    
*   Sell off incrementally.
    

Stop-Loss Strategy

*   No strict loss threshold.
    
*   Emphasize pre-investment research.
    
*   No stop-loss if fundamentals remain unchanged.
    
*   Manage risk through portfolio diversification.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#case-study-usdava-trading)

📜 Case Study: $AVA Trading

**1\. Correct Strategy**

*   Avoid participating in the first stage (from the internal market to $90M market cap).
    
*   Avoid building positions at a market cap of $40M-$60M.
    

**2\. Actual Operation**

*   Started buying incrementally at around $20M market cap (1% position).
    
*   Maintained an average cost basis of $17M.
    
*   Held without stop-loss at $12M market cap (over 30% floating loss).
    
*   Eventually, it rose to around $300M market cap.
    

**3\. Selection Basis**

*   Background as a popular PVP asset.
    
*   Strength of the Holo team.
    
*   Reliable narrative/product direction.
    

**4\. Operational Points**

*   Choose the right entry timing.
    
*   Conduct scientific market analysis.
    
*   Identify precise entry points.
    
*   Allocate position sizes reasonably.
    
*   Utilize GMGN data analysis.
    
*   Continuously monitor token distribution.
    
*   Maintain a firm holding strategy.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#strategy-4-pre-listing-assets-potential-candidate-for-cex-listings)

Strategy 4: Pre-Listing Assets (Potential Candidate for CEX Listings)

Definition: Pre-listing assets refer to projects that have undergone the second stage of the external market, gained widespread market acceptance, and established a strong narrative. These assets are significant within their respective sectors, characterized by high market capitalization, strong liquidity, and a solid community, making them unlikely to suddenly collapse.

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#typical-cases)

Typical Cases

*   $Ai16Z
    
*   $Virtual
    
*   $AIXBT
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#skills-and-characteristics-3)

Skills and Characteristics

**1\. Core Competency Requirements**

*   Deep understanding of listing candidates.
    
*   Firm judgment on sector leaders.
    
*   Substantial capital (e.g., cases involving $10M investments yielding tens of millions in floating profits).
    

**2\. Participant Profile**

*   Investors seeking stable sector returns.
    
*   Large players in both secondary and on-chain markets.
    
*   Investment scale in the range of millions of dollars.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#key-points-3)

Key Points

*   Accurate judgment of sector leaders.
    
*   A clear understanding of Product Market Fit (PMF).
    
*   Ample capital.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#operational-process-characteristics)

🔧 Operational Process Characteristics

*   Similar to the process for second-stage external market assets.
    
*   The main differences lie in certainty and capital requirements.
    
*   Pre-listing assets offer higher certainty.
    
*   Larger capital investments are needed to achieve comparable returns.

This section analyzes and describes the on-chain strategies and their dissemination chains. It aims to clarify how meme coins are traded, who spreads the information, who buys and sells, and the roles each participant plays. It also explains how different players profit in this ecosystem.

From being a "PVP soldier" to becoming a "PVP marshal," the growth path requires selecting the most suitable strategy based on the above analysis and continuously practicing it.

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/gmgn-meme-trading-guide#making-a-name-for-yourself-insights-from-pvp-marshals-and-pvp-generals)

🗡️ Making a Name for Yourself - Insights from PvP Marshals and PVP Generals


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F5tbaf33ByQGgEJEOiRvy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d23c06e-1d44-43e4-9702-6c2289468bac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1bdf4308&sv=2)

I usually maintain over 15 hours of focus using GMGN for on-chain information gathering. When $TRUMP emerged, I was online, and the initial news came from a group chat, with the market cap around $250M at the time. After researching, I found that Trump had posted related information on TruthSocial and provided the contract address on his official website. Initially, I suspected it might be a scam or a hack, but GMGN wallet monitoring showed multiple key addresses consistently buying in. Additionally, $TRUMP's official website allowed the U.S. users to purchase the meme coin with credit cards, which convinced me of its authenticity.

Seizing this opportunity, I invested all $450,000 I had on-chain into $TRUMP. GMGN's node-enabled fast trading allowed me to buy seamlessly within 1 second. However, I did not withdraw additional funds from CEX to on-chain to increase my position, as I considered $450,000 to be the maximum risk I was willing to accept for a potential loss. As for what happened next, most of you probably know—$TRUMP surged from a $200M market cap to $70B, and I successfully profited $17M from it.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FxsAX0mD2bRJuBv3kohtp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db68a966a-5ed1-41b8-82e4-feb9f6e9d655&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=686b6e9e&sv=2)

* * *

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F9gAYYHxfs92Uor6spCXb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2cc6fc04-693e-48da-bcc9-df48b0a8916e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=283291b4&sv=2)

One of the significant advantages of on-chain activities is that everyone can access information, analyze, and execute operations relatively fairly. Take the launch of $TRUMP, for example, which emerged with a relatively low market cap—something unimaginable in the past when centralized exchanges dominated the market. This incident highlights two key points: first, the crypto industry's focus is shifting toward on-chain activities, and second, it demonstrates the opportunities on-chain brings to retail investors.

However, with high returns come high risks. The earlier the project stage, the greater the uncertainty, which significantly tests a player's risk awareness. On-chain, anything is possible, so it's crucial not to get carried away and go all-in.

My personal style is rarely stopping losses. Instead, I aim for overall profitability through the high returns of successful projects. The on-chain environment is rich in high-multiple opportunities, allowing individuals to develop their own methodologies based on their operational style and habits.

* * *

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FBUyXDJOcjYU4jsHn9Qaq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2abae7b5-8b7f-46c6-aa2f-fb62ca1a4d7e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c7b2fb9&sv=2)

I primarily use GMGN's Pumpfun dashboard and wallet monitoring to identify opportunities. Typically, I start by jumping to Twitter and the project's official website to gather information and assess the narrative. If I determine that the narrative has potential, I check the token holder panel below to analyze the token distribution. If the holders are all small accounts or bundled wallets, it’s likely a scam or farm, and I proceed with extra caution. If the token distribution appears natural, with normal players participating and a reasonable market cap, I consider building a position. For early-stage projects, I usually aim to acquire at least 1% of the tokens. GMGN allows me to complete on-chain purchases within 1 second, ensuring my trading decisions are executed swiftly. Additionally, GMGN offers a token distribution analysis feature, displaying a bubble chart that helps analyze the relationships between addresses and token movements.

My judgment of narratives often relies on experience and intuition, requiring quick decisions on whether to participate. Therefore, immersing myself in the market is crucial. Although there are days when I might sit for hours without finding an interesting token, consistent practice is essential to improve my skills and ultimately seize significant opportunities when they arise. For example, when $TRUMP was launched, I noticed purchases through GMGN's wallet monitoring. Using my established information verification process, I quickly completed my checks and began buying. During the selling process, I also refer to signals from monitored wallets to assist in my trading decisions.

* * *

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FbfhNJUZIaZIeSF3n5HfC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86b684dd-1019-4935-8592-f912be1a4efe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=923d0481&sv=2)

When I first saw that Trump had launched a token, my immediate reaction was to suspect whether his account had been hacked again. However, since it was still very early and the market cap was relatively low (around $400M total, with about $100M in circulation), I decided to take a position immediately. I opened GMGN, which I frequently use, and easily found the liquidity pool. I then split my remaining 100 $SOL into two transactions and bought 33,998 $TRUMP tokens. These tokens ended up being my lowest-cost holdings.

After that, I took a moment to calmly review the analysis in group chats. I noticed that respected traders like 0xsun and Calm were also aggressively adding to their positions. This gave me more confidence, so I gradually increased my position to a total value of $100K, with an average cost between $0.6 and $1.5 per token.

As the news spread, $TRUMP quickly rose to $2. However, media outlets began reporting that the authenticity of Trump's token launch was unconfirmed, and some influential KOLs publicly suggested that the account might have been hacked. This caused $TRUMP to rapidly pull back from $2 to below $0.9. Concerned about FUD (fear, uncertainty, and doubt) or a potential reversal, I reduced some of my later-added positions.

When Trump's official Twitter account confirmed the token launch, all doubts vanished. With this second confirmation, $TRUMP's price surged. As more people woke up to the news, they started buying in, and no one questioned whether the account had been hacked anymore—after all, it was unlikely that a U.S. President's social media account could remain compromised for hours without being addressed.

The rest of the story is well-known: $TRUMP quickly listed on all major exchanges, including Binance, Coinbase, and even Robinhood. I sold half of my position at around $65 after the Binance listing and cleared the remaining half at $58 when Melania announced her own token launch, locking in $5M in profits.

Looking back, there are areas where I could have improved. For instance, after the second confirmation from Trump's Twitter, the narrative became highly certain, and I should have aggressively added to my position. Notably, the $TRUMP tokens I bought through GMGN, thanks to their low cost, were held without any swing trading, resulting in a $2.2M profit. Thank you, GMGN!

* * *

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F42OHj1GAjQUCrP5wrgCG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7453606-fc67-4eb1-a1dd-e9d23864c1c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8d4ec65&sv=2)

I’ve been following and using GMGN since its early days, relying on the platform for data analysis and high-frequency trading. Shortly after I started using it, I caught the $TRUMP opportunity—GMGN brought me good luck!

Moreover, data analysis is one of the most essential skills for on-chain players, and this is where I believe GMGN has a broad vision. Even though data analysis doesn’t directly generate profits, GMGN consistently updates and maintains its features, dedicated to serving every memecoin trader.

On the trading front, GMGN was one of the few platforms that allowed early purchases of $TRUMP, thanks to its compatibility with USDC routing and its global multi-node trading services. GMGN also helped me secure a spot on the $TRUMP on-chain profit leaderboard! While tools aren’t the decisive factor in making profits, having reliable tools is essential for success. I believe the era of on-chain assets and meme coins is just beginning.

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252F8wguJHTLC2dSQJCxNAEK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb98a92b-a445-4130-bb9a-8199d1c34fd2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=568ab338&sv=2)

* * *

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FavBjWhDncII2IcZyukit%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddca00c48-1650-4b4a-b3b5-fe184773b7ea&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=130f9c70&sv=2)

Combining my experience with the $TRUMP trade, I’d like to share some of my daily strategies and thoughts on trading memecoins. With thousands of memecoins launching on-chain every day, the first question you need to ask yourself is: Why should I buy this memecoin, and what is its potential upside? These two questions determine the proportion of capital you allocate and your take-profit points, ultimately shaping your risk-reward ratio.

On the day $TRUMP launched, I woke up half an hour late, facing entry costs 3-5 times higher than others. My first move was to analyze the circulating market cap and unlock schedule. After learning that the circulating supply was around 600M with a three-month unlock period, my mind was set on going all-in.

While building my position, I removed all group chats from my pinned messages to avoid external influences. I won’t go into the details of the process, but in the end, I secured a decent profit of $4M. Below, I’ll share some of my personal tips and tricks for trading meme coins based on my accumulated experience.

1.  The platform I use most frequently for dashboards and trading is \[gmgn.ai\] When using the dashboard, my primary focus is on the "Already Launched" section, filtering for market caps above $100K. This helps me avoid early-stage PVP (player vs. player) scenarios and allows me to dedicate more time and energy to analyzing and discovering projects.
    
2.  Once I find a suitable project, the first thing I check is the holder distribution. If GMGN flags a large number of small, suspicious accounts (red indicators) or the token distribution interaction chart looks dubious, I immediately pass on the project. These insights are readily available on GMGN.
    
3.  Currently, meme coins can be broadly categorized into two types: meme coins and utility coins (including celebrity coins).
    

*   For meme coins, my analysis boils down to one question: Does it make me laugh at first glance? Meme coins are highly subjective, and this approach has helped me identify gems like $LLM at a $200K market cap and $moodeng at a $3M market cap.
    
*   For utility coins, I use GMGN's magnifying glass feature to quickly gather information about the project team. Unlike meme coins, utility coins often have a very short window for early positioning, with rapid accumulation in the first few minutes. Speed is crucial, and understanding the team's background and credibility early on can help you secure more tokens at lower prices. I also complement GMGN with AI tools like GROK and ChatGPT to quickly summarize the developers' entrepreneurial history and reputation.
    

1.  During the review phase, GMGN offers a highly useful feature: identifying the top profitable addresses for each trending project. By clicking into these addresses, GMGN provides a clear breakdown of their profits and losses across different projects. This data helps me analyze their trading habits and frequency. Combining this with win rates, I add promising addresses to my monitoring list as alerts for future opportunities
    

Finally, consistent review and thoughtful analysis are key to staying ahead of the curve. Speed and preparation matter more than anything else. There’s no need to feel anxious—this space is full of opportunities. If you truly treat this as your career, take it seriously. The future belongs to us.

* * *

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/index/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3168316658-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcwvUtvEIyqrWZx7sPliY%252Fuploads%252FXxwlf3hDHNYSgdyWVkJa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86594b85-f6d1-4c1e-9285-be2fb4e579f9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a4ef8f37&sv=2)

In this round of on-chain miracles, the window for decision-making was incredibly narrow, requiring rapid judgment under extreme pressure. It was a test of capital, execution, and investment logic at their limits.

When I noticed $TRUMP at $0.8, I had to make a quick decision based on a few key pieces of information: 1. A massive, unlocked liquidity pool worth tens of millions of dollars. 2. Uncertainty about whether the account had been hacked. 3. The project’s official website included a credit card purchase link. Previously, the market had witnessed a similar event with a large pool suddenly disappearing, like the infamous “bald” incident, where the project team drained the pool, causing the token to plummet to zero. However, the presence of a credit card purchase link and related software on the $TRUMP website made it seem relatively trustworthy. At that moment, I decided to take a gamble. I even shared in the community, “Bet on this one—if it works out, it could 10x. If not, it might go to zero, but if they don’t drain the pool immediately, there’s still a chance to exit.” I thought, “If you’re going to gamble, this is the kind of bet worth taking.” Interestingly, during this decision-making process, media outlets spread FUD (fear, uncertainty, and doubt), claiming the pool only had a few hundred $SOL. The price fluctuated wildly, rising from $1 to $2 and then dropping back to $1. As it dipped to $1, I doubled down, thinking, “If you’re going to gamble, go big.” Coincidentally, around this time, Trump’s Twitter account confirmed the launch, and the narrative solidified. In those few minutes, information exploded, and the difficulty of decision-making skyrocketed. Without a robust system and the ability to synthesize information quickly, it would have been terrifying to see a large investment potentially halve or even go to zero in minutes.

When I made the purchase, I used GMGN for the final execution, which completed the on-chain transaction in just 1 second. Looking back, it’s all in the past now, but I remain confident that blockchain will present the next big opportunity.

* * *

# 战壕 | GMGN 使用教程

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/zhan-hao#meme-fa-she-tai)

MEME 发射台


------------------------------------------------------------------

战壕里有着各类meme代币，所以让我向你介绍 Pump.fun 和其他发射台

**1.什么是 Pump.fun？**

Pump.fun 是一个著名的 MEME 代币公平发射平台，没有预售，也没有团队分配。

**2.什么是代币发射台和Pump内盘？**

代币发射台：一句话总结，就是将 meme 代币团队要做的事情产品化，从代币名称、logo 到流动性销毁做到了一条龙服务，从代币发射台发射的代币，在代币合约层面没有貔貅等安全风险。

当成功在 pump.fun 上部署一枚 meme 后，一旦代币市值达到 85 SOL，会自动将 pump.fun 的流动性添加到 Pump AMM，也就是从内盘迁移到外盘。

**3.为什么要玩内盘？**

更早的参与到代币早期，获取更大涨幅，当然风险也会更大，币价波动剧烈，需要盯盘并配合快速交易进行。

**4.GMGN可以提供什么服务**

GMGN网站、App、TG BOT均支持内盘交易，并提供交易meme代币所必须的数据，为你玩转meme代币提供更多数据支撑。

**5.访问战壕**

进入战壕，通过我们提供的各类筛选项，筛选出高质量的meme代币👇🏻：

[![Logo](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgmgn.ai%2Fstatic%2Ffavicon2.ico&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e47fbfa&sv=2)GMGN.AI Fast Trade, Fast Copy Trade, Fast AFK Automation.gmgn](https://gmgn.ai/?chain=sol&ref=Spencer)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/zhan-hao#meme-page-overview)

战壕页面总览：


--------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FarEnXpFOLMUwbnKyljBU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9345a61-3c7b-4cd3-8c8c-c4ed53dcf7c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae9c643&sv=2)

*   快速查看代币各项数据：市值、交易量、总手续费、dev是否出售、社媒信息、捆绑交易比例、狙击者比例、老鼠仓比例、大户持仓比例等。辅助你的交易决策。
    
*   通过丰富的筛选项筛选出高质量代币，挖掘下一个金狗
    

**Pump.fun 上独特的meme上线机制：** 在 pump.fun 上代币上线有两个过程：在 Pump 上线和满足条件后在 Raydium 上线。交互过程与普通代币没有什么不同。 唯一的区别是，Pump 内盘完全填满后，在流动性自动添加到 Raydium 之前有一个等待期，从 10 分钟到大约一个小时不等。

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F1yywDBZVtkZYHoNCxdjX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f886b04-ea7f-4974-bb1a-f302a98ef0ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8128bc0c&sv=2)

**通过 GMGN APP 获取Pump meme打满信号：**

> 如果你在外出时不方便打开 GMGN 网站盯盘，GMGN 还提供 **Pump 打满提醒 Bot**： 你可以通过 Telegram 实时接收打满提醒、外盘开盘提醒，并且一键快速交易。
> 
> 我们也全面支持 **GMGN App** —— 你可以直接在 App 内完成盯盘、接收推送提醒、快速买卖等操作，更适合移动场景下的高频使用。

[Previous安全提示](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi)
[Next新币](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-bi)

# Q＆A常见问题 | GMGN 使用教程

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti#q-how-to-query-token-ca-smart-money-walllet-informations-within-your-tg-group)

Q1：如何在GMGN筛选合适的优质meme


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1）很多小白并不清楚如何去筛选合适的代币，只会找热门币，但通常热门币价格都在高位，已经过了早期增长阶段，此时买入亏损风险很大。在如何筛选优质meme的问题背后是你不知道怎么通过GMGN提供的数据去判断一个meme的各类指标传递出的信号，导致无法选出一部分你认为有潜力的且较为安全的meme。 2）初期你可以首先关注一个meme的安全性，建议你查看这几个页面： [⚡如何成为交易老手](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/ru-he-cheng-wei-jiao-yi-lao-shou)
 [🎯实时监控老鼠仓，狙击手，前70买家持仓出货](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/shi-shi-jian-kong-lao-shu-cang-ju-ji-shou-qian-70-mai-jia-chi-cang-chu-huo)
 [🆗代币安全检测](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/dai-bi-an-quan-jian-ce)
 3）在形成你自己的meme交易体系前可以选择跟单聪明钱：GMGN拥有关于聪明钱的大数据，关注聪明钱后，你可以接收到聪明钱的实时交易动态。特别是随着新meme的发布，会出现聪明钱的集中买入。详情： [💰关注聪明钱，跟单快](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/guan-zhu-cong-ming-qian-gen-dan-kuai)
 4）GMGN只能为你提供数据，本文不作为投资建议，具体的选币思路，交易策略；仓位选择等都需要你自己上手后逐步完善。

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti#q2-jin-fang-jia-mao-guan-li-si-xin-guan-li-yuan-yong-yuan-bu-hui-zhu-dong-si-xin-ni)

Q2：谨防假冒管理私信，管理员永远不会主动私信你


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1）近日多名用户被假冒为管理员的骗子以解决问题为由私信后，向其发送私钥或点击诈骗链接导致钱包被盗，在此提醒各位用户一定要擦亮眼睛，GMGN官方管理员从来不会主动私信任何人，也不会向你索要私钥 2）欺诈账号伪装管理案例：隐藏用户名（user name区），在简介中写上真管理的用户名混淆用户，并实施诈骗，图中即是欺诈账号，请注意辨别，不要相信任何主动私信你的人

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Fe9LEksv8tnicOuCCZxBj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b596490-d253-4250-9972-b130ab0fed9b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f744da9e&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti#q3-ru-he-kai-qi-liu-lan-qi-kong-zhi-tai-yi-xie-zhu-gmgn-jie-jue-ni-de-wen-ti)

Q3：如何开启浏览器控制台以协助 GMGN 解决你的问题


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

第一步：记录问题，全屏截图问题现象，最好录视频

第二步：开控制台并截图

*   在浏览器中右键网页空白处，点击“检查”，自动打开开发者工具后，点顶部“Console”控制台
    
*   把区域高度拖拽拉大，找到红色错误信息（标红或有“Error”）
    
*   截图包含所有红色错误、黄色警告，优先最早错误，截图内容尽可能多
    

第三步：联系客服，或私信官方推特

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FQoRfPq4zBQVz7KaP6be9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D979b8735-4531-4f86-9d29-de1e4d4bf6ce&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ad272787&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti#q4-wang-ye-wu-sheng-yin-wen-ti)

Q4：网页无声音问题


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

当你已经检查过 Chrome 网页声音开关、GMGN 通知设置、GMGN 网页左下角各功能的通知音开关后，仍然没有声音，可以参考以下操作步骤来解决：

*   访问浏览器设置：设置/隐私与安全/网站设置/更多内容设置/声音
    
*   点击「允许播放声音」旁边的添加按钮，输入gmgn.ai 确认添加
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F4nAr5jylWmWChlCvEkWh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db90bf127-6ed4-49cb-80f1-6d930f099173&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bad35f8d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti#q5-qian-bao-bei-dao-dao-ru-si-yao-bei-dao-qian-bao-yuebei-zhuan-yi-wen-ti)

Q5：钱包被盗/导入私钥被盗/钱包余额被转移问题


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

常见情况： 1）是否为安卓机，并且此前点击未知陌生链接导致手机/电脑中了木马或者恶意程序。 2）Telegram app 是否通过官方渠道安装；是否安装了不明来源的第三方电报翻译插件。 3）Telegram 是否授权了陌生假冒bot，并输入了手机号或者点击诈骗链接导致钱包内余额被诈骗bot转移，建议通过多个GMGN官方渠道辨别一致后再进行交易。 4）钱包是否向诈骗应用进行了授权，请进入钱包查询授权列表并取消未知授权。 _例如：有些骗子利用 NFT mint 名额中奖，吸引你在网站签名授权_ 5）如需导入或导出私钥，建议部分复制部分手动输入，降低因为木马读取剪贴板导致的被盗风险。 ⚠️GMGN的第一宗旨即是安全性，不存在因为漏洞导致钱包余额被转移的情况，遇到被盗情况请根据上述列举情况进行自查。 GMGN不会对用户钱包进行任何操作，我们也没有能力转走任何用户的钱包余额。 被盗的心情我们完全理解，被盗的原因基本是上面提到的：设备安全存在问题、使用了假冒诈骗bot，tg异常授权等等，这些都是GMGN官方无法控制的，当前我们只能给你一些自查建议，并告知如何降低后续风险。 建议查看：[OKX 与慢雾安全团队介绍私钥被盗案例、保存方法与防盗策略](https://www.wublock123.com/index.php?m=content&c=index&a=show&catid=47&id=27208)
 建议被盗用户填写[慢雾安全团队被盗申请表](https://aml.slowmist.com/cn/recovery-funds.html)
，可以追踪黑客地址，尝试追回资金。

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti#q6-wei-shen-me-mai-chu-hou-mo-shou-dao-sol-huo-zhe-sol-bian-cheng-le-wsol)

Q6：为什么卖出后没收到SOL或者SOL变成了WSOL？


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1）有可能因为你的滑点以及优先费设置过高，而本金较少，导致卖出后实际还亏损了，误以为SOL未到账，钱包里SOL余额也并未增加。（p1） 2）有可能因为你的钱包里有WSOL，卖出后SOL会自动兑换成WSOL；同时由于SOL链机制问题交易结算时会有一定概率收到WSOL而不是SOL。 GMGN现已上线转换WSOL → SOL快捷功能

具体步骤：在交易机器人 @GMGN\_sol\_bot 里输入/start，点击钱包，点击转换WSOL → SOL即可将收到的WSOL快捷转换为SOL。（p2）

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F2xS84QvRxjfUz8UTMMRI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52cfbdea-3b2f-4a61-a614-bff7b342e984&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8fb8ef8a&sv=2)

p1

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FxdxblBZ0KDhapK2P8cVH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ecca9f9-6207-44fb-ab10-58d806a91a17&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8bc95806&sv=2)

p2

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti#q-how-to-query-token-ca-smart-money-walllet-informations-within-your-tg-group-1)

Q7：关注不了钱包或者关注页面无数据如何解决


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1）网站右上角退出登陆后重新签名，连接钱包后观察是否解决。 2）如果仍然无数据，清理网页缓存可以解决。以google chrome为例：设置-隐私和安全-第三方cookie-查看所有网站数据和权限-清理gmgn缓存。

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Fkp2S7kEq8DyvyD6aklDS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6fe09e58-1702-4921-809f-42e8882a65ef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1ac54780&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti#q-how-to-query-token-ca-smart-money-walllet-informations-within-your-tg-group-2)

Q8：怎么使用GMGN的API?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1）交易API请查看: [🤝🏻 合作-API：📈集成GMGN实时价格图表](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/he-zuo-api-ji-cheng-gmgn-shi-shi-jia-ge-tu-biao)
 [🤝🏻 合作-API：🕹集成GMGN Solana交易API](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/he-zuo-api-ji-cheng-gmgn-solana-jiao-yi-api)
 2）数据API： GMGN目前还没有开放数据API的计划，但可能会为使用我们GMGN交易的用户开放数据抓取IP白名单。我们关心的是你是否已经为我们带来了交易量/用户量 。 如果没有，请选择上面2种的至少其中1种方式做出一定量后再申请。 详情：[🤝🏻 合作-API：🔄接入数据API](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/he-zuo-api-shu-ju-zhua-qu-ip-bai-ming-dan)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti#q-how-to-use-the-contract-query-bot-smart-money-tracking-bot-in-gmgn-official-group)

 2）现在你可以在其中使用合约查询机器人，群组聪明钱跟踪机器人将自动推送消息 3）复制CA或聪明钱地址并发送到社群，机器人将回复详细信息。 详细教程请[点击这里](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/gmgn-tg-xin-hao-pin-dao-he-ji-qi-ren#how-to-use-gmgn-signal-alert-bots)

Q10：如何在你的tg群组中查询代币CA/聪明钱详细信息？

1）添加群组合约查询机器人：[https://t.me/GMGNAI\_bot](https://t.me/GMGNAI_bot)
 2）邀请@GMGNAI\_bot加入你的群组（p2） (_**ps：**__step1）＆2）您可以使用此步骤代替，单击此处立即邀请该机器人加入群组：_[_https://t.me/GMGNAI\_bot?startgroup=true_](https://t.me/GMGNAI_bot?startgroup=true)
 _)_ 3）为机器人设置管理员角色（p3） 4）你的小组成员发送**CA**或**聪明钱地址**，机器人将回复详细信息（p4） 详细教程请[点击这里](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/yao-qing-gmgnaibot)

**Q11：** 如何让机器人在你的 tg 群组中自动发送聪明钱动态信号？


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1）添加群组聪明钱跟踪机器人**：** [https://t.me/alert\_gmgnbot](https://t.me/alert_gmgnbot)
 2）邀请@Alert\_GMGNBOT加入你的群组（p2） (_**ps：**__step1）＆2）您可以使用此步骤代替，单击此处立即邀请该机器人加入群组：_[_https://t.me/Alert\_GMGNBOT?startgroup=true_](https://t.me/Alert_GMGNBOT?startgroup=true)
 ) 3）为机器人设置管理员角色（p3） 4）群组管理员发送**/set**，在设置中添加智能钱包和推荐代码（p4） 详细教程请[点击这里](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/yao-qing-alertgmgnbot)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FUYZT6OejxsOhPW51fDzg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d6b3ff1-a294-4c19-b1df-4d95a72f29ba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=78c729dd&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FDgx60dUXhWrXcmp23lBy%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29b9dba0-92af-4c88-b582-2a64522dc1ce&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71bec7fb&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FXnyL5T7dzgLVs6nL2MtH%252F114.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3d1655d-8271-4024-9b7f-3ca87304ae24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2a44aaba&sv=2)

新池子

添加了流动性的新池子

烧池子

烧池子100%意味着发行方不能砸盘

DEXScreener 花钱

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F32sRNm5u4x1lcW4U5a89%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7896cff6-1dab-4b80-877a-2747a0f804c4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7bc02912&sv=2)

**在最新版本中，我们支持过滤不同种类的meme：**Pump，Moonshot，Raydium

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FeFDKmLeowwV2FnAr92oI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f36164b-2029-458b-b944-ac258aa3abd3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6726f62e&sv=2)

创建时间

该代币创建时间

当前池子/初始

目前池子里的流动性和初始量

流通市值

流通市值

持有者

持有者数量：一般越多盘越大

xx 交易数

绿色为买入数量，红色为卖出数量

xx 成交额

xx时间内成交额，可以用过滤项选择筛选

价格

当前价格

1m% 5m% 1h%

该代币在最近1分钟/5分钟/1小时内的价格波动百分比

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Fm9cb9zfAiXqsAncih1xq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e4bb2e2-faf1-4caf-abdc-119fd27f381e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3bd24cbf&sv=2)

Mint丢弃

“是”时比较安全，意味着项目方不能增发代币砸盘。

Top10持仓

“是”时比较安全，意味着前10持币大户的持仓总量小于总供应量的30%

黑名单

“否”时比较安全，意味着项目方不能拉黑任意钱包的转账，降低貔貅风险 “是”时请注意，你在这个代币开发者的黑名单上，你不能出售这个代币，它会提醒你的钱包被冻结了。

烧池子

显示烧池子百分比，比例越高越好，100%意味着项目方不能撤池子。

老鼠仓

开盘后没有买入，但是有持仓，可能是项目方持仓批量转移到多个小号钱包，偷偷砸盘出货。正规项目一般是空投用户，需要找官方推特查看是否有空投领取活动

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-bi#for-more-details-about-token-security-checks-please-click-the-link)

热门


-------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FupSe6XSL9fCJ9GvmReU7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44164498-9d0f-4108-b19d-a00215e922d0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a611249d&sv=2)

创建

该代币创建时间

当前池子/流通市值

目前池子里的流动性和流通市值

持有者

持有者数量：一般越多盘越大

xx 交易数

绿色为买入数量，红色为卖出数量

xx 成交额

xx时间内成交额，可以用过滤项选择筛选

当前价格

1m% 5m% 1h%

安全检测

[安全检测](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/dai-bi-an-quan-jian-ce)

*   热门趋势页面供你查看人们购买和出售的热门代币
    
*   我们为你提供了多种过滤器供您筛选和排序，就像 NEW PAIR 页面一样。此外，你可以选择不同的时间间隔（1 分钟/5 分钟/30 分钟/1 小时）来查看在这些时间范围内呈趋势的代币
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Fiudccm260PdB3ZufSvHz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b4a5e72-c0f7-4e70-93a1-63477b436d94&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7eefd331&sv=2)

*   在代币左侧，你可以点击小星星，将其添加到 **关注-收藏** 中
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/re-men#xia-ge-lan-chou)

下个蓝筹


------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FDLv3NCQ1666CsdPgK3jn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D667f4bde-55ab-4b4a-ba6c-8ed45d452f70&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c40814d&sv=2)

*   蓝筹代币：蓝筹代币是指各条链上经过市场验证与认可，具有较高价值，不会轻易归零的代币，例如sol链 neiro、popcat
    
*   蓝筹持有者：拥有一定蓝筹代币的持有者
    
*   蓝筹指数：蓝筹指数是指该代币的持有者中同时拥有蓝筹代币的比例
    
*   蓝筹指数意义：在一个代币中，拥有蓝筹代币的持有者越多，即蓝筹指数越高，蓝筹持有者越看好这个币，这个币越有可能成为下一个高价值蓝筹代币
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/re-men#xiang-guan-tu-biao-ding-yi-qing-dian-ji)

相关图标定义请点击：

# 钱包详情页 | GMGN 使用教程

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qian-bao-xiang-qing-ye#qian-bao-xiang-qing-ye)

钱包详情页：

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FyLPwQMwxBOzMH32eNFaF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9077c5da-5f0c-4308-9c34-cd8528f94456&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd4ced56&sv=2)

**上方功能模块：**

*   点击钱包名称旁边按钮可以对钱包名称进行备注
    
*   点击合约地址旁边按钮可以复制CA或者跳转solscan.io查询钱包活动
    
*   点击推特可以跳转到该钱包拥有者的钱包地址
    
*   点击钱包跟单可以复制该钱包的交易，详情请查看：[钱包跟单：跟单聪明钱自动赚SOL！](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qian-bao-gen-dan-gen-dan-cong-ming-qian-zi-dong-zhuan-sol)
    
*   点击【关注】后，该钱包会被加入你的追踪列表，你可以在左下角【钱包追踪】中查看该钱包的全部操作，并通过 **0 延迟机器人** 接收该钱包的实时交易通知
    
    在 **GMGN App** 中，点击底部【钱包跟单】，在顶部切换到【关注】即可查看已关注的钱包，在【活动】页可以看到这些钱包的最新买卖记录；开启 App 通知后，可同步收到相关推送提醒
    

**最近7D/30D盈亏/胜率：**

*   查看该钱包最近的D盈亏比例以及资金盈亏数额
    
*   查看钱包当前胜率以及钱包余额
    

**利润：**

7D 交易数

绿色代表买入笔数/红色代表卖出笔数

总盈亏

该钱包所有交易盈亏数额以及盈亏比例

未实现利润

该钱包当前未出售的代币价值

7D/30D 平均持仓时长

最近7天/30天，买入代币后平均持有多长时间才卖

7D/30D 买入总成本

最近7天/30天，买入代币花费的总成本

7D/30D 代币平均买入成本

最近7天/30天，买入代币花费的总成本除以买入代币数量

7D/30D 代币平均实现利润

最近7天/30天，平均每个代笔已售出部分实现的利润（未计算未实现利润）

**盈利分布：**

*   可以看到该钱包在最近7天/30天，买入的代币的涨跌的幅度以及个数
    

**钓鱼检测：**

黑名单

该钱包买入黑名单/貔貅代币数量，过多可能是项目方钓鱼钱包

没购买

该钱包内非买入代币数量，可以分析有多少代币是从其他地方转账过来，从而分析钱包属性

卖出量大于买入量

该钱包卖出量大于买入量的代币个数

十秒内完成买/卖

十秒内完成买/卖交易的代币个数，可能是刷单机器人或者割跟单的钱包

[Previous信号：狙击新币、已关注、挂单列表](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-hao-ju-ji-xin-bi-yi-guan-zhu-gua-dan-lie-biao)

# 信号：狙击新币、已关注、挂单列表 | GMGN 使用教程

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-hao-ju-ji-xin-bi-yi-guan-zhu-gua-dan-lie-biao#id-1.-ju-ji-xin-bi)

1\. 狙击新币


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-hao-ju-ji-xin-bi-yi-guan-zhu-gua-dan-lie-biao#web-duan-xin-hao-ye-di-bu-xin-hao-ru-kou)

**Web 端信号页（底部【信号】入口）：**

通过底部【信号】入口进入信号页面，你可以看到多种市场信号：

*   DexScreener 付费信号（普通广告、加速推广、顶置广告、更新社媒等）
    
*   价格提醒（价格飙升、历史新高、关键市值）
    
*   其他信号（Pump 直播、社区接管等）
    

支持按时间、市值、总手续费等条件进行筛选，方便你快速发现高关注度、强异动的代币

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-hao-ju-ji-xin-bi-yi-guan-zhu-gua-dan-lie-biao#gmgn-app-xin-hao-ru-kou-ai-xin-hao)

**GMGN App 信号入口（AI 信号）：**

在 App 底部导航点击【监控】，再切换到顶部【AI 信号】标签，即可进入 App 的信号列表页面：

*   查看系统筛选出的优质代币信号
    
*   一键跳转到代币详情页做进一步分析和交易
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-hao-ju-ji-xin-bi-yi-guan-zhu-gua-dan-lie-biao#id-2.-qian-bao-zhui-zong)

**2\. 钱包追踪**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Web左下角【钱包追踪】页面，你可以看到所有已追踪钱包的操作记录，并可开启 GMGN 网页通知，或接入 **0 延迟机器人**，及时收到这些钱包的交易提醒。

在 **GMGN App** 中，钱包追踪入口为：

*   顶部切换到【关注】标签，可查看你追踪的钱包列表
    
*   切换到【活动】标签，可查看这些钱包的实时买卖记录；开启 App 通知后，可同步收到相关推送提醒
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FIVCEphS1FqNarM0wCnYm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da62edfac-74ce-4eaf-9da5-e9b82a383a95&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b68b52c&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-hao-ju-ji-xin-bi-yi-guan-zhu-gua-dan-lie-biao#id-3.-gua-dan-lie-biao)

**3\. 挂单列表**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Web 端**：

*   点击交易，打开挂单列表，查看你的所有挂单信息
    
*   你可以在任意代币的详情页中，切换到顶部的【订单】标签，查看该代币下你的所有挂单、自动交易和高级策略订单信息
    

**GMGN App**：

*   打开 App 进入【资产】页，选择对应钱包后，在钱包详情中切换到【订单】标签，即可在手机上查看和管理当前钱包的挂单以及各类策略订单。
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FPxw3JAMkGKzAlxVhItc4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbdd739f7-7da9-4a47-9771-65a5e5480dfe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d0963e6d&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-hao-ju-ji-xin-bi-yi-guan-zhu-gua-dan-lie-biao#mian-ze-sheng-ming-jiao-yi-qian-qing-jian-cha-dai-bi-feng-xian)

⚠️ 免责声明：交易前请检查代币风险！

# 安全提示 | GMGN 使用教程

本文将介绍常见的黑客攻击钓鱼手段以及如何在网页插件钱包、GMGN TG钱包中做好安全设置，预防被盗

**在区块链黑暗森林世界里，首先牢记下面这两大安全法则：**

*   **零信任** 简单来说就是保持怀疑，而且是始终保持怀疑，对于任何需要输入私钥的平台、机器人、插件钱包授权签名等保持怀疑
    
*   **持续验证** 你要相信，你就必须有能力去验证你怀疑的点，并把这种能力养成习惯
    

1.  [被盗：常见黑客钓鱼以及攻击手段](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi#id-1.-bei-dao-chang-jian-hei-ke-diao-yu-yi-ji-gong-ji-shou-duan)
    
2.  [防盗：在插件钱包以及TG 钱包中做好预防](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi#id-2.-fang-dao-zai-cha-jian-qian-bao-yi-ji-tg-qian-bao-zhong-zuo-hao-yu-fang)
    
3.  [设备安全](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi#id-3.-she-bei-an-quan)
    
4.  [被盗了怎么办](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi#id-4.-bei-dao-le-zen-me-ban)
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi#id-1.-bei-dao-chang-jian-hei-ke-diao-yu-yi-ji-gong-ji-shou-duan)

1\. 被盗：常见黑客钓鱼以及攻击手段


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**TG里的诈骗：**

1）请记得官方管理员不会主动私信你！！！骗子冒充GMGN 管理员发送诈骗信息，骗取私钥或盗取TG账户！

*   常见情况：你在社群内发送消息，骗子借着帮你解决问题的理由要求你配合，最终导致被盗。有的骗子会隐藏用户id，把真的管理员名字填在简介里，迷惑性很强，容易导致被盗用户以为是官方诈骗！
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FgR0gq65LocTtXqL9A0lU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfec5cb12-dbb9-4669-9c02-ed8d1fa96ba5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=961f199b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FCJxlb3EaFt4A3LAlraJ2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb90d6e5-f53e-455c-b61a-8919783620ca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8da7aa3&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FwAMjVy4ak6qul37zMZHY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24c23de8-d74d-41c6-95ec-625ba3542505&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4239be74&sv=2)

2）不要点击显示在 GMGN 机器人上方的任何广告！这些是骗子，可能会盗取你的钱包！ GMGN 官方机器人绝不会先向你索取钱包的私钥！

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FmeUldNXD4q4W8XqXNDsC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D66241d4e-ea68-4df4-9a04-f9f356b85994&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=327fc63a&sv=2)

3）在某些代币的TG群组或者某些骗子发送的链接里会出现该类所谓的“安全验证”，请不要点击！也不要输入你的任何账户信息，包括手机号，密码等！

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FgFNJiaTqbuc19wQiEwvL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D788a00d1-f876-4170-8229-c908112d8988&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c82be57&sv=2)

4）骗子复制一个GMGN仿冒群，将你拉入群组当中，在仿冒群组发布诈骗链接骗取私钥！由于群内有大量机器人导致看上去人数较多，并且会搬运真群消息，容易被误以为是官方群，请通过GMGN官方推特确认是否为真群！！[https://x.com/gmgnai](https://x.com/gmgnai)

*   建议用户在 隐私和安全-群组和频道 中勾选 不允许任何人，这将不允许任何人添加你到陌生的群组和频道，可以有效杜绝被拉入诈骗群组
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FSVw6Yk6mcuD6aVQFUlRg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80cdde2f-0205-410d-9fdb-970f11d65984&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a508dd0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FjLNMNlIzRke1mBjGHxQU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ba1a830-6107-4b62-a62e-fdbd9ec82d22&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=42319317&sv=2)

5）骗子假装是Telegram官方给你发送消息，诈骗话术如图，引导你点击诈骗链接，请不要点击！！直接举报拉黑即可！

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F3y9LwRWu2nziPI9e0VIy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2410b8a-5499-4977-ae0d-76b3782dfb3c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba28aaa5&sv=2)

**Web3 插件钱包里的诈骗：**

1）签名安全里首要遵守的最大安全原则是：所见即所签。因此需要定期确认钱包是否向你不熟悉的，陌生应用进行了授权，请进入钱包查询授权列表并取消未知授权！

*   空投诈骗：Solana 上的授权钓鱼，攻击者批量给用户空投 NFT(图 1) ，用户通过空投 NFT 描述内容里的链接进入目标网站，连接钱包(图 2)，点击页面上的“Mint”，出现批准提示框(图 3)。注意，此时的批准提示框并没有什么特别提示，当批准后，该钱包里的所有 SOL 都会被转走
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FEn40cyaTiWhIYJajYefT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da75ecd5b-c27b-4a43-b4cb-75a7bc60b7f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=227aa0a9&sv=2)

2）陌生转账：有时钱包内会收到这种金额很小的陌生转账，大多为广告或诈骗相关，不必抱有好奇心，也不会影响到你钱包的正常操作，不用过于担心

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FEhlnQMynstZG9SePnruI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1e0e5fc-d68e-4f95-b6a0-339b09daa881&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe29ce09&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi#id-2.-fang-dao-zai-cha-jian-qian-bao-yi-ji-tg-qian-bao-zhong-zuo-hao-yu-fang)

2\. 防盗：在插件钱包以及TG 钱包中做好预防


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Telegram 安全预防：**

1）建议不是那么熟悉“TG 隐私和安全”的用户照搬下列设置，尤其是记得图中标红的几项一定要打开，能有效保证你的TG 账户安全

*   两步验证：开启后，黑客即使得到了你的手机号和密码，但在新设备上登陆时在输入短信验证码后仍然需要输入一个单独的密码，充分保证安全
    
*   手机号码：防止黑客直接获得你的手机号，向你发送诈骗短信或进行其他诈骗行为
    
*   群组与频道：被盗4）中有相关例子，可以有效杜绝被拉入诈骗群组
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FRR5gtvFWzM9AHh7MRHoG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc91d4dd1-5a3e-468e-8f3f-40f5f111b023&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=de841cbd&sv=2)

2）确认你的Telegram app 是否通过官方渠道安装

3）Telegram 是否授权了陌生假冒bot，避免因为输入手机号或者点击诈骗链接导致钱包内余额被诈骗bot转移，建议通过多个GMGN官方渠道辨别一致后再进行交易

4）确认你是否安装的是官方来源的电报中文翻译插件，市面上有很多不明来源的第三方翻译插件，请注意辨别；TG官方有中文测试版，需要到官网下载

*   官网底部点击Translations(图1)，跳转后点击Other languagues，选择中文(图2)，随后拖到底部点击应用(图3)，将打开你的TG应用进行中文配置
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FBc3dNyXV1ssr389lacd8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83f12260-cb1c-40d2-9cf2-18bcdb592839&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c517cbcf&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FCOA4TaxwyUQ4whDMvyYg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09ef40e6-6b9c-4331-92ca-962f7f914728&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9833c8a9&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FnxtYzyAsodPGnIlqMtck%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9de92662-806b-47ff-8385-0a926818d6ac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b506cc54&sv=2)

**Web3 插件钱包：**

1）进入web3 插件钱包中查询授权列表，并取消未知授权，确认已授权的应用都为对应官方应用

2）打开自动锁定时间，避免因为设备离身的时候被其他人看到你的私钥

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F5Wcr4oMGv7ZDTwvbXzFK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7e18092-1602-4743-8ed5-a295850af5bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=63329183&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FSwsCvNcERPxP3Lf7vTh0%252Fimage%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13afca64-ade9-4a6d-8ed3-80e5702917be&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4ebfaac1&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi#id-3.-she-bei-an-quan)

3\. 设备安全


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1）如果你的设备为安卓机/windows电脑/非ipad平板，请注意不要点击未知陌生链接或者下载不明应用，避免手机/电脑中木马或者恶意程序，并且定期用安全软件检查设备，消杀病毒，防范风险

2）如果你的设备为苹果设备，app store以及未正式上线的测试软件中仍有一些诈骗应用的存在，需要注意防范

3）安全原则：

*   网络上的知识，凡事都参考至少两个来源的信息，彼此佐证，始终保持怀疑
    
*   做好隔离，也就是鸡蛋不要放在一个篮子里
    
*   对于存有重要资产的钱包，不做轻易更新，够用就好
    
*   所见即所签。即你看到的内容就是你预期要签名的内容，当你签名发出去后，结果就应该是你预期的，绝不是事后拍断大腿的
    
*   重视系统安全更新，有安全更新就立即行动
    
*   不乱下程序其实已经杜绝了绝大多数风险了
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi#id-4.-bei-dao-le-zen-me-ban)

4\. 被盗了怎么办


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

基本所有Web3用户都被盗过，我们建议被盗用户填写[慢雾安全团队被盗申请表](https://aml.slowmist.com/cn/recovery-funds.html)
，可以追踪黑客地址，尝试追回资金。

1）止损第一。止损就是让损失不会继续放大。这分为至少两个阶段：

*   眼前着急阶段。眼前的绝对是当务之急的，比如你看到黑客正在陆续转移你的资产，需要赶紧抢着把剩余资产安全转移。有交易抢跑经验的，就抢跑。看资产类型，如果是那种可以链上冻结的，就尽可能联系冻结。有能力做链上追踪分析的发现资金转移进中心化平台，就可以联系做必要风控
    
*   局面控制后阶段。局面稳住后，重点要琢磨的是如何不会出现二次、三次伤害
    

2）保护好现场。发现被盗后，千万冷静，深呼吸，一定要保护好有关现场。有几个经验供参考：

*   针对电脑、服务器这类联网设备，一旦这些是事故主场，立即断网，但不关机（电源供电持续）
    
*   除非你自己有能力，否则等待专业安全人员介入取证分析
    

3）分析原因

*   分析原因的目的是了解资产是如何被盗走的：私钥被盗/TG账户被盗/设备被入侵等
    
*   比如至少把以下几点梳理清楚：
    
    *   概要 1：什么人、什么时间、发生了什么事、总损失多少？
        
    *   概要 2：损失有关的钱包地址、黑客钱包地址、币种类型、数量，一个表格就比较清晰了
        
    

4）填写慢雾安全团队被盗申请表

建议被盗用户填写[慢雾安全团队被盗申请表](https://aml.slowmist.com/cn/recovery-funds.html)
，将限制黑客及相关地址在CEX出入金，并且追踪黑客地址，尝试追回资金

⚠️GMGN的第一宗旨即是安全性，不存在因为漏洞导致钱包余额被转移的情况，遇到被盗情况请根据上述列举情况进行自查。 GMGN不会对用户钱包进行任何操作，我们也没有能力转走任何用户的钱包余额。

[PreviousQ＆A常见问题](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qa-chang-jian-wen-ti)
[Next战壕](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/zhan-hao)

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [2\. 防盗：在插件钱包以及TG 钱包中做好预防](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/an-quan-ti-shi#id-2.-fang-dao-zai-cha-jian-qian-bao-yi-ji-tg-qian-bao-zhong-zuo-hao-yu-fang)

# 关注：监控广场、关注、收藏 | GMGN 使用教程

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/guan-zhu-jian-kong-guang-chang-guan-zhu-shou-cang#follow-page-overview)

关注页面总览

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FvacGZZ6hii1aDk2SO6al%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D353a1993-30dc-4760-bd5a-e5bc640d7308&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3c219847&sv=2)

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/guan-zhu-jian-kong-guang-chang-guan-zhu-shou-cang#id-2.in-the-follow-follow)

1.监控广场


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FjRcwPavTPLNYagOHkBVZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4e7ab62-08ef-40ee-816c-4b0f50429a94&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ddeeafe0&sv=2)

GMGN监控广场能让你查看你所有已关注钱包的资金流向，帮助你通过钱包间的共同买入及时抓住金狗

*   可以自由选择净流入时间范围 1m/5m/1h/6h/24h
    
*   可以看到代币的各类数据，包含市值、成交额、社媒等信息
    
*   左下角隐藏不感兴趣的代币
    
*   右下角可以通过预设完成的立即买入按钮实现一键买入
    
*   左侧榜单也能直接查看关注净流入信息
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/guan-zhu-jian-kong-guang-chang-guan-zhu-shou-cang#id-2.in-the-follow-follow-1)

2.关注


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FfmxClwN32S4wKHSpTNAd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D429e6f7f-76c0-426b-8783-18bab9608c91&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0a6f074&sv=2)

*   点击红色区域可自动跳转到 Telegram 页面并关注官方 GMGN 信号机器人
    
*   点击钱包地址查看你关注的钱包详情页面：[钱包详情页](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qian-bao-xiang-qing-ye)
    

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/guan-zhu-jian-kong-guang-chang-guan-zhu-shou-cang#id-1.in-the-follow-watchlist)

3\. 收藏


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Fqqbz1qVllUscUoOX0Nw3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b2169c2-f206-462d-9468-bcc93f9788e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=629b50ff&sv=2)

*   支持收藏代币分组，点击代币左侧小星星即可将代币添加至你的自定义分组列表
    
*   **Web 端**：在代币名称右侧点击编辑按钮，即可新增或修改备注名，Web 端各页面已全面支持代币备注显示
    
*   **H5 页面**：战壕页已支持对代币添加备注，在手机浏览器中也可以为代币做标记。
    
*   **GMGN App**：在【收藏】页面长按某个代币，即可为该代币新增或修改备注名称，方便对重点标的做个性化备注和管理。
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F6eNDt7LUqBzl2IC4qMlm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15c26b74-ae79-4d39-8965-eccc008ed823&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66e840e7&sv=2)

*   点击查看你收藏的代币交易详情页面：[代币详情页：K线 - 多图表、交易活动、交易系统](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/dai-bi-xiang-qing-yekxian-duo-tu-biao-jiao-yi-huo-dong-jiao-yi-xi-tong)

# 探索 | GMGN 使用教程

探索页面总览:


-------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FoLVEagcdZ2tts020hPHR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21f39a68-8a86-4a39-bc32-30b2d01f2370&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5f1b0f5a&sv=2)

# 0 延时钱包监控Bot | GMGN 使用教程

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FYJ1NmSUIhEyaNA2WVhls%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db595ce4a-82dc-4e06-a61c-35bb25ea75e9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8aa4d6e6&sv=2)

0 延时推送钱包监控消息

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FUyr42WPr6oPywgiKzaex%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D852055d1-63e8-46ec-b61a-0fa0b51ce641&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40d36ecd&sv=2)

配置界面，支持10个bot

**低延时钱包监控Bot**

独享私有节点，推送通道加速，毫秒级监控速度，一键快速交易，**突破500个监控钱包上限**(申请多个0延时钱包监控权限账号，然后在各自配置表单里填写同一个群ID)。请访问 [https://gmgn.ai/follow/?chain=sol&tab=follow](https://gmgn.ai/follow/?chain=sol&tab=follow)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FBBytewvtVMWSl4MwNIcO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3f00a34-538f-48f9-bd07-97fe3053b1f4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d6c31c11&sv=2)

**常见问题**

**问：为何测试消息发不出去？**

**解决办法：**一般情况，-4开头或者-1开头的groupid都可以发送测试消息，如果你的Telegram账号是虚拟手机号，可能会触发Telegram安全风险控制，导致bot在建的群内不能发送消息。你可以尝试在群里输入 /groupid ，如果@GMGN\_vip\_bot 可以发送消息，说明群权限配置正常；如果bot无响应，请尝试把@GMGN\_vip\_bot加到管理员角色，或者多拉几个朋友进群，然后尝试发送 /groupid 命令，看看是否可以发送消息。注意，群id不是一直不变的，随着群内成员数增多，群ID可能由-4开头变成-1开头，需要重新配置0延时通知bot表单。

**设置步骤：**

1.  点击创建Telegram群
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FKkE3HjQy7EqkFhv9WbqC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06b26862-2fc5-4c00-848a-51b3afbe634c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebc668b5&sv=2)

1.  [点击这里](https://t.me/GMGN_vip_bot?startgroup=true)
    ，邀请Bot [@GMGN\_vip\_Bot](https://t.me/GMGN_vip_bot)
     进新创建的Telegram群。或者点击群右上角info，点击Add添加成员，搜索"@GMGN\_vip\_Bot" (注意认准Bot唯一ID是"@GMGN\_vip\_Bot"，不要添加其他骗子的bot)
    

1.  复制群ID，或者点击“创建通知”按钮，跳转后自动填写群ID
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FKsWCadz7JeMNenM6ELoB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbb9c770-2712-4814-8125-cc5b53507e00&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bfbdc68f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Fvs1IJbfguWDYetp6mTvT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6547868a-1809-4ba5-8503-6acd217669e7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d0c86815&sv=2)

1.  创建群Bot：点击 [@BotFather](https://t.me/BotFather)
     ，在对话框内输入 /newbot ，先填写bot名称，再填写bot的用户名(必须以"bot"结尾，不能用其他人的bot重复)。创建成功后，复制下图红框里的bot API token。
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FEoEy0JOrlK2Z4G3ohwhM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D162b4fa4-9a66-4c2d-87c7-3266c7cad816&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=397bf837&sv=2)

1.  粘贴bot API token到表单，最多支持填写10个bot token。
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FhQqmisMxDZSC7i9WKcGp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd7b59c8-9553-4aab-a78f-505759480488&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4148a4e4&sv=2)

1.  邀请刚刚创建的bot进Telegram群
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F2rzBaTjQ9cUm43xMY921%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05d7c01e-03e8-42da-8c90-66a0950d0ccb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2620d524&sv=2)

1.  为你的 bot 设置群管理权限
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FSkQmJ0mPJukWVa8vy1Ry%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd143ead0-4d4e-437e-9bcc-c1a05b9b1ba9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc92486f&sv=2)

1.  点击测试消息按钮，查看是否成功发送消息。如果失败，请检查群ID，bot token是否正确，以及Telegram是否给bot开通发送消息权限。
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FLWJiaJ7AzOcWt71PaidE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0bc9c69-eded-431c-a645-edc54516b2c7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f99f952&sv=2)

点击测试消息

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Ff81v4vxtKVMvhGFeGcgx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2999f37b-37c3-42d7-8e26-c860ee3164d3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d187f69b&sv=2)

测试消息发送成功

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FTcSMxzJuUJVxjBPaw60C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c984c01-4b5d-4749-964b-c8dfc24e335b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=92cc9e69&sv=2)

消息发送失败

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FPTTBrtIalT7PJY6g0qic%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5d1e894-e87c-4e1b-a3c6-2e3b15d9affb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71593c94&sv=2)

测试消息发送成功

1.  设置消息参数：支持设置交易类型（全部/买入/卖出），接收通知语言，交易金额(开发中)，然后点击保存
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252F3XCJRwFf3S5LdTv1zYRe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D539ad50e-103f-4172-bc28-7d52e88211f8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf194621&sv=2)

1.  保存成功后，关注的钱包交易动态，会实时推送到Telegram群
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FLvh9erDo62cAZh1HvzxY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D297bb916-0e57-4fc0-a7c3-e8d70476b2c3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a939f61a&sv=2)

# TG ETH 狙击机器人 | GMGN 使用教程

**🌈 使用GMGN Telegram Swap Bot**交易 ETH MEME代币👇🏻**：**

[**https://t.me/GMGN\_swap\_bot**](https://t.me/GMGN_swap_bot)
 [**https://t.me/GMGN\_swap02\_bot**](https://t.me/GMGN_swap02_bot)

⚠️使用机器人的第一件事是在 **钱包** 里导出自动生成的钱包的私钥。私钥代码将允许你在任何支持该链的 web3 钱包中导入。在保存私钥/更换新钱包/导出私钥过程中请务必注意私钥安全

*   只允许导出一次私钥，只能导出 GMGN 生成的bot钱包的私钥，自己导入的私钥不能导出
    
*   请注意，导出是一次性把所有链的钱包私钥都导出，不是只有 SOL 链私钥导出
    
*   请注意 EVM 钱包均为同一套钱包地址和私钥，即ETH、Base、BSC链钱包地址和私钥均相同。因此导出私钥时总共3个钱包地址和私钥（SOL链、EVM链、Tron链）
    
*   文件名：GMGN-wallet-keys 示例： 2YC 为 SOL 链钱包地址，644 为该钱包地址私钥 0xa 为 EVM（同时为ETH、Base、BSC链）钱包地址，0xd 为该钱包地址私钥 TMW 为 Tron 链钱包地址，e95 为该钱包地址私钥
    

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FB8MyRuyDQvCLiGFfHswf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df515fa8f-c1b8-4293-af3d-29e241743a97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8de24fe&sv=2)

[PreviousTG Solana 狙击机器人](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/tg-solana-ju-ji-ji-qi-ren)
[NextTG 钱包：连接TG、多钱包系统](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/tg-qian-bao-lian-jie-tg-duo-qian-bao-xi-tong)

Last updated 11 months ago

# TG Solana 狙击机器人 | GMGN 使用教程

**🌈 使用GMGN Telegram Sniper Bot**交易 Solana MEME代币👇🏻**：**

[@GMGN\_US](https://t.me/US_GMGNBOT)
 |[@GMGN](https://t.me/GMGN_sol_bot)
 |[@GMGN\_02](https://t.me/GMGN_sol02_bot)
 |[@GMGN\_03](https://t.me/GMGN_sol03_bot)
 |[@GMGN\_04](https://t.me/GMGN_sol04_bot)

⚠️上面列出了所有官方的 GMGN 狙击机器人。任何其他机器人都是骗子机器人，小心你的钱包被诈骗转移余额。特别是骗子使用大写的“I”（“i”）伪装成小写的“l”（“L”），假装是GMGN交易机器人。

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/tg-solana-ju-ji-ji-qi-ren#id-1.initial-information)

1.初步信息：


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

注意，第一次使用机器人会自动生成一个solana钱包地址

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Fw6qG1eWgIar1r7zko5x7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda72164f-39d1-4ee7-966f-4426f8618973&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0dbd68f&sv=2)

**输入/start后，让我们研究一下当你使用狙击机器人时首先出现的按钮：**

买/卖

这是你将进行买卖的地方。点击进入代币交易界面，输入合约地址后，你可以进行买入或卖出

挂单列表

你可以点击查看你创建的所有限价挂单

持仓资产

你将看到你持有的代币

钱包

可以看到你的钱包信息，包含SOL以及WSOL余额，支持快捷一键转换WSOL→ SOL； 可以在此处导入导出私钥，更换钱包，但请注意私钥安全

信号跟单

点击使用 PUMP CTO 信号自动跟单功能，更多细节请查看：[信号跟单：PUMP CTO信号自动跟单](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xin-hao-gen-dan-pump-cto-xin-hao-zi-dong-gen-dan)

钱包跟单

点击使用自动跟单钱包功能，更多细节请查看：[钱包跟单：跟单聪明钱自动赚SOL！](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/qian-bao-gen-dan-gen-dan-cong-ming-qian-zi-dong-zhuan-sol)

pump飙升

点击可以看到最近1分钟价格飙升的代币

新池子监控

点击跳转 GMGN 新池子监控信号频道，在该频道中会通知新的 LP 创建，你将看到各类信息，例如烧池子、大额购买、网络、LP池子等

特色信号通知

点击跳转到 GMGN 特色信号频道，超多丰富精选信号等你挑选

监控钱包

点击跳转到 TG GMGN SOL链钱包监控通知机器人，更多细节请查看：[TG监控钱包通知](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/tg-jian-kong-qian-bao-tong-zhi)

邀请返佣

查看邀请人数以及返佣收入等其他详细信息

设置

可以设置开启自动滑点/快速滑点，并且可自定义快速滑点以及防夹滑点； 修改你的买入优先费/卖出优先费； 支持自动买，可自定义自动买策略，更多细节请查看：[限价自动买 - TG bot端](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xian-jia-gua-dan-zi-dong-mai-xian-jia-mai#id-3.-xian-jia-zi-dong-mai-tg-bot-duan)
 支持自动卖，可根据买入交易创建自动卖策略，更多细节请查看：[设置自动卖止盈止损](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xian-jia-gua-dan-zi-dong-mai-zhi-ying-zhi-sun#id-1.-she-zhi-zi-dong-mai-zhi-ying-zhi-sun)
 支持自定义买入/卖出数量，方便快捷买入卖出

切换语言

切换bot语言，支持英文/中文/韩文

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/tg-solana-ju-ji-ji-qi-ren#id-2.prepare-your-wallet)

2.钱包

*   由于SOL链机制问题交易结算时会有一定概率收到WSOL而不是SOL。 GMGN现已上线转换WSOL → SOL快捷功能
    
    具体步骤：在交易机器人 @GMGN\_sol\_bot 里输入/start，点击钱包，点击转换WSOL → SOL即可将收到的WSOL快捷转换为SOL
    

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/tg-solana-ju-ji-ji-qi-ren#id-3.set-up-the-bot)

3.设置机器人

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FgNFeGG0zuXF4MPd7V0XG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dafbdae48-b5fb-40dc-8860-e9c3191283cf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e946202e&sv=2)

必须转到主页中的设置并开始基本设置

自动滑点开启/关闭

将允许你启用或禁用自动滑点。自动滑点：根据价格波动、流动性、链上繁忙程度，滑点将自动改变。你也可以通过禁用此选项来手动配置它

快速滑点

默认建议 5-10，价格波动时成功率低 快速买卖 20-50，提高成功率，少收到一些币

防夹滑点

这是当你受到 MEV 机器人攻击时使用的滑点 ， 调整防夹滑点防夹默认建议 20-50 ；冲新盘建议 50-100，提高成功率

自动买

开启自动买入，发送代币合约给Bot，将会在达到预设值后立即自动买入

自动卖

Bot可以帮你自动创建有效期24小时的止盈/止损限价挂单

自定义买/自定义卖

自定义买入和卖出的数量

**有关自动买/自动卖/限价挂单详细内容请点击** [限价挂单：自动买/限价买](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xian-jia-gua-dan-zi-dong-mai-xian-jia-mai)
 [限价挂单：自动卖/止盈止损](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/xian-jia-gua-dan-zi-dong-mai-zhi-ying-zhi-sun)

### 

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/tg-solana-ju-ji-ji-qi-ren#id-4.buy-sell)

4.买入/卖出

1） 现价

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252FU3IxgYXtqumJtrPHsXSq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D240fcdfd-cf3f-4285-9cc0-0ddfb4b2b731&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74901e01&sv=2)

快速模式

快速提交上链

防夹模式

提交给防夹RPC，交易速度较慢

买

通过点击下面的按钮或者设置确定购买数量

卖

通过点击下面的按钮或者设置确定购买数量

2） 挂单

![](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1305672697-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FivH0y4hvvQWQlOnFKiAg%252Fuploads%252Fu8wMoKdeTFAtG9Xan0Gs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D009b0855-5046-4619-9c8b-eb2ff1841701&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f12ef98b&sv=2)

挂单买

你可以配置要在挂单中购买的 SOL 数量

挂单卖

你可以配置每个限价卖单中要出售的代币数量（百分比）

触发价格

设置后以你希望的价格执行订单

3d/24小时/1小时有效

这是保持挂单有效的时间范围，例如3D 将使订单保持打开状态 3 天

创建挂单

完成所有设置后，点击此按钮，创建挂单

[](https://docs.gmgn.ai/cn/tg-solana-ju-ji-ji-qi-ren#this-is-all-the-steps-and-setup-details-to-use-the-gmgn-trading-bot.-start-trading-with-the-gmgn-tg)

**⚠️**TG账户安全：


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

目前，我们只有sol链上的交易机器人，请谨防假冒机器人，并使用GMGN官方机器人。

*   不要共享私钥。
    
*   TG 客户端应从 Google Play 或app store等正规渠道安装。
    
*   请勿安装第三方语言包。
    
*   使用正确的 GMGN 交易机器人。市场上有假冒的机器人。
    
*   TG账户应经过2FA（双因素认证）验证，以防止TG账户被盗。
